caṇḍanandimahākālagaṇeśavṛṣabhṛṅgibhiḥ ।। stūyamānaṃ maheśānaṃ gaṇamātṛniṣevitam ।। anugrahakaraṃ devaṃ praṇatārtivināśanam ।। yattvayā kathitaṃ mahyaṃ svacchandaṃ parameśvara ।।
catuṣpīṭhaṃ mahātantra catuṣṭayaphalodayam ।। alpāyuṣo alpavittāśca alpasattvāśca śaṃkara ।। bhuktimuktipradātāraṃ kathayasva prasādataḥ ।। bhayābhayapradātāraṃ śiṣyaṃ bhūmiṃ ca kīdṛśīm ।।
yajanaṃ havanaṃ caiva adhivāsaṃ rajāṃsi ca ।। dīkṣā cādhvābhiṣekau ca samayānsādhanāni ca ।। sādhu sādhu mahābhāge yattvayā paricoditam ।। ādau tāvatparīkṣeta ācāryaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam ।।
śivaśāstravidhānajñaṃ jñānajñeyaviśāradam ।। sattvavadvīryasampannaṃ dayādākṣiṇyasaṃyutam ।। īdṛśaṃ tu guruṃ prāpya siddhimuktī na dūrataḥ ।। kekaro danturaḥ kāṇaḥ pāpiṣṭhaḥ śāstravarjitaḥ ।।
tārkiko dambhasaṃyuktaḥ satyaśaucavivarjitaḥ ।। śiṣyo dayānvito dhīro dambhamāyāvivarjitaḥ ।। guruśuśrūṣaṇaparaḥ suśāntendriyasaṃyutaḥ ।। māyānvitaḥ śaṭhaḥ krūro niḥsatyaḥ kalahapriyaḥ ।।
dūṣako guruśāstrāṇāṃ dīkṣito api na muktibhāk ।। mantrasiddhiṃ haret kṣudra ācāryastu varānane ।। kekareṇa bhavedvyādhir danturaḥ kalikārakaḥ ।। śāstrahīne na siddhiḥ syād dīkṣādau vīravandite ।।
kṛśaḥ kṣayakaro jñeyaḥ sthūla utpātakārakaḥ ।। dāmbhikaḥ pāpajanako veditavyo varānane ।। sarve te na śubhā devi iha loke paratra ca ।। viśalyāṃ lakṣaṇairyuktāṃ sarvakāmārthasādhikām ।।
sudhūpāmodabahalāṃ vitānopariśobhitam ।। sudhūpitaḥ prasannātmā khaṭikākarasaṃyutaḥ ।। mātṛkāṃ prastarettatra ādikṣāntāmanukramāt ।। kavargaścaṭavargau ca tapayāḥ śastathaiva ca ।।
mātṛkābhairavaṃ devam avargeṇa prapūjayet ।। avarge tu mahālakṣmīḥ kavarge kamalodbhavā ।। nārāyaṇī tavarge tu vārāhī tu pavargikā ।। etāḥ sapta mahāmātṛḥ saptalokavyavasthitāḥ ।।
ante asya uddharenmantrān yathākramaniyogataḥ ।। anena yojayetsarvaṃ somasūryāgnimadhyagam ।। mūrtiṃ haṃsākṣareṇaiva bindubhinnena kalpayet ।। tadūrdhve sakalaṃ devaṃ svacchandaṃ parikalpayet ।।
tha ghorebhyo samālikhya tato anyattu samālikhet ।। sarvebhyaḥ padamanyacca namaste rudra eva ca ।। mantrarājaḥ samākhyātaḥ aghoraḥ surapūjitaḥ ।। janmakoṭīsahasraistu bhramadbhiḥ samupārjitam ।।
yakārādivakārāntāḥ saṃhāreṇa samāyutāḥ ।। brahmabhaṅgyā niyojyāni mūrdhādicaraṇāvadhi ।। aparaṃ kalpayitvā tu kalābhedena vinyaset ।। ūrdhvamūrdhnā tu saṃyuktaṃ kṣakāraṃ tvīśarūpiṇam ।।
pañcamaṃ yadbhavedvaktraṃ kṣakāreṇaiva nirdiśet ।। pṛṣṭhe corasi vinyased aghoreṇa yathākramam ।। jaṅghayośca sphijoḥ kaṭyāṃ pārśvayorubhayorapi ।। pādau hastau tathā nāsāṃ śiraścaiva bhujāvatha ।।
tāsāṃ nāmāni vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। īśānasya kalā pañca nirañjanapadānugā ।। puruṣasya kalā hyetāś catasraḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। aghorasya kalā hyetā aṣṭau vai varavarṇini ।।
ṛddhirmāyā ca rātriśca bhrāmiṇī mohanī tathā ।। siddhirṛddhirdyutirlakṣmīr medhā kāntiḥ sudhā sthitiḥ ।। punaśca sādhako devi sarvāṅgeṣu yathākramam ।। vidyāṅgāni punarnyasya teṣāṃ mantrān śṛṇu priye ।।
ghoraghoratarebhyaśca tṛtīyaṃ parikalpayet ।। namaste rudrarūpebhyaḥ pañcamaṃ ca vidhānataḥ ।। netratrayaṃ prakalpeta vidyādehasya bhāmini ।। sarvātmā tu brahmaśiro jvālinī piṅgalaṃ tathā ।।
kriyā jñānaṃ tathaivecchā tāsāṃ mantrānnibodha me ।। kriyāśaktiḥ samākhyātā sarvasṛṣṭiprakāśikā ।। jñānaśaktiḥ smṛtā hyeṣā prabodhajananī śubhā ।। icchāśaktiḥ samākhyātā bhairavasyāmitātmikā ।।
bālendunādaśaktyantaḥ svacchando niṣkalaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśāḥ padaṃ gacchantyanāmayam ।। hṛcchiraśca śikhā varma locanāstraṃ prakalpayet ।। namaḥ svāhā tathā vauṣaṭ huṃ vaṣaṭ phaṭ krameṇa tu ।।
hara īma akāraśca ṅādirosvarasaṃyutaḥ ।। lādistrisvarasambhinno haṃso bindusamāyuktaḥ ।। aghoreśvarīti vikhyātā svacchandotsaṅgagāminī ।। hānto yādiryakārānto rādiḥ ṣaṣṭhakalānvitaḥ ।।
sānto binduradho hyagniḥ ṣaṣṭhayuktastu kīrtitaḥ ।। saṃhāraḥ ṣaṣṭhasaṃyuktaḥ ṣaḍantena samanvitaḥ ।। ñādiḥ ṣaṣṭhasvaropetas tripadena samāyutaḥ ।। sāntaḥ śādyena saṃyuktaḥ ṣaṣṭhasvarayuto apyadhaḥ ।।
manmathaḥ kathito hyeṣa surasiddhanamaskṛtaḥ ।। hararādisamāyuktaḥ ūkārādhaḥ sabindukaḥ ।। kṣasāntarbindusaṃyuktaḥ pañcamena vibheditaḥ ।। kṣādiryāntasamopeto hāntenādhoniyojitaḥ ।।
bindvardhendusamāyukto nādaśaktisamanvitaḥ ।। bhairavāṣṭakametaddhi parivāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। namaskārāvamānāṃśca sāstrānsamparikalpayet ।। śaucaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ snānaṃ kartavyaṃ tu mṛdambhasā ।।
prakṣālya jalatīraṃ tu sthāpayettāṃ varānane ।। bhāgārdhena kaṭiṃ corū jaṅghe pādau tathaiva ca ।। avaśiṣṭaṃ tu bhāgārdhaṃ gṛhītvāstrābhimantritam ।। śiraḥprabhṛti pādāntam āguṣṭhya snānamācaret ।।
saṃdhyāyā vandanaṃ kuryāc chāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। bhāgārdhaṃ yatsthitaṃ pūrvaṃ tato bhāgatrayaṃ kuru ।। pūrvabhāgaṃ tato astreṇa saptavārāṃstu mantrayet ।। uttaraṃ cābhimantryaivaṃ devenāṅgayutena ca ।।
uttareṇa tu bhāgena jalaṃ caivābhimantrayet ।। ātmānaṃ guṇṭhayitvā tu dakṣabhāgena suvrate ।। prāṇāyāmābhiṣekau tu kartavyau bhairaveṇa ca ।। upaspṛśya kṛtanyāso mūlamantramanusmaran ।।
tatrastho vandayetsaṃdhyāṃ mārjanādiranukramāt ।। japaṃ kṛtvā nivedyaivaṃ praṇamya ca varānane ।। sarveṣāṃ bhūtasaṃghānāṃ tatastīrthaṃ tu saṃharet ।। malasnānaṃ prakartavyaṃ bhāvitenāntarātmanā ।।
vidhisnānaṃ tataḥ kuryād bhairaveśamanusmaran ।। bhairaveṇāṅgayuktena samuddhūlyaṃ yathākramam ।। saṃdhyāyā vandanaṃ kuryād yathāpūrvaṃ varānane ।। śikhāṃ baddhvā śikhāṃ smṛtvā upaspṛśya vidhānataḥ ।।
diṅmātṛbhyo namaskṛtya dvāraṃ saṃprokṣya yatnataḥ ।। dvāraśākhordhvato devaṃ gaṇeśaṃ ca śriyaṃ tathā ।। arghyapādyopahāraiśca tato dvārasya cottare ।। kālindīṃ caiva saṃpūjya yathānukramayogataḥ ।।
saptābhimantritaṃ kṛtvā jvaladagniśikhākulam ।। nivāritaṃ tena sarvaṃ vighnajālamanantakam ।। madhye sampūjya brahmāṇaṃ gandhaiḥ puṣpairanukramāt ।। upaviśyāsanaṃ baddhvā svabhyastaṃ vai puraḥsthitam ।।
kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaitau plāvayedamṛtena tu ।। mūrtiṃ nyasyānuvaktrāṇi svacchandaṃ parikalpayet ।। bhairavānapi saṃkalpya paraṃ tattvamanusmaret ।। aśuddhaḥ svamarudrecyaḥ śuddhenāpūrayettanum ।।
khadyotakanibhaṃ sūkṣmaṃ karaṇaistu vivarjitam ।। śivīkāryastathātmaiva yathā bhavati tacchṛṇu ।। saṃhāreṇa yabhinnena rudrabījayutena ca ।। adho viṣṇusamāyukto vāyuvarṇaḥ sabindukaḥ ।।
bindumastakasaṃbhinnaḥ śaktinyāsastato bhavet ।। malapradhvastacaitanyaṃ kalāvidyāsamāśritam ।। niyatyā yamitaṃ bhūyaḥ puṃbhāvenopabṛṃhitam ।। buddhitattvasamāsīnam ahaṅkārasamāvṛtam ।।
praṇavena tu sarvaṃ tac charīrotpattikāraṇam ।। ṣaṭtattvī tvātmasaṃbaddhā jñātavyātra varānane ।। caturviṃśatitattvāni caitanyarahitāni tu ।। sacetanāni sarvāṇi jñātavyāni sadaiva hi ।।
tato mūrtiṃ nyaseddevi mūlamantrasulakṣitam ।। mukhāni kalpayetpaścān mūrdhādicaraṇāvadhi ।। uttaraṃ paścimaṃ caiva yathāvatpravibhāgaśaḥ ।। navatattvaṃ tritattvaṃ ca vidyāṅgā locanatrayam ।।
ṣoḍaśāntarhatā sā tu rakṣi"kā vighnanāśikā ।। hṛdaye nābhideśe ca guhya ūrvośca jānutaḥ ।। kriyājñāne tathecchā ca dakṣe vāme ca madhyataḥ ।। niṣkalaṃ tu tathāvāhya aṅgānyevaṃ yathākramam ।।
pūjayeddevadeveśaṃ manasaiva prakalpitaiḥ ।। nābhau kandaṃ samāropya nālaṃ tu dvādaśāṅgulam ।। aṣṭapatraṃ mahādīptaṃ kesarālaṃ sakarṇikam ।। bhuvanāni ca tānyeva rudrāṇāṃ varavarṇini ।।
vidyāpadmaṃ mahādīptaṃ karṇikābījarājitam ।। evaṃ dhyātvā mahāpadmaṃ sarvadevamayaṃ śubham ।। aṅkuraṃ nālavinyāsam anantaṃ parikalpayet ।। dharmaṃ jñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ ca kramānnyaset ।।
pādakāḥ siṃharūpāste trinetrā bhīmavikramāḥ ।। adharmājñānāvairāgyam anaiśvaryaṃ ca prāgdiśaḥ ।। saṃdhānakīlakāścaiva atasīpuṣpasaṃnibhāḥ ।। adhaśchādanamūrdhvaṃ ca raktaṃ śuklaṃ vicintayet ।।
sitaṃ padmaṃ vijānīyāt kesarāṇi vicintayet ।। karṇikā hemasaṃkāśā bījāni haritāni tu ।। raudrīṃ dakṣiṇapatre tu kālīṃ nairṛtagocare ।। balavikaraṇīṃ devīṃ vāyavyadalamāśritām ।।
sarvabhūtadamanīṃ ca aiśānyāṃ viniyojayet ।। śakracāpanibhaṃ devi dhyātavyaṃ śaktimaṇḍalam ।। sūryādhvamaṇḍalaṃ patre somaṃ saṃyojya kesare ।। brahmā viṣṇurharaścaiva maṇḍaleṣvadhipāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
kṛṣṇājinottarīyaśca rājīvāsanasaṃsthitaḥ ।। akṣamālādharo devaḥ padmahastaḥ sulocanaḥ ।। atasīpuṣpasaṃkāśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।। sphuranmukuṭamāṇikyaṃ kiṅkiṇījālamaṇḍitam ।।
dhyātvā viṣṇuṃ mahātmānaṃ kesareṣu niveśayet ।। daśabāhuṃ viśālākṣaṃ nāgayajñopavītinam ।। nīlakaṇṭhaṃ vṛṣārūḍhaṃ rudraṃ dhyātvā varānane ।। mahāpretaṃ nyasetpaścāt prahasantaṃ sacetanam ।।
praṇavena nyasetsarvam āsanaṃ bhairavasya tu ।। kadambakusumākārāṃ tuṣārakiraṇatviṣam ।। dvātriṃśadvarṇakacitaṃ sphurattaḍidivojjvalam ।। mūrdhādicaraṇaṃ yāvat praṇavādinamontataḥ ।।
navatattvaṃ tritattvaṃ ca navakaṃ bhairavābhidham ।। śaktitrayaṃ tato nyasyed dakṣadigvāmagocare ।। tripañcanayanaṃ devaṃ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitam ।। pañcavaktraṃ viśālākṣaṃ sarpagonāsamaṇḍitam ।।
kapālamālābharaṇaṃ khaḍgakheṭakadhāriṇam ।। varadābhayahastaṃ ca muṇḍakhaṭvāṅgadhāriṇam ।। vajradaṇḍakṛtāṭopaṃ paraśvāyudhahastakam ।। siṃhacarmaparīdhānaṃ gajacarmottarīyakam ।।
ūrdhvavaktraṃ maheśāni sphaṭikābhaṃ vicintayet ।। dakṣiṇaṃ tu vijānīyād vāmaṃ caiva vicintayet ।। candrārbudapratīkāśaṃ paścimaṃ tu vicintayet ।। dhyāyate yastu yuktātmā kṣipraṃ sidhyati mānavaḥ ।।
suśāntaṃ niṣkalaṃ devaṃ sarvavyāpinirañjanam ।। hṛtkaṇṭhatālubhrūmadhyanādāntāntasamāśritam ।। saṃsthāpya vidhivaddevam aṅgaṣaṭkaṃ tato nyaset ।। saṃnidhānaṃ ca deveśi niṣṭhurayā nirodhayet ।।
mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścāt tridhā traikālyakarmaṇi ।। paridhāpya suvastrāṇi netrapaṭṭodbhavāni ca ।। puṣpairnānāvidhaiḥ śubhrair arcayedbhūṣayetpunaḥ ।। praṇamya bhairavaṃ devaṃ svacchandaṃ viśvanāyakam ।।
aiśānyāṃ pūrvato yāmyāṃ uttarāpyāvasānakam ।। bāhubhirdaśabhiścaiva śaśāṅkamukuṭaiḥ saha ।। agnīśarakṣovāyavyacaturdikṣu ca taṃ nyaset ।। hṛdayaṃ raktavarṇābhaṃ śiro gorocanaprabham ।।
ādhūmraṃ kavacaṃ vidyāt kapiśaṃ cāstrameva ca ।। pañcavaktrāḥ smṛtāḥ sarve daśabāhvindubhūṣitāḥ ।। nānāvastraparīdhānā mukuṭairujjvalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। dviraṣṭavarṣakākārāḥ surūpāḥ sthirayauvanāḥ ।।
yā sā pūrvaṃ mayā khyātā aghorī śaktiruttamā ।। yādṛśaṃ bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ bhairavyāstādṛgeva hi ।। prasannāsyāṃ sadā dhyāyed bhairavīṃ vismitekṣaṇām ।। kapālīśaṃ tu pūrvāyām āgneyyāṃ śikhivāhanam ।।
manmathaṃ paścime bhāge meghanādeśvaraṃ tathā ।। vidyārājaṃ tathaiśānyāṃ vinyasettu subhāvitaḥ ।। kapālamālābharaṇāḥ sphuranmāṇikyamaṇḍitāḥ ।। dakṣiṇe nīlameghābhaṃ nairṛtyāṃ jvalanaprabham ।।
candrabimbaprabhaṃ saumye īśāne sphaṭikaprabham ।। nāmāni teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। somarājaḥ kuberaśca īśānaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। vajraṃ śaktistathā daṇḍaḥ khaḍgaḥ pāśastathaiva ca ।।
vajraṃ cānekavarṇāḍhyaṃ śaktiṃ hemasamaprabhām ।। kiṃśukābhaṃ tathā pāśaṃ dhvajaṃ śuklaṃ vicintayet ।। saṃpūjyāvaraṇaṃ sarvaṃ saṃdhānaṃ mantranāyake ।। pañca brahmānyathāṅgāni etānyāvaraṇāni tu ।।
mūlamantreṇa kartavyaṃ nāḍīsaṃdhānameva ca ।। ghārikā vaṭakāṃścaiva śaṣkulīrmodakāṃstathā ।। śālyodanaṃ mudgasūpam ājyāktaṃ saṃprakalpayet ।। ghṛtāktāṃścillakāṃścaiva lavaṇānparikalpayet ।।
rasālāṃ ca dadhi kṣīram āsavaṃ vividhaṃ tathā ।। agramāpūrayecchaṃbhor vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ ।। mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścāt tridhā traikālyakarmaṇi ।। akṣamālāṃ tu saṃgṛhya gandhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ samarcitām ।।
mūlamantraṃ samuccārya nāde līnaṃ vicintayet ।। akṣarākṣarasantānaṃ na drutaṃ na vilambitam ।। saṃhāraḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ śivadhāmaphalapradaḥ ।। śarvarī sā tu vijñeyā hṛdabjaṃ yāvadāgataḥ ।।
ātmano bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ sadā bhāvyaṃ varānane ।। japtvā nivedayeddevi bhairavāya varānane ।। trisiddhisiddhidaṃ devi sarahasyamudāhṛtam ।। saśabdaścābhicāre asau prāgudagdakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ।।
ātmanā śrūyate yastu tamupāṃśuṃ vijānate ।। aṣṭottaraśatenaiva akṣamālā samerukā ।। sphāṭikī maṇiratnotthā sauvarṇī vaidrumī tathā ।। sūtraṃ dhyātvā parāṃ śaktim adhvabhāgāṃstato maṇīn ।।
saptaviṃśatibhiḥ kuryād dviguṇairvā caturguṇaiḥ ।। na taṃ vilaṅghayedvidvān sṛṣṭisaṃhārakāraṇam ।। mahāśaṅkhākṣasūtraṃ tu sarvakāmaphalapradam ।। tasmāttu sphāṭikī mālā japtavyā sādhakottamaiḥ ।।
evaṃ hṛdambujāvastho yaṣṭavyo bhairavo vibhuḥ ।। tatrārghapātramādau vai sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tathā ।। padmapatrapalāśotthaṃ gṛhītvā kṣālya vāriṇā ।। mṛṣṭadhūpena saṃdhūpya vāriṇāpūrayettataḥ ।।
varmāvaguṇṭhitaṃ kṛtvā yāgaṃ tatraiva vinyaset ।। yāgārtho dravyasaṃghātaḥ tato yajanamārabhet ।। sakalavyāpikāṃ sūkṣmāṃ śivādhārāṃ tu sarvagām ।। anantaṃ caiva vinyasya dharmaṃ jñānaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
adharmaṃ ca tathājñānam avairāgyamanaiśvaram ।। padmaṃ sakesaraṃ devi karṇikāṃ puṣkarāṇi ca ।। mūrtiṃ brahmakalājālaṃ navatattvaṃ tritattvakam ।। śaktitrayaṃ paraṃ devam aṅgaṣaṭkasamanvitam ।।
nirvartya tu yathānyāyaṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā ।। rodhaṃ niṣṭhurayā kuryān mūlamantramanusmaran ।। mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścāt tridhā traikālyakarmaṇi ।। īśapūrvayāmyasaumyavaruṇāntaṃ prakalpayet ।।
āgneyaiśānarakṣaḥsu sāmīraindradiśorapi ।। netraṃ tu karṇikāyāṃ vai pūrvasyāṃ diśi saṃsthitam ।। mantrasaṃkarapuṣpāṇi na kuryātsādhakaḥ sadā ।। paripāṭyā tu dātavyaṃ na mantrāṃllaṅghayetkvacit ।।
ardhyaṃ pādyaṃ ca dhūpaṃ ca nityaṃ tāvatsamācaret ।। bhairavāṣṭakalokeśān sāstrānsaṃparikalpayet ।। pūrvādīśānaparyantaṃ kalpayeta vidhānataḥ ।। śmaśānaiḥ sakabandhaiśca saśūlodbandhabhīṣaṇaiḥ ।।
agnikaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge kālākhyaṃ paścime tathā ।। nairṛtyāmagnijihvaṃ tu vāyavyāṃ tu karālinam ।। tarpayenmatsyamāṃsādyair āsavairvividhaistathā ।। praṇipātaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā japtvā mantraṃ subhāvitaḥ ।।
huḍḍuṅkāranamaskārān kṛtvā caiva tato vrajet ।। kuṇḍaṃ tu lakṣaṇopetaṃ prokṣayedastravāriṇā ।। uddhṛtya prokṣayetpaścād astramantreṇa bhāmini ।। secanaṃ kuṭṭanaṃ caiva lepanaṃ tena kārayet ।।
pūjanaṃ gandhapuṣpādyaiḥ asinā cābhimantraṇam ।। yāmyasaumyamukhī caikā vajrametatprakīrtitam ।। yāmyasaumyamukhā tvekā vajrametatprakīrtitam ।। sabāhyābhyantaraṃ chādyaṃ gṛhahetvarthamīśvari ।।
darbheṇa viṣṭaraṃ puṣpaṃ praṇavena prakalpayet ।। āmantraṇapadenaiva brahmāṇaṃ sthāpya pūjayet ।। catuṣpathaṃ kuṇḍamadhye darbhābhyāṃ praṇavena tu ।। puṣpaṃ tasyopariṣṭāttu hṛdayenaiva pūjayet ।।
nīlotpaladalaśyāmām ṛtumaccārulocanām ।। dhyātvā caivaṃvidhāṃ devīṃ sthāpayetkuṇḍamadhyataḥ ।। pūjayedgaṃdhapuṣpādyair bhavamantramanusmaran ।। tato agnipātramādāya śivāmbho astreṇa prokṣayet ।।
araṇyādisamudbhūtaṃ lokāgnyantaṃ vidhānataḥ ।। ṣaḍaṅgenaiva saṃpūjya amṛtatvaṃ dhruveṇa tu ।। dhruveṇa kuṇḍabāhye tu tridhābhrāmyāvatārayet ।। astramuccārya saṃprokṣya yoniṃ pracchādayedbudhaḥ ।।
astreṇaiva caturdikṣu darbhaireva prakalpayet ।। dakṣahaste tu badhnīyād astramantramanusmaran ।। aparāsyatrirāhutyā pūjanaṃ hṛdayena tu ।। hṛdā vai jalabinduṃ tu darbhāgreṇātra pātayet ।।
trirāhutiṃ cottareṇa śikhayā ca trirāhutim ।। sīmantaṃ dakṣiṇāsyena darbhāgreṇa prakalpayet ।। pratyaṅgāni ca saṃkalpya sīmantonnayanaṃ bhavet ।। pūrvamadhyāparānvahnau trīnbhāgānparikalpayet ।।
śirāṃsi pañcāhutyaiva ūrdhvāsyena tribhistribhiḥ ।। aparaṃ cāpyāhutibhiḥ pūrvāsyena trisaṃkhyayā ।। netraṃ netreṇa saṃkalpya mukheṣvevaṃ trayaṃ trayam ।। tataḥ kalāsamūhaṃ ca pañca cātha catuṣṭayam ।।
śeṣāsyaiḥ saṃprakalpyaivaṃ kalāmūrtistato bhavet ।। trirāhutiṃ dakṣiṇena śirasā cāhutitrayam ।। astreṇa vījayedagnim astreṇaiva tu pūjayet ।। evaṃ mantradvayenaiva jātakarma kṛtaṃ bhavet ।।
vaktrāṇi śodhyānyasinā āhutitrayayogataḥ ।। prokṣayetkuṇḍapārśvāni sāstreṇaiva śivāmbhasā ।। saumyāgrānpūrvavāruṇyoḥ paridhīnviṣṭarāṃstathā ।। rudra ca dakṣiṇe sthāpya viṣṇuṃ paścimaviṣṭare ।।
ādau dhruvaṃ smareddevi namaścānte prakalpayet ।। mekhalopari lokeśān pūjayetpraṇavena tu ।। tataḥ kaṅkaṇakaṃ muktvā dakṣahastavyavasthitam ।। kavacenopacāraṃ tu gandhapuṣpādidhūpakaiḥ ।।
śivanāmāṅkitaṃ vahniṃ janayitvā surāṃstataḥ ।। puṣpādibhiḥ samabhyarcya homaireva tribhistribhiḥ ।। caturviṃśatisaṃkhyātāḥ śivāgnestarpaṇāya tu ।। kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaitau śivāgnau bhrāmayettridhā ।।
punaragnau paribhrāmya prokṣayettau śivāmbhasā ।। śivāmbhasā mārjayitvā darbhamūlena saṃspṛśet ।। darbhāṇāṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ pūjyau dakṣiṇe agneḥ sadā budhaiḥ ।। ājyaṃ saṃprokṣya cāstreṇa kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet ।।
kuṇḍasya parito devi tridhā bhrāmya tu sthāpayet ।। darbhāgradvayamādāya prādeśaṃ madhyagranthitam ।। aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu gṛhītvaitatpavitrakam ।। astreṇaiva tu mantreṇa avadyotaḥ śivāgninā ।।
nīrājanaṃ tataḥ kuryāt paryagnikaraṇaṃ tataḥ ।। dhāmnaiva vidhinā mantrī prokṣayedastravāriṇā ।। sakṛduccārayogena pūjayedbhairaveṇa tu ।। aparāsyena tadvaktrasaṃdhānaṃ tu samācaret ।।
trirāhutiprayogeṇa dakṣiṇasyāpyayaṃ vidhiḥ ।। trirāhutiprayogeṇa vaktrasaṃdhiḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। muktikāmasya dīkṣāyām ūrdhvavaktrasya mukhyatā ।। sadāśivāntagāḥ sarvāḥ pūrvavaktre tu homayet ।।
dakṣiṇe caiva vaktre tu homātsiddhiḥ parā bhavet ।। saubhāgyārohasiddhiṃ tu uttare homayetsadā ।। ājyabhāgo hi hotavya ūrdhvavaktre tu paścime ।। nyasitavyo varārohe tato vai vartmakalpanā ।।
nāḍītrayeṇa yugapat pātre bhāgatrayaṃ nyaset ।। iḍābhāge tu yattejo vāme saumyaṃ prakalpayet ।। bhairaveṇaiva mantreṇāgnaye svāhāntameva ca ।। somabhāgastu somāya svāhetyante samuccaran ।।
agnīṣometi saṃjñe dve svāhānte dhāma cāditaḥ ।। śuklapakṣe vidhirhyeṣa kṛṣṇapakṣe anyathā bhavet ।। agneḥ sūryasya madhyādvai āhutiṃ pratipādayet ।। prāśanārthamato homo vaktrāṇāṃ bhairaveṇa tu ।।
prāpaṇārthāya sarveṣāṃ pūrṇāmekāṃ pradāpayet ।। agniṃ tu proddharetpaścāt pātre saṃsthāpya rakṣayet ।। praṇītaṃ kalpayettatra camasaṃ vāripūritam ।। praṇavādi samāvāhya viṣṇunāma tato namaḥ ।।
svāgatāsanapādyārghaiḥ tato vijñāpayettu tam ।। bhagavaṃstvatprasādena yāge niśchidratāstu naḥ ।। sthaṇḍiloktavidhānena anantādīnprakalpayet ।। tanmukhyavaktraṃ saṃkalpya mukhaṃ kuṇḍapramāṇataḥ ।।
prāgādyaṣṭau madhya ekā kāmyārthe diggatāstu yāḥ ।। vaśīkartryuccāṭanī syād arthadā muktidāyikā ।। pūṇā tu bhairaveṇaiva jihvānāṃ kalpanāya ca ।। jvālāgraṃ tu hṛdāgṛhya vahnicaitanyakalpitam ।।
madhyajihvānusāreṇa agninābhau tu kandakam ।। patrāṣṭakasamopetaṃ sitavarṇaṃ sutejasam ।। oṃkāreṇa śivāntaṃ ca agnimūrtiṃ prakalpayet ।। recakeṇa kṣipedvahnau sā mūrtirbhairavātmikā ।।
śodhyādhvānaṃ tu vinyasyed dīkṣākāle varānane ।। vaktrasaṃdhiśca vaktrabhyāṃ śivavaktrāgnivaktrayoḥ ।। mūlamantraṃ samuccārya agnināsāvinirgatam ।। śuddhājyenāhutiśatam aṣṭotkṛṣṭaṃ varānane ।।
bhairavāṣṭakalokeśān daśamāṃśena homayet ।। bhairavāpyāyanārthāya tathā pūrṇāṃ prapātayet ।। paścāddhomaḥ prakartavyo yathecchaṃ tu varānane ।। dhānyairdhanārthasiddhyarthaṃ ghṛtaguggulahomataḥ ।।
śvetāravindairājyāktaiḥ bilvaiśca śriyamāpnuyāt ।। sitaraktapītakṛṣṇaiḥ śamanākṛṣṭipauṣṭikam ।। kundapuṣpaiḥ sutārthāya aśokaiḥ priyasaṃgamaḥ ।। nāgaistu nāgakanyā vai siddhārthaiḥ siddhakanyakā ।।
ghṛtāktena varārohe samantrī sapurohitaḥ ।। yakṣiṇī vaśamāyāti puṣpaiścaiva kadambajaiḥ ।। mṛgīṃ baddhvā tilairhomaḥ padmabilvairadhiṣṭhitam ।। evaṃ homānusāreṇa sādhako vidhisaṃsthitaḥ ।।
tāṃstānsa sādhayatyeva bhairavasya vaco yathā ।। vāriṇā suviśuddhātmā kṛtakṛtyaḥ prasannadhīḥ ।। jihmajenopavītena savāsā vā digambaraḥ ।। divyābharaṇasampannaḥ suprasannaḥ subhāvitaḥ ।।
mahadvārapradeśe tu sthitvā prāgiva bhāvitaḥ ।। humphaṭkāraprayogeṇa tālāśabdaṃ vidhāya ca ।। pārṣṇyā bhūmigatān hanyāt tālayā cāntarikṣagān ।। rakṣāṃ pūrvavadastreṇa paritaḥ parikalpayet ।।
tato dakṣiṇadigbhāge upaviśya varānane ।। plāvanāpyāyane caiva sakalīkaraṇaṃ tathā ।। śaktyādhāramanantaṃ ca dharmādicaraṇāvadhi ।। adhaśchādanamūrdhvaṃ ca padmakesarakarṇikāḥ ।।
śivāntamāsanaṃ dadyāt pūrvarūpaṃ dhruveṇa tu ।। dvātriṃśadakṣaraṃ devaṃ bhairavāṣṭakameva ca ।। śaktitrayaṃ paraṃ devam aṅgaṣaṭkasamanvitam ।। saṃkalpya ca yathānyāyaṃ yathāyogaṃ prakalpayet ।।
puruṣeśau ca devasya dalasthāṃścopakalpayet ।। pūrvato yāvadīśāntaṃ bhairavāvaraṇaṃ bahiḥ ।। astrāṇi lokapālāṃśca bhairavāṣṭakameva ca ।। krameṇoccārayet sarvān yāvattadgarbhamaiśvaram ।।
uccārayettato devaṃ hrasvadīrghaplutānvitam ।। adhaḥśakteryāvadūrdhvaṃ somasūryapathāntarā ।। devatāpañcakaṃ śaktiṃ vyāpinīṃ samanonmane ।। nistaraṅgaṃ niradhvākhyaṃ sakalavyāpi conmanam ।।
sarveṣvāvaraṇeṣvevaṃ devi tadvyāpakaṃ nyaset ।। yathā svarūpasaṃsthānavarṇā ye kathitā mayā ।। karṇikāyāṃ tu saṃsthāpya dvidhāvasthaṃ ca bhairavam ।। tatrāpi parito jñeyam anirdeśyamanāmayam ।।
oṃkārabindunādānāṃ vilayaṃ taṃ vinirdiśet ।। yasya nāgraṃ ca mūlaṃ ca diśo vidiśastathā ।। prathamaṃ mānasaṃ yāgaṃ paścāddravyasamanvitam ।। svahaste sthaṇḍile liṅge maṇḍale caruke tathā ।।
akṛtvā mānasaṃ yāgaṃ yo anyaṃ yāgaṃ samārabhet ।। ātmayāge kṛte caiva dehaśuddhiḥ prajāyate ।। ātmanirdahanaṃ caiva mānasaṃ ca yaduktavān ।। yatra yatra sthito deśe yaścaivaṃ tu vidhiṃ yajet ।।
sarvāvasthāgataścaiva viṣayairanurañjitaḥ ।। etattantroktavidhinā yaduktaṃ vidhipūrvakam ।। nānāsiddhiguṇairyuktaṃ nānākāmaphalapradam ।। sadāśivo api jānāti devāścaivāsurādayaḥ ।।
parāṃ vṛttimanudhyāyan dravyāṇyādau vilokayet ।। puṣpāṇi divyagandhīni tilavrīhighṛtādikam ।। karaṇīṃ kartarīṃ caiva pāśabandhanasūtrakam ।। samidho dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca carusthālīṃ srucaṃ sruvam ।।
tato arghapātramādāya kṣālayedastravāriṇā ।। udakādibhiraṣṭāṅgaḥ pūrayettu varānane ।। praṇavenāsanaṃ sarvaṃ tato mūrtiṃ nyaset priye ।। gandhaiḥ puṣpaistathā dhūpair mantrasandhānapūrvakam ।।
pātrāṇāṃ tritayaṃ kalpyaṃ nirodhārthe vidhau tathā ।। mantrasandhānakaṃ prāgvan nāḍīsandhānameva ca ।। bhrūmadhyaṃ śabdakūṭaṃ tat turyasthānaṃ vibhedayet ।। dvādaśāntaṃ paraṃ nītvā karastho mantravigrahaḥ ।।
ātmano recakenaiva pūrakeṇa viśeddhṛdi ।। vyāpakaṃ tu śivaṃ dhyāyen mantramūrtimadhiṣṭhitam ।। pañcagavyāya pātraṃ tu śodhayettu śivāmbhasā ।। darbhāsanaṃ dhruveṇaiva maṇḍalaṃ tu prakalpayet ।।
pṛthakpātrasthitānyeva prokṣyāstreṇa śivāmbhasā ।। śikhayā varmaṇā kṣīram astreṇājyaṃ kuśodakam ।। pūrvasaṃskṛtapātre tu svamantrairgomayādikam ।। praṇavena tu saṃkalpya anantaṃ mūrtivigraham ।।
mantrasandhānakaṃ kṛtvā amṛtīkaraṇaṃ tathā ।। astrābhimantritaṃ darbhaṃ gṛhītvollekhanaṃ kuru ।। tataścaivoddharecchalyam ājalāntaṃ vyavasthitam ।। samīkaraṇamastreṇa kavacena tu secanam ।।
astreṇa pañcagavyena gandhatoyena copari ।। saptakṛtvo astramantreṇa sthitvā mantre tu prāgdiśaḥ ।। cāmareṇa suśubhreṇa astramantreṇa saṃharet ।। pañcagavyena samprokṣya gandhāmbhobhiḥ śivāmbhasā ।।
śuklapuṣpāṇi muñcantīṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutām ।। brahmasthānopaviṣṭāṃ tu dvārābhimukhabhadradām ।। aiśānīṃ diśamāśritya pañcagavyena maṇḍalam ।। anantādyāsanaṃ dattvā dhruveṇāmaṇḍalāvadhi ।।
svastikādyaiścārcayitvā yavasiddhārthadūrvabhiḥ ।। sampūrya sarvataśchannaṃ cūtāśvatthādipallavaiḥ ।। prokṣya cāstreṇa saṃgṛhya kavacenāvaguṇṭhitam ।। kalādhvabhairavādīni nyasyārghādīn prakalpayet ।।
gandhapuṣpapavitrādyaiḥ sitavastreṇa bhūṣayet ।। śivāmbhasā tu samprokṣya praṇavenāsanaṃ nyaset ।। kumbhavaccārcayitvā tām āsanasyopari nyaset ।। uccāryāstraṃ krameṇāgre dravyāṇāṃ vārdhanīṃ nayet ।।
tatsthānāttu samuddhṛtya yāvatkoṇaṃ tu śāṅkaram ।। nayedvārdhānimārgeṇa tasmin saṃsthāpayetpunaḥ ।। viśeṣapūjāmubhayor gandhapuṣpapavitrakaiḥ ।। vikirān saṃhitān pūrvaṃ vārdhānyāḥ kalpayedadhaḥ ।।
cakrapaṭṭisavajrāditriśūlāntānyanekaśaḥ ।। vārdhānyastrasya sarve te raśmibhūtā vyavasthitāḥ ।। tenaitaṃ yajñarakṣārthaṃ yāgādau kalaśaṃ nyaset ।। bhagavaṃstvatprasādena yāgaṃ nirvartayāmyaham ।।
anujñātotthito yāyād arghahasto digīśvarān ।। gandhapuṣpapavitrādyaiḥ pūjayettān prayatnataḥ ।। tato maṇḍalakaṃ madhye yāgabhūmau prakalpayet ।। śivāmbhasāstramantreṇa samprokṣya tvavaguṇṭhayet ।।
vāyavye pūjayeddevi gandhapuṣpairanukramāt ।। tatastu madhyadeśasthaṃ yogapīṭhaṃ prakalpayet ।। pūjayitvā pavitrādyais trirāvaraṇasaṃyutam ।। mantrasandhānakaṃ pūrvaṃ nāḍīsandhānameva ca ।।
naivedyān vividhākārān dattvā mudrāṃ pradarśayet ।। paścādbaliḥ pradātavyo mātṛṇāṃ bhūtasaṃhate ।। tataḥ snāyādathoddhūlya athavācamya suvrate ।। bhairavaṃ pūjayettatra vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।।
tataścaruṃ ca śrapayet sthālīṃ saṃgṛhya nirvraṇām ।। candanādyairvilimpettāṃ mṛṣṭadhūpena dhūpayet ।। darbheṇāstrasvarūpeṇa kalpayenmaṇḍalaṃ priye ।। āsanaṃ tatra vinyasyed anantādiśivāntakam ।।
trirāvaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ gandhapuṣpairanukramāt ।। cullīṃ samprokṣya cāstreṇa kuṇḍavaccārcayettataḥ ।। kṣīraṃ prokṣya śivāmbhobhis taṇḍulāṃśca samāsataḥ ।। mūlamantreṇa deveśi ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ ।।
taptābhidhāraṃ susvinne aṅgaiścaiva prakalpayet ।। bhūmau maṇḍalakaṃ kṛtvā praṇavenāvatārayet ।। bhairaveṇa ṣaḍaṅgena vaṣaḍjātiyutena ca ।। sthālyāṃ tasyopari nyasya sampātaṃ mantrasaṃhitām ।।
aṣṭotkṛṣṭaśatenaiva parāmṛtamanusmaran ।। khaṭikātilājyasampātaṃ mūlamantreṇa kārayet ।। śivāgnisādhakebhyaśca śivāyāgraṃ nivedayet ।। caruṃ pātre tu saṃgṛhya pūjayedbhairaveṇa tu ।।
hṛdādyāvaraṇasthānāṃ daśamāṃśaṃ nivedayet ।। bhairavasya śataṃ homyam aṅgānāṃ tu daśāṃśakam ।। vināyake śataṃ homyaṃ bhūparigrahaṇe tathā ।। prāyaścittanimittaṃ tu anulomavilomake ।।
bhairavaṃ pūjayitvātha prārthyānujñāṃ varānane ।। dvāre maṇḍalakaṃ kṛtvā darbhaṃ tasyopari nyaset ।। samapādaṃ stabdhakāyaṃ saumyānanakṛtāñjalim ।। bhasmanā tāḍayenmūrdhni astramantreṇa cālabhet ।।
śivaṃ nyāsāṅgasahitaṃ pūjayedbhairaveṇa tu ।। pūjayedbhairaveṇaiva mukhaṃ pracchādayettathā ।। devasyābhimukhaṃ kṛtvā puṣpaṃ prāṇau pradāpayet ।। vidyāmantragaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ kāraṇaṃ sasadāśivam ।।
daṇḍavaddharaṇīṃ gatvā praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ ।। utthāpya hastān saṃgṛhya dakṣiṇāṃ mūrtimānayet ।। tasyopari śiśuṃ nyasya ūrdhvakāyamudaṅmukham ।। upaveśya tataḥ kṛtvā sakalīkaraṇe vidhim ।।
gandhadigdhau karau kṛtvā astreṇa pariśodhayet ।। anantamāsanaṃ kalpyaṃ bhairavāṅgāni vinyaset ।। āgneyīṃ dhāraṇāṃ dhyātvā nirdahyāstreṇa taṃ śiśum ।। bhasmībhūtaṃ tataḥ śāntaṃ plāvayedamṛtena tu ।।
śaktinyāsaṃ nyasetpūrvaṃ kamalaṃ praṇavena tu ।। mūrtimantraṃ samuccārya mūrtibhūtaṃ prakalpayet ।। mantranyāso yathāpūrvam aṣṭātriṃśatkalāvadhi ।। sphaṭikābhā tathā kṛṣṇā raktā śuklā ca pītakā ।।
dhāmnāvāhya tathāṅgāni nyasyāntaḥkaraṇaṃ bhavet ।। dhāma proccārya sandadhyāt sabāhyābhyantaraṃ punaḥ ।। dhāmoccārya ca sandhāya śiṣyamūrdhni karaṃ nyaset ।। utthāpya dattvā puṣpaṃ tu añjalau bhairaveṇa tu ।।
nirgatya vandayeddevaṃ daṇḍavat triḥ pradakṣiṇam ।। śivapūjāgnikāryādau sakalīkṛtavigrahaḥ ।। nītvā kuṇḍasamīpaṃ taṃ śiṣyahastāviyogataḥ ।। praṇavenāsanaṃ dattvā tasyopari śiśuṃ nyaset ।।
mūlaṃ śiṣyasya hastasthaṃ sāgramācāryajaṅghayoḥ ।। saivātra darbhabhūtā tu gurunāḍyāṃ layaṃ gatā ।। tayā nāḍyā praveṣṭavyaṃ śiṣyasya hṛdaye sakṛt ।। dīkṣākāle yataścaivaṃ tadarthaṃ nāḍisaṃhatiḥ ।।
sampātaṃ sarvamantraistu dhruveṇājyāhutiṃ kṣipet ।। heti śiṣyasya śirasi sampātaḥ śivacoditaḥ ।। kuṇḍasthāḥ pūjitā ye tu dhāmādyāvaraṇāntagāḥ ।। ekaikasyātra mantrasya āhutitritayena tu ।।
bhairavāya śataṃ hutvā hṛdādau daśakaṃ hutiḥ ।। mantrāṇāṃ dīpanaṃ kuryād dhāmādyastrāvadhi kramāt ।। praṇavādiphaḍantena āhutīḥ pratipādayet ।। pāśānāṃ bandhanārthāya mantrāṇāṃ dīpanaṃ smṛtam ।।
ācāryaḥ karaṇaṃ proktaḥ śivarūpo yataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। krūrajātyanurūpeṇa vācakān yojayet sadā ।। saumyajātiyutān saumye saumyarūpān vicintayet ।। triguṇaṃ triguṇīkṛtya pāśabandhanasūtrakam ।।
pūjayitvā vidhānena gandhapuṣpādidhūpakaiḥ ।। śiṣyasya stabdhadehasya nāḍībhūtaṃ vicintayet ।। oṃkārādi svanāmnā tu namaskārāvasānakam ।। gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ pūjya kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet ।।
śivāmbho astreṇa samprokṣya śiṣyasya hṛdayaṃ punaḥ ।। huṃkāroccārayogena recakena viśeddhṛdi ।। kadambagolakākāraṃ sphurattārakasannibham ।। dhāmnā cāṅkuśarūpeṇa karṣecchaktyavadhi kramāt ।।
saṃhāramudrayā yojyaṃ sūtre nāḍīprakalpite ।। bhairaveṇāhutīstisraḥ sannidhānasya hetave ।। bandyāścedyāstathā dāhyāḥ sūtrasthāne na vigrahe ।। caitanyarodhakāstvete kāryakāraṇarūpiṇaḥ ।।
ādhārarūpaṃ naimittaṃ śarīrabhuvanādikam ।। tāṃścāvalokayet sūtre bandhyabandhanahetutaḥ ।। svanāmapraṇavādyena śāntyatītādyanukramāt ।। huṃphakārāntayogenāgṛhya saṃhāramudrayā ।।
evaṃ śāntyādikān pāśān sthānāt saṃgṛhya yojayet ।। trayāṇāṃ vyāpikā śaktiḥ kriyākhyā pārameśvarī ।। ādheyagraha ādhāraṃ gṛhītaṃ bhāvayet paśoḥ ।। śāntyatītākrameṇaiva āhutīnāṃ trayaṃ trayam ।।
svanāmajātiphaṭkāradhāmabhiśca trayaṃ trayam ।। dīptāḥ pāśāstato bandhyās tāḍanagrahaṇādinā ।। dhāmnā ca sampuṭīkṛtya svanāmnā ca sakṛtsakṛt ।। bandhane parimāṇaṃ ca karmaṇo viṣayasya ca ।।
pāśān saṃsthāpya pātre tu saṃpātaṃ juhuyāt sakṛt ।। nītvā samarpayet kumbhe pāśān saṃrakṣa he vibho ।। shtaṇḍile śivakumbhe ca śivāgnau ca prapūjayet ।। utthāpya pañcagavyādīn dadyādvai bhairaveṇa tu ।।
ekasmin maṇḍale viṣṭaḥ pañcagavyaṃ śiśuḥ pibet ।। ācamya dantakāṣṭhaṃ tu tṛtīye maṇḍale sthitaḥ ।। pūrvaṃ paścāttathaiśordhvaṃ cottarasyāṃ ca śobhanam ।। ācāryo juhuyāt paścāt prāyaścittaṃ śivena tu ।।
aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā prāyaścittād viśuddhyati ।। mantrāṃśca daśabhāgena vahnau naivedyadāpanam ।। stotraṃ vādyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā caruṃ prāśya visarjayet ।। recakena tu saṃgṛhya bhairavaṃ tamanusmaran ।।
agniṣṭhaṃ vai pūrakeṇa gṛhītvā sthāpayet punaḥ ।। kusumādibhirabhyarcya kumbha eva tu bhairavam ।। śivāmbhasā tu samprokṣya śiṣye śayyāṃ prakalpayet ।। pūrvāśirā gṛhī kāryo yatirvai dakṣiṇāśirāḥ ।।
siddhārtharocanādyaiśca rakṣāṃ kuryādasiṃ smaran ।। kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaiva śiṣyaṃ tu svāpayettataḥ ।। balistu kalpitaḥ pūrvaṃ sarvabhūteṣvathādarāt ।। bhūtā ye vividhākārā divyabhaumāntarikṣagāḥ ।।
dhruvādisarvabhūtāśca aindrādyāśāsthitāśca ye ।। namaskāreṇa sampūjya gandhairdhūpairanukramāt ।। koṇasthān kṣetrapālāṃśca patitāñchvapacānapi ।। sakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā krameṇa prāśayeccarum ।।
prāṅmukha udaṅmukho vā maṇḍalasthaḥ pṛthakpṛthak ।। prāśyaivaṃ sakalīkṛtya rakṣāṃ pūrvavadeva ca ।। bhairavadhyānayogena samādhau jāgradeva vā ।। sakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pūrvavat praviśedgṛham ।।
praṇamya śirasā hṛṣṭo guroḥ svapnānnivedayet ।। svapneṣu madirāpānam āmamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇam ।। bhakṣaṇaṃ dadhibhaktasya śvetavastrānulepanam ।। siṃhāsanaṃ rathaṃ yānaṃ dhvajaṃ rājyābhiṣecanam ।।
darśanaṃ śrīsarasvatyoḥ śubhanāryavagūhanam ।। ācāryaiḥ saha saṃvādaṃ kṛtvā svapne prasiddhyati ।। bhāskarodayanaṃ caiva prajvalantaṃ hutāśanam ।। harmyasyārohaṇaṃ caiva prāsādaśikhare api vā ।।
vimānagamanaṃ caiva siddhamantrasya darśanam ।। guṭikāṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca khaḍgapādukarocanāḥ ।। śaktiṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ padmam akṣasūtraṃ manaḥśilām ।। dṛṣṭvā siddhyati svapnānte kṣitilābhaṃ vraṇaṃ tathā ।।
jvalatpitṛvanaṃ ramyaṃ vīravīreśibhirvṛtam ।। mahāpāśoḥ saṃvibhāgaṃ labdhvā devebhya ādarāt ।। suhutaṃ cānalaṃ dīptaṃ pūjitaṃ vā prapaśyati ।। mātṛbhirbhairavaścaiva mātṛrudragaṇaiḥ saha ।।
śubhāḥ svapnā mayākhyātā aśubhāṃśca nibodha me ।। andhakūpe ca patanam atha paṅke nimajjanam ।। kartanaṃ karṇanāsābhyām atha vā hastapādayoḥ ।। vetālakrūrasatvānāṃ tathaiva kālapūruṣāḥ ।।
raktākṣī strī ca yaṃ svapne puruṣaṃ tvavagūhayet ।। gṛhaprasādabhedaṃ ca śayyāvastrāsaneṣu ca ।। kharoṣṭraśvasṛgāleṣu kaṅkagṛdhrabakeṣu ca ।। bhakṣaṇam pakvamāṃsasya raktamālyānulepanam ।।
hasanaṃ valganaṃ svapne mlānasragdāmadhāraṇam ।। udvāhaṃ ca tathā svapne dṛṣṭvā naiva prasidhyati ।। śubhāstatrānumedyāstu aśubheṣu tu homayet ।। pūrvavat sakalīkṛtya vighnoccāṭanarakṣaṇam ।।
lokapālāṃstu saṃpūjya śivakumbhaṃ ca sthaṇḍilam ।। prāyaścittaṃ tataḥ paścād dusvapnārthaṃ yaduktavān ।। nirmālyāpanayaṃ kṛtvā bhūmiṃ saṃśodhya pūrvavat ।। nityāhnike samāpte tu naimittikamathācaret ।।
bhāvena gandhapuṣpādyaiḥ tato maṇḍalamālikhet ।। dhāmnā tu rajasāṃ pātaḥ sitādyaśvāgamoditaḥ ।। nityakarmasamāptau tu kuryānnaimittikaṃ budhaḥ ।। ātmarakṣāstraprākāradvārapālādipūjanam ।।
astraprākāramāropya kavacenāvaguṇṭhanam ।। śivāmbhaḥ śivahastaṃ ca arghatrayaprakalpanam ।। maṇḍalasyāgrato bhūtvā maṇḍalaṃ prokṣya cāsinā ।। aṣṭottaraśataṃ dhāmnā rajodoṣairviśuddhyati ।।
prākāraṃ bhāvayedastraṃ maṇḍalaṃ praviśet tataḥ ।। anantamāsanaṃ prāgvac chivāntaṃ praṇavena tu ।। pūrvoktavidhinā pūjya naivedyāni nivedayet ।। japadhyānādikaṃ kṛtvā agniṣṭhaṃ bhairavaṃ yajet ।।
ātmano niṣkaloccāraṃ kṛtvā kumbhe niveśayet ।। maṇḍalasthasya savyena punarvāmena rocayet ।। evaṃ sādhanakaṃ kṛtvā tatastarpaṇamārabhet ।। prāyaścittaviśuddhyarthaṃ kuryādaṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।।
ācāryoṭhārdhahastastu maṇḍalaṃ praviśettataḥ ।। mudrāṃ baddhvā praṇamyādau jānubhyāmavaniṃ gataḥ ।। snānādhivāsanādyaṃ yan maṇḍale agnau ca yatkṛtam ।। idānīṃ śiṣyadehe tu sakalīkaraṇādikā ।।
evamastvityanujñātaḥ parameśena vīrarāṭ ।। paśvarthāya kṛtaṃ yattu tadgṛhītvārdhapātrakam ।। praṇavāsanaṃ kuśairnyasya śuciṃ śiṣyaṃ niveśayet ।। maṇḍale kalpite śiṣyaṃ mūrtibhūtaṃ prakalpayet ।।
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ nyāsaṃ mantrasaṃdhānameva ca ।। mūrdhni saṃpātayettejaḥ pāśāṅkuravināśanam ।। vastraṃ saṃprokṣya toyena kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet ।। netre baddhā tu netreṇa puṣpaṃ pāṇau pradāpayet ।।
puṣpapātavaśānnāma kuryādvai sādhakasya ca ।। mukhamudghāṭya taṃ śiṣyaṃ śivāya praṇipātayet ।। agnikuṇḍasamīpe tu ācāryaḥ paśunā saha ।। pūrvannāḍisaṃdhānaṃ tad arthaṃ cāhutitrayam ।।
pūrṇāhutiṃ tato dattvā prāyaścittāni homayet ।। jātyuddhāre dhruveṇaiva dvijatvāpādane tathā ।। praṇavenāhutīstisro rudrāṃśāpādane tathā ।। recakena tato gatvā śiṣyadehe viśeddhṛdi ।।
viśleṣakaraṇaṃ kṛtvā caitanyasya vidhānataḥ ।। aṅkuśena samākṛṣya dvādaśānte tu kārayet ।। saṃhāramudrayā samyak pūrakeṇa viśeddhṛdi ।। tyajantaṃ devatāṣaṭkaṃ tataścāpi svakaṃ padam ।।
saṃhāramudrayoddhṛtya śiṣyasya hṛdi yojayet ।। ādhānādyāvadantyeṣṭiṃ dvijatve saṃskṛto bhavet ।। caitanyasyāpi saṃskāram ādhānāntyeṣṭitaḥ param ।। śatahomaṃ sahasraṃ vā hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ ।।
śravaṇe adhyayane home pūjanādau tathaiva ca ।। atha dīkṣādhvaśuddhyarthaṃ bhuktimuktiphalārthinām ।। guruḥ saṃpṛcchate śiṣyaṃ dvividhaṃ phalakāṅkṣiṇam ।। vāsanābhedataḥ prāptiḥ sādhyamantrapracoditā ।।
vāsanābhedato bhinnaḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ ca gurostathā ।। śivamantraviśuddhādhvā sādhyamantraniyojitaḥ ।। trividhāyāstu siddhervai so atrārhaḥ śivasādhakaḥ ।। karmakṛtphalamākāṅkṣañ śubhaikastho aśubhojjhitaḥ ।।
gṛhastho vā yatirvāsāv āśramaikatamasthitaḥ ।। bālabāliśavṛddhastrībhogabhugvyādhitātmanām ।। vidvaddvandvasahānā tu sabījā kīrtitā priye ।। viśeṣasamayācārā mantrākhye ye prakīrtitāḥ ।।
sabījā sā tuvijñeyā putrakācāryayoḥ sthitā ।। pāśasūtrakamādāya śiṣyadehe avalambayet ।। kumbhamaṇḍalavahnisthaś cādhvātmasthaḥ śiśośca yaḥ ।। ṣaḍvidhasyādhvamārgasya sādhāraṇagatasya tu ।।
mūlamantrāṣṭaśatikamadhvasaṃdhānahetutaḥ ।। bhuvanavyāptitā tattveṣv anantādiśivāntake ।। tattvāntarbhāvinaḥ sarve vācyavācakayogataḥ ।। hṛdādyā vācakāstāsāṃ bījāmantrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।
pṛthivyādikalā jñeyā brahmādyāḥ kāraṇāśca te ।। trirāhutiṃ dhruveṇaiva adhvaśuddhirato bhavet ।। tadeva pādādārabhya pṛthivyādikramānnyaset ।। upasthāpanamantro ayaṃ vyāptiṃ dhyātvādhvasaṃsthitām ।।
tasyāṃ ca bhuvanānāṃ ca śatamaṣṭottarāvadhi ।। mantrau dvāveva vijñeyau adhvaṣaṭkaṃ vibhāvayet ।। māyīyā bhuvanākārā malāḥ karma ca saṃsthitāḥ ।। bhogahetuśca karma syād abhilāṣo malo atra tu ।।
tadviśuddhyai ca dīkṣā ca kriyate sā yathāvidhi ।। hṛdā saṃkalpya vāgīśīṃ vyāpikāṃ sarvayoniṣu ।। samakālamṛtutvena vāgīśīṃ saṃnidhāpayet ।। oṃkāreṇāhutistisro vāgīśīsaṃnidhāpane ।।
recakenātmano gatvā chindyāttasyāsinā hṛdaḥ ।। dhruveṇa tatsthaṃ saṃpuṭya caitanyaṃ mudrayātmani ।। dvādaśāntāttu saṃgṛhya yojayedbhavamudrayā ।। saṃyojya tasyāṃ caitanyaṃ śarīrāṇyadhvani sṛjet ।।
yugapadbhinnabhogāni deśakālaśarīrataḥ ।। bhinādehā visṛjyante garbhe vāgīśiyoniṣu ।। yugapatsarvagarbheṣu dehā vividharūpakāḥ ।। garbheṣu garbhaniṣpatti bhairaveṇāhutitrayam ।।
sarvayoniṣu dehāste yugapadvṛddhimāgatāḥ ।। tadabhāvānna bhogaḥ syāt tadarthaṃ mārjanaṃ smṛtam ।। layaḥ paramayā prītyā sukhaduḥkhādike apyalam ।। āhutīnāṃ śataṃ homyaṃ dhāmnā niṣkṛtaye punaḥ ।।
niṣkṛtyante viśuddhyettad bhūlokasamavasthitam ।। catvāriṃśad dvijatvāya vakṣyante bhuvanādhvani ।। eteṣāṃ śodhanaṃ devi rudrāṃśāpādanaṃ tathā ।। viṣayā bhuvanākārā ye kecidbhogyarūpiṇaḥ ।।
viśleṣo niṣkṛterbhogāt bhogābhāve sa hi smṛtaḥ ।। bhoktṛtvābhāvastatraiva śarīreṇa tu yatkṛtam ।। dhāmnā cāhutayastisro viśleṣakaraṇāya ca ।। pāśā dehe tu māyīyāḥ kalādyā bhūtakāvadhi ।।
bhogābhāvādvipadyante śarīrāṇi sahasradhā ।। evaṃ pāśatrayasyāpi viśleṣo dīkṣayocyate ।। pūrṇāhutiṃ śivenaiva vauṣaḍjātiyutena ca ।। uddhārāyāhutīstisraḥ punardhāmnā tu dāpayet ।।
mudrayā prāgvidhānena ātmasthaṃ pūrayedddhṛdi ।। śiṣyadehe niveśyaitan nāḍīrandhreṇa pūrvavat ।। kalāśuddhyavasāne tu brahmāṇaṃ kāraṇādhipam ।। śabdasparśo tyajet tasmin dhruvādyau nāmasaṃyutau ।।
tisṛbhistisṛbhirhomāt puryaṣṭāṃśaṃ nivedayet ।। brahmāṇaṃ pūjayitvā tu homaṃ kṛtvā visarjayet ।। hutvāvalokayettatra viśuddhaṃ pāśajālakam ।। mumukṣornirapekṣatvāt prārabdhrekaṃ na śodhayet ।।
prākkarmāgāmi caikasthaṃ bhāvayitvā ca dīkṣayet ।। prāktanāgamikasyāpi adharmakṣayakāriṇī ।। prārabdhadehabhede tu bhuṅkte sa hyaṇimādikān ।। sakale niṣkale vāpi śiṣyācāryavaśādbhaved ।।
samayācārapāśaṃ hi dīkṣitaḥ pālayettu yaḥ ।। samayācārapāśaṃ tu nirbījāyāṃ viśodhayet ।। sadyonirvāṇadā dīkṣā nirbījā sā dvitīyakā ।। dīkṣāvasāne śuddhiḥ syād dehatyāge paraṃ padam ।।
phalaṃ tu vividhākāraṃ niṣpādyeta sudīkṣayā ।। kriyā kāle prayoktavyā guruṇā bhaktipūrvikā ।। karoti mantratattvajñaḥ śivāveśī guruḥ kṣaṇāt ।। śuddhamuccārayedhrasvam aśuddhaṃ dīrghameva ca ।।
praṇavādinivṛttistu pratiṣṭhā tadanantaram ।। āvāhya sthāpya saṃpūjyāhutīstisraḥ prapātayet ।। gulphādārabhya nābhyantaṃ śiṣyadehe adhvakalpanam ।। ṣaṭpañcāśadbhuvanikā trayoviṃśativarṇikā ।।
mukhyā hyete smṛtāḥ pāśāḥ sūkṣmānantarvibhāvayet ।। ṣaṭkośānviṣayān pañca tadantarbhāvayetsadā ।। bhairaveṇāhutīstisraḥ tasyā vāgīśikalpanā ।। prokṣaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ cheda ākarṣagrahaṇe tathā ।।
yojanaṃ garbhadhāritvaṃ jananaṃ pūrvavatkramāt ।। adhikārasthathā bhogo layo niṣkṛtireva ca ।। viśleṣaśca hṛdā homyaḥ pāśacchedastathāsinā ।। sadāśivatanau sthitvā viśleṣādīni kārayet ।।
svanāmnoccārayedviṣṇuṃ dhyātvāvāhya tu sthāpayet ।। rasaṃ puryaṣṭakāṃśaṃ tu arpayedviṣṇave sadā ।। kalāsaṃdhiryathāpūrvaṃ hrasvadīrghaprayogataḥ ।। kalādvayavinirmuktaḥ paśurūrdhvagamotsukaḥ ।।
sthāpayitvā saṃpūjya juhuyādāhutitrayam ।। puṃstattvādyāvanmāyāntaṃ vidyāyā vyāptiriṣyate ।। padaviṃśatirākhyātā varṇāḥ sapta prakīrtitāḥ ।। praṇavena samāvāhya vyāpinīṃ sarvayoniṣu ।।
tataḥ śivāmbhasā śiṣyaṃ prokṣya cāstreṇa tāḍayet ।। ātmano revakenaiva śiṣyadehe viśeddhṛdi ।। dvādaśāntāttu saṃgṛhya ātmasthaṃ pūrvavatkuru ।। pūrvavaddvyāpakaṃ tasya caitanyaṃ sarvayoniṣu ।।
śikhayā śatahomāttu vidyāyā niṣkṛtirbhavet ।। tato asya vinyaseddevi gandharūpe dhruvāhutī ।। vāgīśīṃ ca visarjyaivaṃ kalāsaṃdhiśca pūrvavat ।। saṃdhānārthaṃ tu mūlena juhuyādāhutitrayam ।।
prameyabhāvanāṃ kṛtvā pūjayet kusumādibhiḥ ।। tattvānāṃ tritaye vyāptir varṇānāṃ traya eva ca ।। mantrau dvau ṣaḍvidho adhvaivaṃ mukhyāḥ pāśā ime smṛtāḥ ।। vagīśīṃ kalpayettatra pūrveṇa vidhināhutiḥ ।।
chedākarṣagrahaṃ caiva yogadhāritvajanma ca ।। sarve te mūlamantreṇa āhutitritayena tu ।। viśleṣaṃ pāśachedaṃ tu kuryādastreṇa daiśikaḥ ।। svanāmnā praṇavādyena īśamāvāhya pūjayet ।।
svanāmnā praṇavādyaṃ tu svāhānte buddhimarpayet ।। vāgīśīṃ pūjayitvā tu tarpayitvā visarjayet ।। hrasvadīrghavibhāgena juhuyādāhutitrayam ।। kalopasthāpanaṃ paścād dhruveṇa juhuyātpriye ।।
śāntyatītāṃ samāvāhya sthāpayetpūjayetpunaḥ ।। bindurnādastathā śaktiḥ śivatattve vyavasthitāḥ ।। bhuvanāni tu sūkṣmāṇi śāntyatīte tu bhāvayet ।। śivasyordhve śivo jñeyo yatra yukto na jāyate ।।
kalāśca pañca vijñeyās tattvaṣaṭtriśadeva tu ।। ekāśītipadānyatra varṇārdhaśatikā smṛtā ।। etasmiñśuddhimāpane muktimāpnoti dīkṣitaḥ ।। saṃpūjya kusumādayistu tadyonau pūrvavatpaśum ।।
niṣkṛtau śatahomaṃ tu mūlamantreṇa kalpayet ।। graheṇātmasthatatsthatvaṃ praṇavena paśoḥ smṛtam ।। namaskāreṇa saṃsthāpya puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjya tarpayet ।। praṇavādi samuccārya manaḥsaṃjñāṃ namastathā ।।
āhutitritayaṃ hutvā puryaṣṭāṃśādviśuddhyati ।। puṣpādibhiḥ samabhyarcya vāgīśīṃ tadanantaram ।। kṣamasva devadeveśi paśvarthaṃ kheditā mayā ।। visarjyaivaṃ kalā bhāvyā śāntyatītā layaṃ gatā ।।
ātmatattvavibhāgena dhāmnā vai juhuyācchatam ।। māyātattvāvadhi jñeyaṃ daiśikena mahādhvare ।। vidyātatve tu hotavyaṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ priye ।। sadāśivāntamadhvānaṃ vidyātattvaṃ vinirdiśet ।।
tadviśuddhyai sa homaḥ syād vidyātattve tu yaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। tacchuddhyarthaṃ śive tattve mūlamantreṇa homayet ।। tattvatrayaviśuddhyante śikhācchedaṃ tu kalpayet ।। vyāpinīṃ sarvatattvānāṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam ।।
kartarīṃ śikhayāmantrya śikhayā cchedayecchikhām ।। snānaṃ samācarecchiṣyaḥ gurorācamanaṃ bhavet ।। praviśya sakalīkṛtya pūrṇayā juhuyācchikhām ।। praviśya sakalīkṛtya śivahastānupūjanam ।।
puṣpādibhiraśeṣaistu tato vijñāpayecchivam ।। paśuṃ saṃgṛhya saṃśodhya śikhācchedāvasānakam ।। tvacchaktyaiva tu gantavyam āśu dhruvapadaṃ śivam ।। ājñā me dīyatāṃ nātha śiṣyaṃ saṃyojayāmyaham ।।
ardhahasto vrajedagnim śiṣyamāhūya prokṣayet ।। antaḥkaraṇavinyāsaṃ nāḍīsaṃdhānapūrvakam ।। daśabhāgavibhāgena yathā dravyānusārataḥ ।। sakṛdāhutiyogena adhikāro vivarjyatām ।।
yojanīyaṃ prayogaṃ tu adhunā kathayāmi te ।। ṣaḍvidhādhvavibhāgaṃ tu prāṇaikatra yathāsthitam ।। śūnyaṃ samarasaṃ jñeyaṃ tyāgaṃ saṃyogamudbhavam ।। ātmavidyāśivavyāptim evaṃ jñātvā tu yojayet ।।
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulaścāro hṛtpadmādyāvaśaktitaḥ ।। saṃcarantaṃ vibhāgena yathāvattaṃ śṛṇuṣva me ।। nāsikāgre dvitīyaṃ tu śaktyante tu tṛtīyakam ।। vidite tu pare tattve tatrastho api na bādhyate ।।
hṛdgataḥ punaruttiṣṭhed budhyamānaḥ sa ucyate ।। atītaḥ suprabuddhastu unmanastvaṃ tadā bhavet ।। sunirvāṇaṃ paraṃ śuddhaṃ gurupāramparāgatam ।। adhvaṣṭkaṃ yathā prāṇe saṃsthitaṃ kathayāmi te ।।
bhuvanādhvā sa vijñeyas tattvādhvā ca tathaiva hi ।। nivṛttiśca pratiṣṭhā ca adhobhāge pravartike ।। tadatītaḥ paro bhāvaḥ tadūrdhvam padamavyayam ।। vyāpinyādyātmikā yāśca vyāpyavyāpakabhedataḥ ।।
kalādhvaivaṃ samākhyāto varṇādhvānaṃ nibodha me ।। sthitāḥ pañcaśatā bhedaiḥ śāstreṣvānantyakoṭiṣu ।। utpadyante layaṃ yānti yatra śabdo layaṃ gataḥ ।। yuktaḥ sarvagato devi dharmādharmavivarjitaḥ ।।
adho vai yātyadharmeṇa dharmeṇordhvaṃ vrajetpunaḥ ।। varṇādhvaivaṃ samākhyātaḥ padādhvā procyate adhunā ।। varṇātmakāni tānyatra varṇāḥ prāṇātmakāḥ sthitāḥ ।। padādhvaivaṃ samākhyātaḥ mantrādhvānaṃ nibodha me ।।
padikādaśikā sā ca prāṇe carati nityaśaḥ ।। ardhacandro nirodhī ca nādo nādānta eva ca ।। unmanā ca tato atītā tadatītaṃ nirāmayam ।। hakārastu smṛtaḥ prāṇaḥ svapravṛtto halākṛtiḥ ।।
makāramātrayā yukto varṇoccāro bhavetsphuṭaḥ ।। nādo asya vadanaṃ proktaḥ vadanaṃ śabdamīrayet ।। brahmaviṣṇvīśamārgeṇa caranvai sarvajantuṣu ।। vyāpinīṃ samanāṃ tyaktvā vrajedunmanayā śivam ।।
haṃsoccāraḥ samākhyātaḥ kāraṇaiśca samanvitaḥ ।। hṛdi tyāgo bhavettasya ukāro viṣṇuvācakaḥ ।। tālumadhye tyajettaṃ tu binduścaiveśvaraḥ svayam ।। lalāṭānmūrdhaparyantaṃ tyāgastasya vidhīyate ।।
mūrdhamadhye tyajecchaktiṃ tadūrdhve vyāpinīṃ tyajet ।। sūkṣmasūkṣmatarairbhāvair evamevaṃ tyajetpriye ।। sūkṣmo atyantaṃ paro bhāvas tv abhāvaḥ sa vidhīyate ।। tasyāparaṃ punaḥ śūnyaṃ saṃsparśaṃ ca tato aparam ।।
pañcabhūtātmabhuvanaṃ kāraṇaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitam ।। bhuvaneśatvamāpnoti śivaṃ dhyātvā tu tanmayaḥ ।। pūrvoktalakṣaṇaṃ yaśca tanmayatvamavāpnuyāt ।। pūrvoktarūpakadhyānāt siddhyantyatra na saṃśayaḥ ।।
tanmayatvaṃ yadāpnoti yogināmadhipo bhavet ।। sparśadhyānācca sparśātmā jagataḥ kāraṇaṃ bhavet ।। samanadhyānayogena yogī sarvajñatāṃ vrajet ।। sarvendriyamanotītas tv alakṣyo abhāva ucyate ।।
sarvopādhivinirmuktam abhāvaṃ labhate padam ।। tuṭiṣoḍaśasaṃyuktaḥ prāṇastu samudāhṛtaḥ ।। ahorātravibhāgena kurvantyudayameva te ।। sarvaṃ kālaṃ tyajetprāṇe yathāvatkathayāmi te ।।
tadādiḥ saṃsthitaḥ kālaḥ sarvaṃ carati vāṅmayam ।। muhūrtaścāpyahorātraḥ pakṣo māsa ṛtustathā ।। kalpaścaiva mahākalpaḥ śaktyante taṃ parityajet ।। sa ca saptadaśo jñeyaḥ parārdhaparataḥ sthitaḥ ।।
sarvakālaṃ tu kālasya vyāpakaḥ paramo avyayaḥ ।। nityo nityodito vyāpī ādirūpaṃ na saṃtyajet ।। kālatyāgo bhavedevaṃ śūnyabhāvastvathocyate ।। śūnyatrayaṃ calaṃ hyetat tadadho madhya ūrdhvataḥ ।।
unmanāyāṃ tathā ṣaṣṭhaṃ ṣaḍete sāmayāḥ sthitāḥ ।। ṣaṭ śūnyāni parityajya saptame tu layaṃ kuru ।। aśūnyaṃ śūnyamityuktaṃ śūnyaṃ cābhāva ucyate ।। sattāmātraṃ paraṃ śāntaṃ tatpadaṃ kimapi sthitam ।।
tatra tatra paraṃ śūnyaṃ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitam ।। sthūlasūkṣmaprabhedena tadekaṃ saṃvyavasthitam ।। śūnyabhāvaḥ samākhyātaḥ sāmarasyaṃ nibodha me ।। tṛtīyaṃ nāḍigaṃ kuryāc chaktau kuryāccaturthakam ।।
tātvaḥ samaraso devi saptamastu vidhīyate ।। paścādātmani saṃyojya lolībhūtaṃ vicintayet ।। yāvatyo nāḍayo devi tiryagūrdhvamadhaḥsthitāḥ ।। tāsu ye vāyavaste api prāṇe samarasīgatāḥ ।।
tato vai uccarenmantraḥ nāde līnaṃ vicintayet ।। vāmadakṣiṇamadhye tu tato nādaṃ pramocayet ।। brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśca īśvaraḥ śiva eva ca ।। tasminsamuccarennādaṃ yāvacchaktau layaṃ gataḥ ।।
sarvaṃ śaktimayaṃ tatra sarvaṃ samarasībhavet ।। samantādvyāpnuyādyasmād vyāpinītyabhidhīyate ।। sā ca sarvagatā jñeyā sāmarasyena saṃsthitā ।। taṃ prāpya tanmayatvaṃ hi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।
sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva cetanācetanasthitam ।। prasahya cañcalītyeva yogināmapi yanmanaḥ ।। mano na calate tasya sarvāvasthāgatasya tu ।। calitvā yāsyate kutra sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ yataḥ ।।
yatra yatra nirūpyeta nāśivaṃ vidyate kvacit ।। yasyaivaṃ sarvato bhāvaḥ so api sarvagato bhavet ।। prathamaṃ prāṇaviṣuvan mātraṃ jñeyaṃ dvitīyakam ।। pañcamaṃ śaktiviṣuvat ṣaṣṭhaṃ vai kāla ucyate ।।
ātmānaṃ ca manaḥ prāṇe saṃyojya viṣuvadbhavet ।। mantramuccārayettāvad yāvannānyamanā bhavet ।। māntraṃ viṣuvadityuktaṃ nāḍisthaṃ tannibodha me ।। suṣumnā nāma sā jñeyā nābheḥ śaktyā śivaṃ gatā ।।
praśāntaṃ viṣuvaccaivam adhunā kathayāmi te ।। tānyadhastātparityajya kāraṇāni ṣaḍeva tu ।। praśāntaḥ stimito jñeyaḥ stimito niścalaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। evaṃbhāvaṃ samāsthāya dīkṣā kāryā tu daiśikaiḥ ।।
śaktimadhyagato nādo nādordhvaṃ ca caredyadā ।। tuṭiḥ ṣoḍaśakā yā tu prāṇānte saṃvyavasthitā ।। taṃ parāparabhāgena punareva tridhā kuru ।। parāparastu yaḥ kālaḥ sa priye aṣṭādaśaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
aparaḥ śaktimūrdhastho vyāpinyāṃ ca dvitīyakaḥ ।। etatṣaṣṭhaṃ samākhyātaṃ saptamaṃ tātvvamucyate ।। tasminyuktastato hyātmā tanmayaśca prajāyate ।। viṣuvadevaṃvidhaṃ jñātvā ko na mucyeta bandhanāt ।।
tyāgaṃ cānubhavaṃ caiva yojanaṃ ca pare pade ।। bhedayejjñānaśūlena jñānaṃ jñeyasya jñāpakam ।। dīpahasto yathā kaścid dravyamālokya cāharet ।। jñānaṃ vai lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ jñeyatatvasya suvrate ।।
na guṇena vinā tattvaṃ na tattvena vinā guṇaḥ ।। gṛhyate hyanumānena pratyakānubhavena ca ।। āgamo jñānamiyuktam anantāḥ śāstrakoṭayaḥ ।। haṃsayogaḥ purākhyātaḥ mātrāsaṃkhyā tvathocyate ।।
nābherūrdhvaṃ vitastyante kaṇṭhādhastātṣaḍaṅgule ।। caturviṃśatitattvaistu brahmā tatra vyavasthitaḥ ।। tattvāṣṭakena saṃyuktaḥ tadūrdhvaṃ caturaṅgulam ।। aṅguladvayamānaṃ tu bhruvormadhyaṃ prakīrtitam ।।
ekādaśāṅgule caiva mūrdhvaṃ devaḥ sadāśivaḥ ।। tadūrdhvaikāṅgulā śaktiḥ śivastatra vyavasthitaḥ ।। tatparaṃ tu paraṃ tattvaṃ pramāṇaparivarjitam ।। akāraśca hakāraśca dvāvetāvekataḥ sthitau ।।
ekamātraḥ sa vijñeyo hṛdayātsaṃpravartate ।। trimātrastu makāro vai tālumadhyagataścaret ।। bhruvormadhye sa uccāras tasya devi vidhīyate ।। nirodhī cārdhapādastu lalāṭānte samuccaret ।।
dvātriṃśadaṃśā śaktistu ṣaṭtriṃśānte samuccaret ।। samanā conmanā cordhvam amātraḥ paramo avyayaḥ ।। evaṃ jñātvā varārohe padārthān bhedayettataḥ ।। mantro vai jñānaśaktiśca mudrā caiva kriyātmikā ।।
paraśca manasā gamya icchāśaktyā tvadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। kriyākaraṇasaṃbandhāt tattvasyoccāraṇaṃ bhavet ।। kriyā karaṇabhedena sā caiva trividhā smṛtā ।। nāḍīścātha dvitīyena dvārāṇi ca nirodhayet ।।
pūrakaṃ kumbhakaṃ kṛtvā sarvadvārāṇi rodhayet ।। dvāramekaṃ tataścordhve pravahattadvicintayet ।। te kumbhakena saṃruddhā vikasanti samantataḥ ।। jihvā tu tāluke yojyā kiṃcidūrdhvaṃ na saṃspṛśet ।।
dantapaṅktī tathaiveha dṛṣṭiścādhordhvavarjitā ।। divyaṃ ca karaṇaṃ kṛtvā tattvasyoccāraṇaṃ kuru ।। nāḍayo granthipadmāśca dehe yāḥsaṃvyavasthitāḥ ।। tato vai jñānaśūlena granthīnbhindan samuccaret ।।
yadākāśasamāyogāt ghoṣaśabdopamo bhavet ।। bhindataḥ kaṇṭhadeśaṃ tu śabdo dhugadhugāyate ।। bindatastālugranthiṃ tu śabdo ghumaghumāyate ।। trayaste aṣṭakalāḥ proktā uparyuparitaḥ kramāt ।।
tattadrūpaṃ bhavettasya sthānabhāvānurūpataḥ ।। binduṃ bhedayato devi śabdo dhumadhumāyate ।। abhinnena kuto mokṣaṃ sabāhyābhyantaraṃ priye ।। bhidyataścārdhacandrasya lalāṭe jhimijhimāyate ।।
tasyāstu bhidyamānāyāḥ śabdaḥ simisimāyate ।। prāṇasya caratastatra yasminsthāne sa tiṣṭhati ।। nirodhinīṃ bhedayitvā tato nādaṃ vrajedbudhaḥ ।। bhedayennādasaṃsthānaṃ brahmarandhraṃ sudurbhidam ।।
śaktimadhyagataḥ prāṇo vaṃśanādāntasaṃnibhaḥ ।। bhidyate ca yadā śaktiḥ śāntaḥ śumaśumastataḥ ।। anubhāvo bavettatra sparśo yadvatpipīlikā ।। yatra yatra caretprāṇas tattadrūpamavāpnuyāt ।।
tasmādvai suprayatnena bhitvā yāti parāṃ gatim ।। manasā tu manastyaktvā jīvaḥ kevalatāṃ vrajet ।। bandhanāśeṣanirmuktaḥ sattāmātrasvarūpakaḥ ।। gṛhāṇāti nāparaṃ bhāvaṃ na paraṃ ca śivātmakam ।।
ātmavyāptirbhavedeṣā śivavyāptirataḥ param ।। aviditvā paraṃ tattvaṃ śivatvaṃ kalpitaṃ tu yaiḥ ।। ātmatattvagatiṃ yānti ātmatattvānurañjitāḥ ।। ātmatattvaṃ tatastyājyaṃ vidyātatve niyojayet ।।
saṃkalpaḥ kramato jñānam unmānaṃ yugapatsthitam ।। vindate hyatra yugapat sārvajñyādiguṇān parān ।। varjanā paramātmatve tasmādvidyeti socyate ।। parasmiṃstejasi vyakte tatrasthaḥ śivatāṃ vrajet ।।
dehaprāṇasthito hyātmā tadvallīyeta tatpade ।। ahameva paro haṃsaḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।। mantrakaraṇakriyāyogād yojayāmi pare śive ।। yadvadvahniśikhātītā tadvadyojayate pare ।।
śiva eko bhaveddevi avibhāgena sarvataḥ ।। bhedanaṃ tu padārthānāṃ tyāgānubhavayojanam ।। saṃkṣepeṇa tu tattvasya vyāptiṃ śṛṇu sureśvari ।। nādaśaktitanuścaiva vyāpinīkaraṇānvitaḥ ।।
tritatvaṃ yatparaṃ proktaṃ tena cāpūritā tanuḥ ।। tattvatrayaṃ paraṃ yacca sarvatattvādhvavarjitam ।। evamācarate yastu ācāraṃ tu śivātmakam ।। tasya darśanasaṃbhāṣāsparśanātsmaraṇādapi ।।
tena saṃyojito jantuḥ brahmahāpi śivo bhavet ।। śiva ācāryarūpeṇa lokānugrahakārakaḥ ।। ācāryasya ca mantrasya śivajñāne śivasya ca ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā vai vīravandite ।।
anyathā prāksvarūpeṇa ye paśyanti narādhamāḥ ।। na tena saha saṃbhāṣā kartavyā tu śivārthinā ।। tasmācchivasamāḥ sarve draṣṭavyā muktimicchatā ।। ācāryaḥ svajānānāṃ ca kulakoṭisahasraśaḥ ।।
evamuktavidhānajño bhāvajñaścāpi daiśikaḥ ।। pūrṇāhutiprayogaṃ tu kathayāmyadhunā tava ।। nābhisthāne sruco mūlam uttānāgramukhaṃ samam ।। puṣpaṃ dattvā srugagre tu darbheṇa sahitau karau ।।
agrato dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ vāmaṃ vai pṛṣṭataḥ priye ।। tato ghṛtena saṃplāvya abhimānaṃ tu kārayet ।। tattvamekaṃ hi sarvatra nānyaṃ bhāvaṃ tu kārayet ।। maṇḍale agnau śiśorantaḥ sādhāraṇavikalpitaḥ ।।
prāṇadhāre samīkṛtya srucā dhārāṃ vinikṣipet ।। nābhisthāne sruco mūlaṃ nayannāsāntagocaram ।। prāṇo api varṇatāṃ yāti ṣaḍvidhādhvamayastu saḥ ।। tasmānmāntre parāmarśe heyopādeyataḥ sthitāḥ ।।
akāraśca ukāraśca makāro bindureva ca ।। śaktiśca vyāpinī hyetāḥ samanā ca tataḥ param ।। kāraṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhirākrāntaṃ mantrasthaṃ heyalakṣaṇam ।। śivatattvaguṇāmodāc chivadharmāvalokakaḥ ।।
ātmavyāptirbhavedeṣā śivavyāptistato anyathā ।। śivavyāptirbhavedeṣā caitanye heturūpiṇī ।। unmanāśca manogrāhyaḥ ātmabodhe sthitonmanāḥ ।। tadā śivatvamāyāti paśurmukto bhavārṇavāt ।।
sruco randhreṇa taddravyaṃ yāvadvahnau prayujyate ।। bahirnirodhabhāvena sāmarasyaṃ śivena ca ।। sthitaḥ sa sāgaredbhistu sindhuḥ samarasībhavet ।। srucastu pūraṇaṃ yāvat tāvatkālaṃ samādiśet ।।
ātmā samarasatvena śivībhavati sarvagaḥ ।। yathā nṛpatve saṃprāpte kalaśaiścābhiṣicyate ।। tathā śivatve saṃprāpte guṇānāpādayedbudhaḥ ।। anādibodho bhava ca tataḥ svātantryaśaktikaḥ ।।
guṇānāpādya sarvāṃstān mūlamantramanusmaret ।। svāhākāraprayogeṇa āhutīḥ pratipādayet ।। dadyāt tato abhiṣekaṃ tu mūlamantreṇa suvrate ।। turyadvāraṃ viśettaddhi sabāhyābhyantaraṃ smaret ।।
śarīraṃ śoṣyate tābhis tadarthamabhiṣecanam ।। darbhaṃ vimocayitvā ca śivāgnau kalaśe gurau ।। kṛtakṛtyaḥ prahṛṣṭātmā bhavottīrṇaḥ sunirmalaḥ ।। iyaṃ nairvāṇakī dīkṣā nirbījā vā sabījikā ।।
śrutaśīlasamācārān deśakatve niyojayet ।। pañcabhiḥ kalaśairbhadre sitacandanalepitaiḥ ।। ṛddhivṛddhyādibhiḥ pūtair oṣadhyakṣatapūritaiḥ ।। pṛthivyādīni tattvāni pañca pañcasu vinyaset ।।
nivṛttyādyāḥ kalāḥ pañca teṣu caivātra vinyaset ।। pūjayedbhairavaṃ devaṃ sarvasaṃbhārakaiḥ kramāt ।। bhairaveṇābhimantreta ekaikaṃ kalaśaṃ priye ।। vāruṇyāṃ saumyayamyāyam endryāmaiśyāṃ tathaiva ca ।।
yāgaharmyasya aiśānyāṃ pīṭhaṃ saṃkalpyayebudhaḥ ।। vitānoparisaṃchannaṃ dhvajaiśca pariśobhitam ।। tatrānantāsanaṃ nyasya mūrtibhūtaṃ śiśuṃ nyaset ।। gandhapuṣpādinābhyarcya nirbhartsyaḥ kāñcikaudanaiḥ ।।
siddhārthadadhitoyaiśca nirājanasamanvitaiḥ ।। pṛthivyādighaṭāsayirvā dhāmānusmṛtya secayet ।। abhiṣikto anyavāsastu paridhāpyācanettataḥ ।। saṃsthāpya sakalīkṛtya adhikāraṃ prakalpayet ।।
hastyaśvaśivikādyāṃśca rājāṅgāni hyaśeṣataḥ ।। akṣasūtrādikaṃ dattvā caturāśramasaṃsthitāḥ ।। adyaprabhṛti kartavyety adhikāraḥ śivājñayā ।। jānubhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ gatvā saṃpūjya bhairavaṃ tataḥ ।।
ācāryapadasaṃsthena tavānujñāvidhāyinā ।। śivatattvārthakathanaṃ śivasya purataḥ shitaḥ ।। mantratarpaṇakaṃ kṛtvā kalānāṃ pañca cāhutīḥ ।। arghapūjādikaṃ kṛtvā praṇamya khyāpayetprabhoḥ ।।
hṛdādyaiḥ pañcabhiścāṅgair dakṣiṇaṃ lāñchayetkaram ।। puṣpaṃ pāṇau pradadyāttu maṇḍalāgnau prapātayet ।। labdhādhikāro hṛṣṭātmā dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalānvitaḥ ।। śāntyante bhūtidīkṣā ca sadāśivapadātmikā ।।
śivadharmiṇyasau yeṣāṃ sādhakānāṃ prakīrtitā ।। sādhakasyābhiṣeko ayaṃ vidyādīkṣāta uttaraḥ ।। karmabhedo na vidyeta sarvatrādhvani saṃsthitaḥ ।। tāni saṃśodhya vidhivat kalāpañcasthitāni tu ।।
prārabdaṃ karma pāścātyaṃ na caikasthaṃ tu bhāvayet ।। dhāma proccārya sakalaṃ sadāśivatanau nyaset ।। pūrṇāhutiprayogena aṇimādiguṇairyutam ।। aṣṭāvevāhutīrdattvā abhiṣiñcettu sādhakam ।।
śāntyatītāṃ pañcame ca śāntiṃ paścāccaturthake ।। ekaikakalaśe paścāt sādhyamantraṃ tu vinyaset ।। saṃmantryāṣṭaśatenaiva ekaikaṃ kalaśaṃ tataḥ ।। sādhakaṃ tatra saṃsthāpya sakalīkaraṇaṃ tataḥ ।।
nivṛtyāditribhiḥ kumbhaiḥ snāpayetpūrvadiṅmukham ।। śāntiṃ paścāttu gṛhṇīyāt saṃpuṭenābhiṣecayet ।। abhiṣicya praveśyainaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ mūrtimāsthitam ।। sādhakasyādhikārārtham akṣamālādi kalpayet ।।
uṣṇīṣarahitaṃ datvā praviśya śivasaṃnidhau ।। bhūyātsiddhistvadājñātas triprakārasya bhaktitaḥ ।। tasya haste samarpyeta siddhyarthaṃ sādhakasya tu ।। prahṛṣṭavadanaḥ śiṣyo guruścāpi praharṣavān ।।
sahasraṃ vā śataṃ vāpi sādhyamantrasya tarpaṇam ।। tristhaṃ saṃpūjya devaṃ tu tato api triḥpradakṣiṇam ।। utthāpya sādhakaṃ brūyāt samayānpāhi yatnataḥ ।। evaṃ dīkṣāṃ tu nirvartya sarvadaiva varānane ।।
vaijñānakī prākṛtī vā ācāryasya yadṛcchayā ।। tilājyādisamāyuktā adhvavāgīśikalpanā ।। pūjāhomopacārādyān kṛtvātmānaṃ niyojayet ।। puṣpādyaiḥ pūjayitvā taṃ yogārthamāhutitrayam ।।
yugapaddhomayeddevi mūlamantreṇa suvrataḥ ।। hotavyā niṣkṛtirbhinnā pañcasthānakalātmasu ।। viśleṣapāśacchedādye dhāmnaiva yugapaddhutiḥ ।। ātmānaṃ yojayettattve śive paramakāraṇe ।।
ātmadīkṣā samāptau tu prāyaścittanivṛttaye ।। heyopādeyapāśānāṃ yugapadbhairaveṇa tu ।। viśeṣapūjanaṃ homaṃ yathāśakti prakalpayet ।। triḥ pradakṣiṇamāvartya kalaśāgnisamaṇḍalam ।।
bhagavanpaśuhetvarthaṃ yenmayāvāhito bhavān ।। vidhinyūnamakāmasya pūjā śāstoditā yathā ।। avalambya bhaktimātraṃ vidhānaṃ yatkṛtaṃ mayā ।। prasannavadano hṛṣṭo varaṃ dattaṃ vibhāvayet ।।
agraṃ saṃprārthya gṛhṇīyāt sthāpayeccāstrarakṣitam ।। nirodhārdhaṃ tato gṛhya ardhaṃ savyāpasavyataḥ ।। ātmano recakaṃ kṛtvā puṣpaṃ devāya nikṣipet ।। vidyudvaccalitān dhyātvā dhāmadehe tu vinyaset ।।
binduṃ tu nādaśaktisthaṃ śaktirūpaṃ tu grāhayet ।। saṃhāriṇyā tu saṃgṛhya dvādaśāte tu yojayet ।। sakalaṃ niṣkalaṃ rūpaṃ tathā sakalaniṣkalam ।। visarjanavidhirhyevaṃ agnāvevaṃ prapūjayet ।।
ardhāmācamanaṃ datvā praṇipatya kṣamāpayet ।। saṃgṛhya mantrasaṃghātaṃ yathāsthānaṃ prakalpayet ।। nirmālyanayanaṃ kuryād rajāṃsyapaharetpriye ।। bahirnirgatya bhūtānāṃ balikarma tu pūrvavat ।।
guruṃ saṃpūjayecchiṣyo yathāvibhavavistaraiḥ ।। śatabhukpañca vai dadyād grāmaṃ viṃśatibhuktathā ।। yena yena gurustuṣyet tatsarvaṃ vinivedayet ।। tatastu samayāñśrāvyas tantre bhairavanirgate ।।
vāṅniruddhaḥ prasannātmā pṛthak pātravyavasthitaḥ ।। anenaiva vidhānena dīkṣitā ye varānante ।। sarve te samadharmāṇaḥ śivadharme niyojitāḥ ।। ekapaṅktibhujaḥ sarve samayinastu varānane ।।
cumbakānāṃ bhavedekā na prāgjātivibhedataḥ ।। tantrametatsamāśritya prāgjātiṃ na hyudīrayet ।। prāgjātyudīraṇāddevi prāyaścittī bhavennaraḥ ।। pitāmahasya pakṣaikaṃ narake pacyate tu saḥ ।।
avivekena deveśi siddhirmuktirdhruvaṃ bhavet ।। tattvadīkṣā samāsena kathayasva prasādataḥ ।। ṣaṭtriṃśattattvamukhyāni yathā śodhyāni pārvati ।। yathā śuddhyānti deveśi tathā te kathayāmyaham ।।
vācakāste ca tattvānāṃ kathayāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।। puruṣasya yakāro vai rāgatattvānvitasya ca ।। kālaṃ kalāṃ lakāreṇa kalpayettu varānane ।। repheṇa caiśvaraṃ tattvaṃ hakāreṇa sadāśivaḥ ।।
vyāpinīṃ samanāṃ cordhvaṃ tatraiva tu viśodhayet ।। yojya ātmā pare tattve unmanātītasarvage ।। ṣaṭtriṃśattattvamākhyātaṃ navatattvaṃ pracakṣmahe ।। māyā vidyā tatheśaśca sadāśivaśivau tathā ।।
pañcatattvī yadā śodhyā vaktramantrāstu vācakāḥ ।। kalānāṃ yāvatī vyāptis tattvānāṃ tāvadeva hi ।। akāra ātmatattvasya vācakaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। sakalāvadhi tajjñeyaṃ śivasya tu makārakaḥ ।।
śodhayitvā krameṇaiva pare tattve niyojayet ।। paradīkṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। pṛthagbhedena teṣāṃ tu vinyāsaṃ kathayāmi te ।। navahastaṃ likhedveśma aṣṭaparvādhikaṃ budhaḥ ।।
caturaśraṃ vibhajyādau matsyaiścaivātra cihnitam ।। madhyame koṣṭhake sūtraṃ dvātriṃśāṅgulasammitam ।। prathame karṇikāṃ kuryāt kesarāṇi dvitīyake ।। dikṣu rekhāṣṭakaṃ dattvā pratidikṣu tathaiva ca ।।
dvābhyāṃ pratidigrekhābhyāṃ madhye sūtraṃ nidhāpya tat ।। madhyasūtraṃ ca dātavyaṃ kiñjalkasthaṃ vipaścitā ।। kesarāṇi ca saṃlikhya caturviṃśatisaṃkhyayā ।। tasyāntaṃ caturaśraṃ tu kartavyaṃ tatpramāṇataḥ ।।
pūrvapaścāttataṃ sūtraṃ śaṅkunā sādhayet priye ।। pārśveṣu bhrāmayedrekhāṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulasammitām ।। aparasthena sūryeṇa prākchāyāṃ lāñchayet priye ।। tataḥ samālikhet padmam aṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam ।।
śeṣā lopyā varārohe ekāntaritayogataḥ ।। vīthyardhasammitāṃ devi śobhāṃ caiva prakalpayet ।। tathā kaṇṭhaṃ ca tanmānaṃ dvārametatprakīrtitam ।। snātvā tu vidhivad devi praviśedbhavanaṃ guruḥ ।।
tataḥ sampūjayeddevaṃ bhairavaṃ parameśvaram ।। madhye sampūjayeddevaṃ svacchandaṃ parameśvaram ।। patrāṣṭake nyasedvarṇān pūrvādīśāṃśtataḥ kramāt ।। prakṛtyantaṃ vijānīyān madhye pīṭheśakalpanā ।।
tatsthāne bhairavaḥ pūjyaḥ śeṣā varṇairyathākramam ।। īśānadiśa ārabhya madhyapīṭhaṃ viśodhayet ।। evaṃ varṇāstathā mantrān bhuvanāni viśodhayet ।। samayān śrāvayetpaścāt tantrāmnāyotthitān priye ।।
sāṃkhyaṃ yogaṃ pāñcarātraṃ vedāṃścaiva na nindayet ।। smārtaṃ dharmaṃ na nindettu ācārapathadarśakam ।। vīrāścaiva bhaginyaśca gāvo bhūtagaṇāstathā ।। gurorannaṃ na bhuñjīta adattaṃ parameśvari ।।
sācārāśca nirācārāṃl liṅgino na jugupsayet ।। upaskarān mahādevi pādena tu na saṃspṛśet ।। āhnikaṃ na vilumpettu sandhyākarma varānane ।। trikālaṃ pūjayeddevaṃ japadhyānarataḥ sadā ।।
ato vijñānadīkṣāṃ tu pravakṣyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।। śiṣyātmānaṃ gṛhītvā tam ātmaprāṇe niyojayet ।। udghātaiśca tato adhvānaṃ śiṣyasya tu viśodhayet ।। bhinnābhinnasvarūpeṇa ekaikaṃ tu yathākramam ।।
bindunā śaktisaṃyogād udghātaḥ prathamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। udghātaḥ sa tu deveśi dvitīyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। ardhacandrānnirodhinyām udghātastu tṛtīyakaḥ ।। udghātaḥ sa tu deveśi caturthaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
udghātaḥ sa tu deveśi pañcamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। akārokāramakārāntam evaṃ śuddhyati nānyathā ।। jalībhūtaṃ tadevaitad ātmanā saha yogataḥ ।। bindvantaṃ dhāraṇāyuktaṃ śiṣyādātmani cintayet ।।
tejodghātāstrayasteṣu nirodhyantamavasthitāḥ ।। ākāśe līyamānaṃ tam udghātena tu cintayet ।। vyāpinī sā tu vijñeyā pañcamānte vyavasthitā ।। ātmavyāpī tataścordhvaṃ sarvavyāpī tataḥ punaḥ ।।
yojayetparame tattve unmanātītasarvage ।। mantramuccārayeddevi hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutaṃ param ।। tridevaṃ bindusaṃyuktam ardhacandraṃ nirodhikām ।। unmanā ca paraścaiva sarvavyāpī śivo avyayaḥ ।।
tadā tu yojayenmantrī anyathā naiva yojayet ।। brahmā viṣṇustathā rudraḥ trimāṇaṃ varṇa ucyate ।। tatra śabdaḥ kriyāntasthaḥ kriyāśaktiriti smṛtā ।। tasya kiṃcidgataḥ śabdo nāsikānte pravartate ।।
mūrdhasthānagataḥ śabdo lalāṭāntamavasthitaḥ ।। tatrasthā vinivartante śivajñānavivarjitāḥ ।। tasyātīto bhavennādaḥ avicchinnastvasau bhavet ।। caturvidho bhavecchabdo yaḥ suvegavahaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
tasyātītā bhavecchaktiḥ pañcadhā tu vyavasthitā ।। vyāpinī parataścaiva pañcadhā tu vyavasthitā ।। vyāpinī sā samuddiṣṭā na jñānaṃ parameśvari ।। unmanāpadamārohan śuddhātmā tu tato bhavet ।।
tatra yuktaḥ pare śānte mahāśāntimavāpnuyāt ।। yojane tu pare tattve upāyaḥ kathitastava ।। tattvādhvānaṃ kalādhvānaṃ bhuvanādhvānameva ca ।। eṣā vai dhāraṇādīkṣā kartavyā yoginātra tu ।।
mantrasiddhena vā devi kṛtā vai sukṛtā bhavet ।। jāyate vividhā siddhiḥ girigahvaramāśrite ।। pracchanne vijane ramye bhairavaṃ tatra pūjayet ।। pañcapraṇavasaṃyogāj japataḥ siddhyate dhruvam ।।
hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutaṃ sūkṣmam atisūkṣmaṃ paraṃ śivam ।। praṇavaḥ pañcadhāvasthaḥ haṃsena saha saṃyuktaḥ ।। śivajñānaṃ ca tatrasthaṃ haṃsaḥ praṇavasaṃyutaḥ ।। yathāprakṛti saṃyukto na ca tiṣṭhati caikataḥ ।।
coditastu yadā tena tadā cordhvaṃ pravartate ।। kathitaṃ nābhijānanti vinā śāstreṇa codanām ।। aprakāśaḥ svadehastho guṇabhūtaḥ pravartate ।। vijñātavyaṃ na kiñcitsyāt kevalo niṣkalastu saḥ ।।
sa kathaṃ gṛhyate sūkṣma agrāhyo nityamavyayaḥ ।। pañcapañcakasaṃyukto dehe sakalaniṣkalaḥ ।। yogenāvāhitasyāpi bhāvamātraṃ tu bhāvayet ।। bindūpari ca yacchāntaḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।।
ṣaṣṭhasvarasamāyogād abhyāsādacirāllabhet ।। saguṇaḥ sakalo jñeyo nirguṇo niṣkalaḥ śivaḥ ।। sakale japyamāne tu japto bhavati niṣkalaḥ ।। rūpaṃ tu sakalaṃ tasya dvidhāvasthaṃ prakāśitam ।।
prakṛtirvikṛtiścaiva ubhe ṣaṣṭhena saṃyute ।। pravartate ca etena punastena nivartate ।। bindunādasamāyuktaḥ praṇavaḥ paripaṭhyate ।। varṇatrayamidaṃ proktaṃ brahmādyā devatāstrayaḥ ।।
ete vai praṇavāḥ pañca haṃsaḥ prāṇayutaḥ sadā ।। parataḥ praṇavān pañca punareva vadāmyaham ।। unmanā ca tathā devi praṇavāḥ pañca kīrtitaḥ ।। ete vai praṇavāḥ pañca parāparavibhāgaśaḥ ।।
pravartante hi sarvatra bhuktimuktiphalapradāḥ ।। tatrasthaḥ ekarūpastu niṣkalastattvataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pravartate ayato yasmād devāsuraniketanam ।। tasya boddhādvimucyante ahikañcukavat priye ।।
vidite tu pure tattve na bhūyo jāyate kvacit ।। praṇavena samāyuktaṃ kṛtārtha iti nirdiśet ।। uccārastrividho devi haṃsasya samudāhṛtaḥ ।। sṛṣṭinyāsena tūccāraḥ saṃhārayoga ucyate ।।
bindusthaṃ tritayaṃ kṛtvā vaktramudghāṭayettataḥ ।। nādasthaṃ pañcadhā caiva śaktisthaṃ pañcadhā punaḥ ।। unmanā ca paraṃ tattvaṃ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitam ।। anyathā naiva mucyante bindvante ye vyavasthitāḥ ।।
śaktisthaṃ sparśagaṃ caiva tadūrdhvaṃ śūnyarūpakam ।। parāparavibhāgena te sarvatra vyavasthitāḥ ।। sarvātītaṃ paraṃ tattvaṃ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitam ।। tatrasthā sarvakarmāṇi sādhayanti na saṃśayaḥ ।।
sparśaścaiva tathā śabdo rūpaṃ ca tadanantaram ।। tatrasthā jñānayogaṃ ca prayacchanti varānane ।। japet tu sakalān devi niṣkalena samanvitān ।। śaktisthāḥ śaktidāḥ proktāḥ śūnyasthā vyāpakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
kaivalyadāstataścordhve sarvajñāśconmane pade ।। tajjñātvā siddhidāḥ sarve muktidāśca na saṃśayaḥ ।। pañcapraṇavapūrveṇa oṃkārādyayutena tu ।। japataḥ siddhimāpnoti lakṣenākṣarasaṃkhyayā ।।
japānte tu punarhomaṃ daśamāṃśena kārayet ।। tataḥ siddhimavāpnoti adhamāṃ madhyamottamam ।। brahmaviṣṇvindradevānāṃ siddhadaityorageśinām ।। darpaṃ harati kālasya pātayed bhūdharānapi ।।
brahmarākṣasavetālān krūragrahavināyakān ।। prākṛtānyapi karmāṇi siddhyanti japalakṣataḥ ।। mohanā sahadevā ca bhūdhātrī cakralāñchanā ।। bhakṣe pāne ca dātavyaṃ vaśīkaraṇamuttamam ।।
ātmendriyeṇa saṃyuktaṃ vaśīkaraṇamuttamam ।। bhūkadambasamopetaṃ dātavyaṃ payasā niśi ।। ṣaṣṭiṃ kanakabījāni ṣoḍaśa maṇicandrikāḥ ।। eṣa kāpāliko yogo gacchantamanugacchati ।।
gṛhodbhavasya kuṣṭhaṃ ca svaraktendriyasaṃyutam ।। mohanā caiva kāntārī mayūraśikhayā yutā ।। lajjālukā ca gorambhā caṇḍālīkarmakaṃ tathā ।। eṣa yogavaro divyo dīyate yasya suvrate ।।
caṇakā māṣamudgāśca apānena vinirgatāḥ ।। mūtraṃ raktaṃ tathā keśo lālā caiva varānane ।। mohanā viṣṇukrāntā ca dhātrī caivaikataḥ sthitā ।। bhakṣye pāne pradātavyo yogastridaśapūjitaḥ ।।
kākolūkasya pakṣāṃśca kharoṣṭramūtramṛttikā ।। kākolūkasya pakṣāṃśca gude tasya vinikṣipet ।। prajvālya homayettatra kākapakṣāṃśca suvrate ।। yasya nāma samuddiśya yakārādyantarodhitam ।।
bhramate kākavat pṛthvīṃ śatrurvyādhinipīḍitaḥ ।। śatroḥ pratikṛtiṃ kṛtvā akṣapuṣpaistu veṣṭitām ।। puṣpairvibhītatarujair yasya nāmnā tu homayet ।। priyaṅgulatikāmiśraṃ gugguluṃ ghṛtavedhitam ।।
jātikuṭmalakairmiśrais trimadhvaktaistilairhutaiḥ ।। tilairlavaṇasammiśrais trimadhvaktairhutaiḥ priyaiḥ ।। rājikā lavaṇaṃ caiva madhukṣīraghṛtaplutam ।। narasya rocanāṃ gṛhya dviradasya madena tu ।।
snāne vilepane madye gandhe vā yasya dīyate ।। athavā mārayetkṣipraṃ śatruṃ niścitamātmanaḥ ।। kapāladvayamādāya nāma śatroḥ samālikhet ।। rudhireṇa samāyuktaṃ humphaṭkāravidarbhitam ।।
kṛṣṇamālyopahāraiśca tataḥ karma samārabhet ।। anujñātastu devena gṛhittvā tacchirodvayam ।। tatrastho roṣasampūrṇo dakṣiṇābhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ ।। kruddhaḥ samuccarenmantrī dvātriṃśākṣarasammitam ।।
humphaḍdvayaṃ samuccārya kādye cāsphālayedbhṛśam ।। saptarātreṇa deveśi prayogastvanivartakaḥ ।। prayogāṇāṃ karotyeṣa mantrarājeśvareśvaraḥ ।। kṣīraṃ tu homayeddevi śāntyarthe hitakārakam ।।
mantrāṇāṃ tarpaṇārthaṃ ca natyantaṃ cārcane smṛtam ।। kriyākālāṃśayuktasya akleśāttu sukhāvaham ।। kālāṃśakaṃ ca deveśa kathayasva prasārataḥ ।। suvārakaraṇe lagne suyoge sudine priye ।।
grahaṇaṃ candrasūryābhyāṃ kālaśca ṛtavastathā ।। puṇyāpuṇyodayo devi saura eṣa prakīrtitaḥ ।। ṣāṭkośikastu yo deho bhūtatanmātrasaṃyutaḥ ।। sarvatattvaistathā devaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitavigrahaḥ ।।
nābhyadhomeḍhrakande ca sthitā vai nābhimadhyataḥ ।। cakravat saṃsthitāstatra pradhānā daśa nāḍayaḥ ।। punarvinirgatāścānyā ābhyo apyanyāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। yathā parṇa palāśasya vyāptaṃ sarvatra tantubhiḥ ।।
mārutāpūritāḥ sarvā ātmaśakticarāḥ sadā ।। cāravṛttiprabhedena saṃjñābhedo varānane ।। pradhānā daśa yāḥ proktā nāḍayaśca varānane ।। nāḍīnāṃ caiva vāyūnāṃ saṃjñāvṛttīrnibodha me ।।
gāndhārī hastijihvā ca pūṣā caiva yaśasvinī ।। etāḥ prāṇavahāḥ proktāḥ pradhānā daśa nāḍayaḥ ।। nāgaḥ kūrmo atha kṛkaro devadatto dhanañjayaḥ ।। tāsu saṃcarataḥ siddhiṃ yogaṃ caiva varānane ।।
daśānāṃ tu paraṃ devi nāḍītrayamudāhṛtam ।। hṛccakre tu samākhyātāḥ sādhakānāṃ hitāvahāḥ ।। tathā te kathayiṣyāmi pravibhajya yathāsphuṭam ।। traya ete avibhāgena saṃcarante samantataḥ ।।
vṛttisaṃjñāprabhedena varṇarūpāṇyanekadhā ।। koṭidhāto varārohe sa ekaḥ saṃvyavasthitaḥ ।। nityamāpūrayanneva prāṇināmurasi sthitaḥ ।। ahorātragatiṃ prāṇe adhunā kathayāmi te ।।
bāhye naiva tu kālena te lavāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। taireva praharairdevi caturbhistu dinaṃ bhavet ।। śivo dharmeṇa haṃsastu sūryā haṃsaḥ prabhānvitaḥ ।। tasyodayātkaletkālaḥ grahāṇāmudayo bhavet ।।
prāṇe vai udayantyete ahorātreṇa suvrate ।। hṛdayordhve tu kaṇṭhādho yāvadvai pravahet priye ।। dvitīya ūrdhve vijñeyo madhyāhnastālumadhyataḥ ।। nāsāgryatryaṅgulordhve tu yāvatprāptastu suvrate ।।
śaktyante ca caturthastu praharo ahaḥ prakīrtitam ।। tato astamayasandhyātra tuṭyardhaṃ tu bhavet priye ।। sa ca candrodayo devi rajanī ca vidhīyate ।। tāluke cārdharātrastu punarevaṃ vidhīyate ।।
tuṭyardhaṃ tu varārohe pūrvasaṃdhyā bhavettataḥ ।। pūrvavat kramayogena sa careddhi sadā śubhe ।। candrasūryodayo hyeṣa mayā te parikīrtitaḥ ।। prāṇe cāpyudayantyete prahare prahare priye ।।
rāhuścarati somena ketuścarati bhāsvatā ।। mūrtayaścaiva te cāṣṭāv aṣṭau te ca gaṇeśvarāḥ ।। anantādiśikhaṇḍyantās te ca vidyeśvarāṣṭakāḥ ।। pūrvoktā bhairavāścāṣṭau sarve te ca vyavasthitāḥ ।।
rāśibhiḥ saha nakṣatrais ta udyanti aharniśam ।। abhīpsitaṃ phalaṃ tatra sādhakānāṃ bhavediha ।। adhunā pakṣamāsāṃśca varṣāṇi kathayāmi te ।। māsenādhyātmikenaiva bāhye caiva kalā bhavet ।।
māsaidvadaśabhiścaiva bāhye atha ghaṭikā bhavet ।। varṣametat samākhyātaṃ bāhye vai ghaṭikā ca sā ।। tā evāntaracāreṇa ṣaṣṭiḥ saṃvatsarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ṣaṭ śatāni varārohe sahasrāṇyekaviṃśatiḥ ।।
prāṇasaṃkhyā samākhyātā jñātavyā sādhakena tu ।। tasyāyaṃ japa uddiṣṭaḥ siddhimuktiphalapradaḥ ।। muktiścaiva bhavedūrdhve paratattve tu suvrate ।। yathā pravartate prāṇas tv ayatnādeva sarvadā ।।
svayamuccarate haṃsaḥ prāṇināmurasi sthitaḥ ।। candrasūryoparāgaṃ tu kathayāmi tataḥ param ।। sa eva pakṣadvitayaṃ māsaṃ ca kathayāmi te ।। madhye pañcadaśoktā yās tithayastāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।
dvitīye caiva tuṭyardhe yadā carati śarvarī ।। asminnevamahorātre pūrvavacca varānane ।। tithicchede ṛṇaṃ jñeyaṃ vṛddhau caiva dhanaṃ bhavet ।। kṛṣṇapakṣordhvacāreṇa saṃhāraḥ saṃkṣayo bhavet ।।
śubhakarmāṇi kṛṣṇe ca na ca siddhyanti suvrate ।। amāvasyā tu sā jñeyā kṛṣṇapakṣe varānane ।। pakṣasaṃdhistvasau jñeyo amāvasyārdhapratipadā ।। ravibimbāntare devi candrabimbaṃ tadā bhavet ।।
amṛtaṃ sravate candro rāhuśca grasate tu tam ।। ādityagrahaṇaṃ caiva loke tadupadiśyate ।। dṛśyante samavāyena tanmahāgrahaṇaṃ bhavet ।। tatra snānaṃ tathā dānaṃ pūjāhomajapādikam ।।
tāṃ caivārdhatuṭiṃ tyaktvā śuklapakṣodayo bhavet ।। tadārabhya ca karmāṇi śubhānyabhyudayāni ca ।। prāṇahaṃso yadā prāptas tv adhastāṃ prathamāṃ tuṭim ।। rāśayo graha ṛksāṇi yogāśca karaṇāni ca ।।
pratipatsā tu vijñeyā candraścaikakalo bhavet ।। tithayaścaivamārabhya yāvatpañcadaśī tuṭi ।। tatra pūjā japo dhyānaṃ saṃpūrṇaṃ saphalaṃ bhavet ।। tasyāścārdhatuṭiryā tu pakṣasaṃdhyā tu sā smṛtā ।।
hṛtpadmasaṃdhimadhye tu somasya grahaṇaṃ bhavet ।। tatraiva ca mahatpuṇyaṃ dhyānahomajapādibhiḥ ।। nānādiddhipradaṃ hyetat sādhakasyābhiyoginaḥ ।। pakṣadvayaṃ parityajya pūvoktakaraṇena tu ।।
parityajya tvadhaḥ sarvaṃ dhyānamāsthāya yojayet ।। pakṣadvaye api grahaṇaṃ bhavedvai sarvadehinām ।। atraivādhyātmāhorātre tv athābdodaya ucyate ।। aṅgulaiḥ ṣaḍbhirekaiko hṛtpadmādyāva śaktitaḥ ।।
tasyāpyardhaṃ dinaṃ pūrvam aparārdhaṃ niśā bhavet ।। triṃśatā tairahorātrair dvipakṣo māsa ucyate ।। hṛdayādudayasthānāt saṃkrāntirmakare sthitā ।। kaṇṭhordhve dvyaṅgulaṃ tyaktvā mīne saṃkramate punaḥ ।।
nāsāntaṃ yāvatsaṃkrāntir aṅgulāni ṣaḍeva hi ।। japahomārcanadhyānān mahābhyudayakārikā ।। ṣaḍaṅgulāni saṃtyajya saṃkramenmithune punaḥ ।। makarācca samārabhya mithunāntaṃ ca suvrate ।।
snānaṃ dhyānaṃ tathā dānaṃ pūjāhomajapādikam ।। iha janmani nāpnoti paratraivopatiṣṭhate ।। tatkāle saṃharedvīryaṃ jagatyasmiṃścarācare ।। garbhasthānekadhārūpaṃ yadgṛhītaṃ purātanam ।।
tasmādārabhya makarād dhyānahomajapādikam ।। puraścaryānimittāya mantragrahavrataṃ ca yat ।। bāhye api taravo loke ṛtuṣaṭkasamīritam ।। mantrāḥ kālānurūpeṇa vratacaryādineritāḥ ।।
adhyātmaśabdarūpātmā ṣaḍrasāsvādaneritaḥ ।। śabdasaṃvedanaṃ tasya sphuṭaṃ tatra bhavedyataḥ ।। mithunāntaṃ ca deveśi tataḥ siddhiḥ prajāyate ।। karkaṭādau sa varṣettu tulāntaṃ tālukāntare ।।
tasmādihātmasiddhyarthaṃ puṣṭyarthaṃ caiva sādhayet ।। śaktyadho hṛdaye haṃsaḥ saṃkrametkarkaṭe priye ।। ṣaḍaṅgulaiḥ punastyaktaiḥ kanyāṃ saṃkramate punaḥ ।। tulāsaṃkrāntireṣoktā dakṣiṇaṃ viṣuvadbhavet ।।
mṛtyorjayaṃ tathā śāntiṃ puṣṭiṃ tasmātsamārabhet ।। ṣaḍaṅgulāni tyaktvā tu vṛścike kramate punaḥ ।। vṛścikaṃ tu parityajya dhanvisaṃkrāntirucyate ।। hṛtpadmāntaṃ tu vai haṃsaś caritvā ūrdhvagodayaḥ ।।
amunoktakrameṇaiva āyurvai sarvadehinām ।। ayanadvayamākhyātaṃ mokṣasiddhirdvayojjhitā ।। tatrastho vai japadhyānān mokṣasiddhimavāpnuyāt ।। asminnabdodaye bhūyo dvādaśābdodayaṃ śṛṇu ।।
tadādi sādhakaistasmāt kartavyaṃ mantrasādhanam ।। lakṣaṇaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi prāṇo asminpravibhāgaśaḥ ।। ahorātrastu yaḥ prokto dvādaśāṃśaṃ bhajetpriye ।। pañcabhistāṃstu saṃguṇya dvādaśābda ṛturbhavet ।।
triguṇenaitadayane vatsaraḥ ṣaṅguṇena tu ।। dvādaśābdodaye prāṇe vatsarāste prakīrtitāḥ ।। sahasrāṇi tu catvāri triśatī viṃśatistathā ।। ṣaṣṭyabdodayamatraiva punaśca kathayāmi te ।।
te cādha ūrdhvage prāṇe ekasminsurasundari ।। ānandaprabhṛterdevi mantramārādhayettu yaḥ ।। dvādaśābde tvahorātraṃ pañcadhā bhedayecca tam ।। te vai ṣaṅguṇitāstatra māsa ekaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।
aṅgule tu sapañcāṃśe mānametatprakīrtitam ।। hṛtpadmādyāva śaktyūrdhvaṃ triṃśadabdodayo bhavet ।। ṣaṣṭyabde ye tvahorātrāḥ saṅkhyāṃ teṣu vadāmyaham ।। ahorātrāstu ṣaṣṭyabde saṅkhyātāstu varānane ।।
candrasūryoparāge ca pakṣamāsāyaneṣu ca ।। varṣadvādaśake caiva ṣaṣṭyabde atha varānane ।। jñānayogādibhiścaiva bāhye kāle tu yatkṛtam ।। prāṇahaṃsagatiṃ cāre jñātvaikasmiṃstu tadbhajet ।।
athavā sa japādevam atyarthamupabṛṃhitaḥ ।। punareva pravakṣyāmi nāḍitrayavibhāgataḥ ।। yathā caratyasau haṃso jagatyasmiṃścarācare ।। nāḍitrayakṛtādhāro mārgatrayavyavasthitaḥ ।।
kāraṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhirākrāntaḥ śaktitritayasaṃyutaḥ ।। dakṣanāsāpuṭe caiva nāḍī vai piṅgalā smṛtā ।। dakṣiṇe devamārgastu pitṛmārgastathottare ।। dakṣiṇe sattvajāgratsthaḥ svapnastho vāmato rajaḥ ।।
brahmeśvaraśca dakṣastho vāme viṣṇusadāśivau ।। jyeṣṭhājñāne ca dakṣe ca kriyā vāmā tathottare ।। dakṣiṇo tu sthitaḥ sūryo vāme somo virājate ।। pācayetsarvapākaṃ hi somādiguṇasambhavam ।।
rāśayaśca grahāḥ sarve ṛkṣayogādayaśca ye ।। sūryasomau ca te sarve bhuñjate kramaśaḥ priye ।। vāyati tapati sūryaḥ somo varṣati cāmṛtam ।। sauro dakṣiṇamārgastu uttarāyaṇasaṃjñitaḥ ।।
somasūryātma viṣuvat puṭadvayaviniḥsṛtam ।। dakṣiṇottarayormadhye saṃkrāntyā viṣuvaddvayam ।। āpyāyane tathā puṣṭau śāntike saumya uttaraḥ ।। dakṣiṇottarasaṃkrāntiḥ sā caivaṃ saṃvidhīyate ।।
yāvadardhaṃ tu tatrasthaṃ madhyenottarato vahet ।। uttarāddakṣiṇāyāṃ tu saṃkrāmansa varānane ।। viṣuvaddakṣiṇaṃ tāvad dakṣiṇāyanajaṃ priye ।। dhyānayogena dīkṣāyāṃ tatstho vai mocayedguruḥ ।।
caturviṃśatisaṃkrāntīḥ prāṇahaṃsastu saṃkramet ।। pūrvāhṇe viṣuvattvekaṃ madhyāhne tu dvitīyakam ।। caturdhā viṣuvatproktam ahorātreṇa muktidam ।। śatāni nava vai haṃsa ekāmekāṃ vahetsadā ।।
iṣṭaṃ caivāpyaniṣṭaṃ ca tadā saṃsūcayettu saḥ ।। pūrvodaye tu saṃprāpte bhāskarasya varānane ।। susaṃyatamanā yogī vīro yogāsanasthitaḥ ।। supraśāntastadā tiṣṭhet prāṇaikagatamānasaḥ ।।
pravāhe viṣuvaddevi jñātvā kālaṃ samādiśet ।। abdadvayaṃ sa jīvettu ahorātradvayena tu ।। pañcābdaṃ pañcadivasaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍvarṣameva ca ।। navabhirnavavarṣāṇi daśabhirdaśa eva ca ।।
dinairdvādaśabhiryogī jīvedvarṣāṇi dvādaśa ।। praharānṣaḍvahedyasya māsāṃstrīnvai sa jīvati ।। caturbhiḥ praharaidevi māsamekaṃ sa jīvati ।। praharadvayaṃ vahedyasya dinānyaṣṭau sa jīvati ।।
praharārdhaṃ vahedyasya sa jīvetpraharadvayam ।। yadārabhya nirūpyeta prāṇe vai kālamīśvaram ।। saṃlakṣyaivaṃ prayatnena tatkāle niścayo bhavet ।। ayuktasyāpi ca prāṇe mṛtyujñānaṃ nibodha me ।।
maraṇaṃ tasya deveśi ṣaṇmāsena vinirdiśet ।। māsamekaṃ sa jīvettu na śṛṇoti yadā priye ।। saṃkrāntipañcakaṃ prāṇo mukharandhre vahedyadā ।। vittanāśastathodvego rogavṛddhiśca jāyate ।।
dakṣiṇe puṭa ekasmin dakṣiṇāyanavarjite ।। bhagandharo anugranthaśca netrarogaśca kāmalā ।। vāmanāsāpuṭenaiva saṃkrāntīśca trayodaśa ।। mūtrakṛcchraṃ pramehaśca pāṇḍurogaśca jāyate ।।
yasmiṃścāre nirūpyeta tatkāladivase pare ।। athānyatsparśavijñānaṃ nāsādhastāttathopari ।। vācākrośābhibhavanaṃ dakṣiṇena vahedyadā ।। itaścetaśca bahudhā saṃkrāntyekā vahedyadā ।।
mandacāre suṣumnāyāṃ prāṇahaṃso vahedyadā ।। dvādaśaiva tu saṃkrāntīr vahedviṣuvataikataḥ ।। hrasetsaṃkrāntirekaikā māsa eko hrasettadā ।। dine dine vahedbāhye yāvattriṃśaddināni tu ।।
mṛtyuyogaḥ samākhyāto mayā te varavarṇini ।। yatkālāttu samārabhya tatkālaṃ tu samādiśet ।। dakṣiṇāyanaje kāle evaṃ te kathitaṃ śubham ।। jñātvā yogī jayenmṛtyum aśubhānyapyaśeṣataḥ ।।
nāsikārandhramārgasthaḥ sa sṛjetsaṃharejjagat ।। tatsthaṃ dhyātvā jayenmṛtyuṃ nākalasthaṃ kaletprabhuḥ ।। kālatrayaṃ vijānāti kālayuktastu yogavit ।। sa bhavetkālarūpī vai svacchandaḥ kālavaccaret ।।
vijñānaṃ śravaṇaṃ dūrān mananaṃ cāvalokanam ।। dakṣanāsāpuṭe dhyātvā brāhmaiśvaryamavāpnuyāt ।। bhaviṣyajjño bhavedvāme viṣṇutulyabalaśca saḥ ।। bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca sarvaṃ jānāti madhyataḥ ।।
āyuṣā balavīryeṇa rūpaiśvaryeṇa tatsamaḥ ।। viṣṇoḥ sadāśivaiśvaryaṃ parabhāvādavāpnuyāt ।। evaṃ mṛtyujayaḥ khyātaḥ amṛtaṃ dhyāyato jayaḥ ।। dhyātvā sitaṃ suvikacaṃ kalāṣoḍaśakānvitam ।।
tanmadhye cintyamātmānaṃ śuddhasphaṭikanirmalam ।। upariṣṭāddvitīyābjaṃ śaktāmṛtamahodadhau ।। tanmadhye cintayeddhaṃsam adho binduśikhānvitam ।। ātmordhvarandhramārgeṇa praviṣṭaṃ tacca cintayet ।।
tenāplāvitamātmānaṃ pūryamāṇaṃ vicintayet ।। amṛtāpūritaṃ dehaṃ sarvameva vicintayet ।। vyādhīnmṛtyuṃ jarāṃ tyaktvā krīḍate tvaṇimādibhiḥ ।। athavā paratattvasthaḥ sarvakālairna bādhyate ।।
kalākalaṅkanirmuktaṃ niṣkalaṃ paramaṃ padam ।। saṃyuktaḥ kāraṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ sarvatattvasamanvitaḥ ।। samanāvadhiparyantaḥ kalaṅkādhāra ucyate ।। tasyāścānte paraṃ tattvaṃ sakalākalavarjitam ।।
pañcapañcakatattvastham aṣṭādaśaguṇānvitam ।। kāraṇāni ca mantrāśca nivṛttyādyāḥ kalāstathā ।। śaktiśca vyāpinī caiva samanātmā tathonmanā ।। tattvānyeva tu ṣaṭtriṃśat guṇāṃścaiva nibodha me ।।
grahaṇaṃ sparśa ādhāraḥ śaktiścaivāṣṭamī smṛtā ।। prāṇahaṃsastathā śaktiḥ guṇā aṣṭādaśa tvime ।। akṣarākṣaranirmuktaṃ paraṃ tattvamanakṣaram ।। yāvaduccāryate vācā yāvallekhye api tiṣṭhati ।।
sṛṣṭisaṃhāranirmuktaḥ kriyākālavivarjitaḥ ।। adhaścāreṇa jāto asau urdhve caiva mṛto bhavet ।। tattvavṛttiśca vyākhyātā sarvādhvopādhivarjitā ।। tattvavṛttau sthito yogī sarvārambhavivarjitaḥ ।।
nākāṅkṣenna ca nindettu viṣayāṃśca kadācana ।। tulyadarśī bhavennityaṃ sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ smaret ।। sarvatattvāni bhūtāni varṇā mantrāśca ye smṛtāḥ ।। nacāsau kurute puṇyaṃ naiva pāpaṃ ca suvrate ।।
iha loke parasmiṃśca paripūrṇastu sarvadā ।। na cāsya bhakṣyābhakṣyaṃ hi na peyāpeyameva ca ।। nirapekṣo hyasau nityaṃ sarvāpekṣāvivarjitaḥ ।। kṣetraṃ tasya parā śaktir yataḥ sarvaṃ prasūyate ।।
tīrthaṃ caiva paraṃ śāntaṃ nityaṃ cānandaviśvagam ।। nityaṃ viraktiḥ saṃsārād yamo ayam parikīrtitaḥ ।। nātmano bhāvayejjātiṃ na kulaṃ na ca bāndhavān ।। parabhāvanayā nityaṃ paradharmeṇa vartayet ।।
svatantro aluptasāmarthyas tv anādinidhanāśritaḥ ।। cāroccāravinirmuktas tv ahorātravivarjitaḥ ।। svabhāvenaiva saṃtiṣṭhad dinarātrivivarjitaḥ ।। na ca taṃ kalayetkālaḥ kalpakoṭiśatairapi ।।
śivo hi bhāvito nityaṃ na kālaḥ kalayecchivam ।। sa svacchandapade yuktaḥ svacchandasamatāṃ vrajet ।। evaṃ vai mṛtyuliṅgāni riṣṭānyanyāni yāni ca ।। nirjityaitāni yogena evamuktavrameṇa tu ।।
bahirliṅgāni tānyatra aṅgāriṣṭāni me śṛṇu ।। skandhau ca bhaṅgamāyātaḥ ṣaṇmāsānmṛtyumāpnuyāt ।। sitaṃ haritakṛṣṇaṃ ca vatsarārdhānmriyeta saḥ ।। tārāṃ jyotsnāṃ ca kṛṣṇāṃ vai paśyetṣaṇmāsajīvitaḥ ।।
svapne saṃpaśyate yo vai ṣaṇmāsānso api jīvati ।। tailābhyaṅgaṃ tathā pānaṃ raktasraganulepanam ।। pretaiḥ piśācai rakṣobhiḥ śvagomāyukasūkaraiḥ ।। aṅgabhakṣaṇamudvāhaṃ nagnaṃ cātīva vihvalam ।।
śaṃkhāvarte bhujāmadhye gulphayormarmasandhiṣu ।। somārkamaṇḍalaṃ dehe dhruvaṃ caiva tvarundhatīm ।। tālurandhragato dhūmo mahāyānaṃ taducyate ।। netrānte karajākrānte maṇḍalaṃ somasūryayoḥ ।।
sthūlo akasmācca jāyeta akasmādvai bhavetkṛśaḥ ।। kṛṣṇāmbaradharaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ lohadaṇḍakarodyatam ।। hṛdayaṃ śuṣyate yasya snātamātrasya tatkṣaṇāt ।। dhanurniśi divā colkā vyabhre vidyutpradarśanam ।।
cakṣuṣī sravato yasya śabdaṃ na śṛṇuyāt sphuṭam ।। raktapadmopamaṃ vaktraṃ jihvā kṛṣṇā ca yasya vai ।। tālukampo atha nābheśca ardhamāsaṃ sa jīvati ।। pūrvadṛṣṭaṃ na jānāti caturmāsaṃ sa jīvati ।।
nityaṃ vahati hikkāṃ tu varṣamekaṃ sa jīvati ।। pūjayā japahomena dhyānadhāraṇayā priye ।। nāḍīnāṃ śodhanaṃ caiva vāyūnāṃ ca jayaḥ katham ।। paramo yogasadbhāvo guhyādguhyataraḥ priye ।।
supraśaste bhūpradeśe nāgnitoyasamīpataḥ ।। niḥśabdakīṭavalmīke ītibhiḥ parivarjite ।। devadevaṃ samabhyarcya bhairavaṃ savināyakam ।। āsanaṃ svastikaṃ baddhvā padmakaṃ bhadrameva vā ।।
dahanotpūyane kṛtvā plāvayedamṛtena ca ।। antaryāgaṃ yathāpūrvam uccāryaṃ ca paraṃ tathā ।। mantraṃ bindumatītaṃ tu nādāntajyotirākṛtim ।। apasavyena pūryeta savyenaiva virecayet ।।
recanātpūraṇādrodhāt prāṇāyāmasridhā smṛtaḥ ।। ābhyantareṇa recyeta pūryetābhyantareṇa tu ।। nābhyāṃ hṛdayasaṃcārān manaścendriyagocarāt ।। prāṇarodhe tu saṃpūrṇe nābhau nītvā samucchvasan ।।
vāyavī dhāraṇāṅguṣṭhe āgneyī nābhimadhyataḥ ।। ākāśadhāraṇā mūrdhni sarvasiddhikarī smṛtā ।। saṃniruddhe tu vai prāṇe mūrdhni gatvā nivartate ।। rāgadveṣau prahīyete prāṇāyāmaiḥ sudhāritaiḥ ।।
hṛdgude nābhikaṇṭhe ca sarvasandhau tathaiva ca ।। drutatāranibho rakta indragopakasaṃnibhaḥ ।। ghaṇṭākaṃsābdamadhuro gajanādo mahādhvaniḥ ।। jalpitaṃ hasitaṃ gītaṃ nṛttaṃ yuddhagatiḥ kalāḥ ।।
praveśayedannapānaṃ tanmalaṃ srāvayedadhaḥ ।। aśitaṃ līḍhapītaṃ ca samānaḥ samatāṃ nayet ।। svedaśca romaharṣaśca śūlaṃ dāho aṅgabhañjanam ।। aṅguṣṭhajānuhṛdaye locane mūrdhni saṃsthitāḥ ।।
āhlādodvegajanakaḥ śoṣaṇastrāsanastathā ।। atinidrākaraścānyo yojakaśca dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। nāgādīnāṃ tu pañcānāṃ mṛtyukāle viceṣṭitam ।। ākuñcayati vai kūrmaḥ śoṣayecca kalevaram ।।
jite manasi śāntasya paraṃ tattvaṃ prakāśate ।। prāṇodānaṃ tu kaṇṭhe tu prāṇavyānaṃ tu sarvagam ।। niruddhasya ca yaḥ kālas taṃ vakṣyāmi nibodha me ।। jito anilo bhavatyeva saṃkrāntyutkrāntikarmaṇi ।।
divyā dṛṣṭiśca śravaṇaṃ divyā vākca prajāyate ।। manasā cintitāvāptiḥ pravarteta guṇāṣṭakam ।। saṃsārabandhanirmuktaḥ śivatulyaśca jāyate ।। nābhyādhāre ca yogīndraḥ svedaḥ kampaśca jāyate ।।
dīrghakoṭisamāyogāt tatkṣaṇācca patedbhuvi ।। plutakoṭisamāyogāt svapnavṛttistato bhavet ।। suṣuptaṃ jāyate tatra kṣaṇāccaiva prabuddhyate ।। evamabhyasatastasya pratyayastu tadā bhavet ।।
bhittvā krameṇa sarvaṇi unmanyantāni yāni tu ।। jāyate unmanastvaṃ hi dehenānena sādhake ।। atītānāgataṃ caiva trailokye yatpravartate ।। prasaṅge adhyātmakālasya jñānaṃ vijñānameva ca ।।
sarvametatsamākhyātam aṃśakāṃśca nibodha me ।। bhāvāṃśakaḥ svabhāvāṃśaḥ puṣpapātāṃśa eva ca ।। devānusmaraṇaṃ bhāvaḥ sahajaṃ taṃ vijānata ।। brahmāṃśo vedabhaktastu rudrāṃśaṃ ca nibodha me ।।
viṣṇvaṃśo viṣṇubhaktaśca candrāṃśaḥ priyadarśanaḥ ।। lubdho garvitamṛṣṭāśī vātāṃśaścapalaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। dīrgharoṣaḥ pūtivaktro gurukṣīraruciḥ sadā ।। vidyādharāṃśakaḥ prāṇī daityāṃśo dveṣaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
