rakṣoṃśaḥ krūranistriṃśo devadveṣī dvijeṣu ca ।। agnyaṃśaḥ paruṣastīvra uṣṇādaḥ piṅgalastathā ।। iṣṭāni kurute nityaṃ dayāluḥ śivabhāvitaḥ ।। bhairavāṅgasamālabdhāḥ sarve devā varānane ।।
svabhāvāṃśaḥ samākhyātaḥ sādhakānāṃ hitāya vai ।। sa mantraḥ siddhyate tasya tamevārādhayedyadi ।। vaihāyasaṃ dhvaja caiva homayedyastu sādhakaḥ ।। anaṃśako api yo mantro jñātacihnairvarānane ।।
śiṣyasya pūrvavatkarma kṛtvā tu vidhipūrvakam ।। paratattvamabhidhyāyan sādhayenmanasepsitam ।। hīnamadhyasamutkṛṣṭaṃ kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। siddhaṃ caiva susiddhaṃ ca uttamaṃ parikīrtitam ।।
ātmanāmākṣaraṃ tadvad adhobhāge asya yojayet ।। yasminsa nipateddevi tamāyaṃ parikalpayet ।। parvaṇi prathame siddhaḥ sādhyaścaiva dvitīyake ।। arisādhyau parityajya dātavyaścumbakena tu ।।
yastvaṃśakaviśuddhaḥ syād bhairavo atra varānane ।। yataḥ sarvagato devaḥ sarveṣvantargataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। kathitaṃ sarahasyaṃ te guhyādguhyataraṃ param ।। adṛṣṭavigrahāyātaṃ śivātparamakāraṇāt ।।
tadevāpararūpeṇa śivena paramātmanā ।। puruṣārthaṃ vicāryāśu sādhanāni pṛthak pṛthak ।। tadanugrahayogyānāṃ sve sve viṣayagocare ।। guruśiṣyapade sthitvā svayaṃ devaḥ sadāśivaḥ ।।
tajjñānamīśvare adāttad īśvareṇa śivecchayā ।। māyāniyatiparyantais tasmādrudrairavāpi tat ।। tenāpi tadadhaḥ proktaṃ rudrāṇāmīśvarecchayā ।। mamāpi ca purā dīkṣā tathā caivābhiṣecanam ।।
mayāpi tava deveśi sādhikāraṃ samarpitam ।। brahmaviṣvindradevānāṃ vasumātṛdivākṛtām ।। kathayasva ṛṣīṇāṃ ca ṛṣibhyo manujeṣvapi ।। tvayā guptataraṃ kāryaṃ na deyaṃ yasya kasyacit ।।
yanna kasyacidākhyātaṃ tatte vakṣyāmi suvrate ।। sṛṣṭisaṃhārakartāraṃ hṛdayāttu vinirgataḥ ।। taḍitpuñjanibhoddaṃṣṭraṃ jaṭājvālāsamaprabham ।। bṛhadvakṣaḥ sthalābhogaṃ nāgayajñopavītinam ।।
sarpahārakṛtāṭopaṃ sarpakaṅkaṇanūpuram ।। gajacarmāvṛtapaṭaṃ śaśāṅkakṛtaśekharam ।। kapālamālābharaṇaṃ khaḍgakheṭakadhāriṇam ।। kapālakhaṭvāṅgadharaṃ varadābhayapāṇikam ।।
brahmendraviṣṇunamitaṃ tridaśairapi durlabham ।। smaraṇānnāśayeddevaḥ pāpasaṃghātamulbaṇam ।। pañcapraṇavapūrvāntaṃ tatra līnaṃ japenmanum ।। pūrvoktabhūpradeśe ca viśuddhe śubhalakṣaṇe ।।
tatra maṇḍalamālikhya pūrvoktairvarṇakaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। susūtritaṃ samaṃ kṛtvā caturasraṃ samantataḥ ।। madhye padmaṃ samālikhya kesarairupalakṣitam ।। evaṃ susūtritaṃ kṛtvā bāhye caiva tu vartulam ।।
madhyapadmapramāṇena dvāraṃ kalpyeta pūrvavat ।। keśayajñopavītī ca digvāsāḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। parito astraṃ pravinyasya bhairavaṃ pūjayetpriye ।। tameva sakalaṃ devaṃ svacchandaṃ parameśvaram ।।
tena cāvāhayeddevi hṛcchiraśca śikhāṃ tathā ।। sthāpanaṃ saṃnidhānaṃ ca nirodhārdhādipūjanam ।। madhyasthaṃ bhairavaṃ pūjyam aṅgaṣaṭkasamanvitam ।। pūrvārakātsamārabhya yāvadante vyavasthitāḥ ।।
aruṇā ghoṣā devī ca revatī bhogadāyikā ।। ghorarūpā ravā ghoṇā ratistārātha rūpiṇī ।। takṣakī ca tathā śārvī barbarā sarvagā tathā ।। stambhanī roṣaṇī caiva drāvā rudrā praśāsinī ।।
praṇavādistato varṇo devīnāma natistathā ।। hemābhaṃ prākcatuṣkaṃ tad indracāpasamaprabham ।। kapālamālābharaṇaṃ prahasattu vicintayet ।। daṇḍahastaṃ smaredyāmyāṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ subhīṣaṇam ।।
śyāmaṃ vāruṇadigbhāge pāśahastaṃ vicintayet ।। uttaraṃ dhavalaṃ jñeyaṃ gadākheṭakadhāri ca ।। evaṃ dhyānaparo yastu cakrametatsadābhyaset ।। mahendre malaye sahye pāriyātre arbude tathā ।।
gaṅgāyamunāsaṃbādhe kurukṣetre varānane ।। antarvedyāṃ supuṇyāyāṃ narmadāyāṃ tathaiva ca ।। yeṣu yeṣu pradeśeṣu svayaṃbhūrbhagavāñchivaḥ ।। vāṅniruddhaḥ prasannātmā lakṣākṣarajape rataḥ ।।
trikālapūjānirato athāgnikāryaparāyaṇaḥ ।। tasya mantraḥ prasiddhyettu sādhayetsacarācaram ।। saptalokaṃ sabrahmāṇḍaṃ pañcāṣṭakamataḥ param ।। niyatiḥ kālatattvaṃ ca rāgo vidyā kalā tathā ।।
sarvaṃ siddhyatyanāyāsān mantrarājaprabbhāvataḥ ।। sādhayennātra saṃdeho bhairavasya vaco yathā ।। jātiyogayutaṃ kṛtvā aṣṭapatre kuśeśaye ।। dhyāyanneva mahādevi svacchandaṃ parameśvaram ।।
atha rakṣāvidhāneṣu aghoraṃ yojayedyathā ।। dvātriṃśadarasaṃyuktaṃ cakramālikhya bhāmini ।। gorocanāṃ tu saṃgṛhya siddhālaktakasaṃyutām ।। vidyārājaṃ karṇikāsthaṃ bindunādasamanvitam ।।
kaṣamadhye varārohe nayanādyantarodhitam ।। pūrvoktadevatā devi tadgarbhe sādhyamālikhet ।। trīnvārāṃstu varārohe dhyānayogasamāśritaḥ ।। indunācchuritaṃ kṛtvā puṣpadhūpaiḥ prapūjayet ।।
pañcaraṅgakasūtreṇa veṣṭayitvā varānane ।। yadā mṛtyuvaśāghrātaṃ kālena kalitaṃ priye ।। tasya mṛtyurna jāyeta ityevaṃ bhairavo abravīt ।। bhūrjapatre varārohe rocanāyā rasena tu ।।
vauṣaḍjātiprayogeṇa tasya mṛtyurna jāyate ।। analārṇamadhaścordhve sādhyārṇeṣu niyojayet ।। jvalantaṃ cintayetsādhyaṃ dinānāṃ saptakaṃ yadi ।। krodharājaniruddhaṃ tu śmaśānapaṭamadhyagam ।।
yasya nāma varārohe huṃphaṭkāravidarbhitam ।। mriyate saptarātreṇa yo rakṣābhiḥ surakṣitaḥ ।। sādhyanāmnastu deveśi huṃphaṭkāravidarbhiṇaḥ ।। manmathena yutaṃ kṛtvā sādhyanāma varānane ।।
amuko atra varārohe taddiśo abhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ ।। saptāhādvaśamāyāti iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ ।। yakārādyantasaṃruddhaṃ mantraṃ phaḍdvitayānvitam ।। akṣapuṣpairvarārohe taddiśo abhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ ।।
somarājena deveśi ādimadhyāntasaṃyutam ।। saṃnidhāpya trimadhure sthāpayetsurasundari ।। asādhyaṃ sādhayatyāśu dhanaṃ ca vipulaṃ labhet ।। saṃjñāṃ samuccareddevi krūrajātisamanvitām ।।
mṛtyunñjayaṃ pravakṣyāmi tamekāgramanāḥ śṛṇu ।। tasminsamālikhetpadmam aṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam ।। saṃveṣṭayāṣṭau diśo devi svacchandena kṛśodari ।। patrāṣṭake apyaghorasya nāmādhastātsamālikhet ।।
ādau tryakṣaravinyāsaṃ svacchandaṃ tadanantaram ।। punastryakṣaravinyāsaṃ vaṣaḍantaṃ niyojayet ।। jāyate paramā śāntiḥ punaranyannibodha me ।। nāma kṛtvā varārohe prakṣipenmadhuratraye ।।
bhūrjapatraṃ samādāya rocanāyā varānane ।। tadabhyantaragarbhe tu svarairantarītaṃ kuru ।। dhruveṇa veṣṭayetpaścād vakāreṇa tataḥ priye ।। punarveṣṭaya ṭhakāreṇa māyābījena suvrate ।।
svacchandasahitāṃ devi praṇavenādiyojitām ।। gandhapuṣpādinā pūjya prakṣipenmadhuratraye ।। athavā guṭikāṃ kṛtvā kaṇṭhe bāhau ca dhārayet ।। tryakṣaraṃ mūlamantraṃ ca vaṣaḍjātisamanvitam ।।
na tasya jāyate mṛtyur bhairavasya vaco yathā ।। mūlamantrasamopetam aghoraṃ tatra yojayet ।। daṃṣṭrākarālavikaṭaṃ jvālāmālopaśobhitam ।। pūrvarūpasamopetaṃ sūryakoṭisamaprabham ।।
tajjvālābhiḥ sudīptābhir dagdhaṃ saṃcintayedviṣam ।। graheṣvevaṃ vidhaṃ dhyānaṃ yaḥ kuryānmocayetkṣaṇāt ।। tadāgadairmahādevi nirviṣaṃ kurute kṣaṇāt ।। gokarṇikāsitaṃ mūlaṃ somāhvāmūlasaṃyutam ।।
gonimbasya ca mūlena nirviṣatvaṃ prajāyate ।। pāne nasye pradātavyaṃ tadā bhavati nirviṣaḥ ।। pāne nasye pradātavyaṃ tadā bhavati nirviṣaḥ ।। nirviṣastu prajāyeta bhairavasya vaco yathā ।।
nirviṣastu bhaveddevi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। mayūrapittasaṃyuktaṃ guṭikāṃ kārayetpriye ।। na viṣaṃ kramate tasya yaśca daṣṭo mahoragaiḥ ।। na viṣaṃ kramate tasya iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ ।।
kālāgnirnarakāścaiva pātālā hāṭakeśvaraḥ ।। svacchandeneti sarvaṃ hi parameśvareṇa pravartitam] ।। kathayasva prasādena sādhakānāṃ hitāya tam ।। atha kālāgnirudrādhaḥ kaṭāhaḥ saṃvyavasthitaḥ ।।
navanavatikoṭyaścāpy aṇḍānāṃ tu sahasrakam ।। arbudānyatha vṛndāni kharvāṇi ca tathaiva ca ।। teṣāṃ vai nāyako hyatra tv anantaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। śaktyādhārāśrayaireva dvātriṃśatparisaṃkhyayā ।।
divyāṅgānaughasaṃkīrṇā bhrūbhaṅgalalitekṣaṇaiḥ ।। na tatra diḥkhitaḥ kaścin muktvā diḥkhamanaṅgajam ।। bhuvaneṣu vicitreṣu yonyākāreṣu saṃsthitāḥ ।। sarvāṇi śuddhimāyānti tānyanante viśodhite ।।
adhikāraṃ prakurute tadājñānuvidhāyakaḥ ।। adhunā saṃpravakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ śivanirmitam ।। avyaktāddaśabhirbhāgair mahānsthūlo vibhāvyate ।। bhūtādeḥ parimāṇaṃ ca bhāvagrāhyaṃ na cākṣuṣam ।।
jālāntaragate bhānau paramāṇuḥ sa ucyate ।। trasareṇuḥ sa vikhyātaḥ tatpadmaraja ucyate ।। vālāgrāṇi tathātvaṣṭau likṣeti parikīrtitā ।। aṣṭau yavā varārohe parvāṅguṣṭhamathāṅgulam ।।
tāladvayaṃ bhaveddhastaś caturviṃśatikāṅgulaḥ ।। dhanuḥ sahasre dve pūrṇe krośaḥ samabhidhīyate ।। anena parimāṇena yojanānāṃ yaśasvini ।। sahasramucchritaṃ tasya mahāpīṭheṣu suvrate ।।
sitaraktapītakṛṣṇaś caturvaktro mahābalaḥ ।। vaktrajvālā jaṭājvālā lomajvālāḥ sujājvalāḥ ।। jvalatparvatavaddīpto jvalajjvālābhirājitaḥ ।। śaraśārṅgavihastaśca pāśāṅkuśadharastathā ।।
daśayojanalakṣāṇi śarīraṃ bhāti bhāsvaram ।। saṃbhṛtaṃ rudrakanyābhī rudrairjvalitaśūlibhiḥ ।। jvālāstasya viniṣkrāntāḥ koṭayo daśacordhvataḥ ।। na kaścinnavasatyatra dhūmoṣmaparivāritaḥ ।।
pañcāśatkoṭayo devi kathitāhyanupūrvaśaḥ ।। catvāriṃśatsamopetaṃ kathitaṃ nāmataḥ śṛṇu ।। tāmisraścāndhatāmisraḥ saṃjīvanasujīvanau ।। sūcīmukhaḥ mahākāyaḥ kṣuradhāro asiparvataḥ ।।
drumārāmaśca vikhyātaḥ kumbhīpākastathaiva ca ।। vajratuṇḍaśca śakuniḥ mīnodarakharodarau ।। uṣṭragrīvo mahākāyo vetālo vaḍavāmukhaḥ ।। saṃgrahaśca kapālaśca taptakavaca eva ca ।।
pīḍanaścaivakumbhīraḥ krakacaḥ śūlameva ca ।। pañcavaktraḥ śatāsyaśca jalauko biladhūmakaḥ ।। asthibhaṅgaḥ pūtimāṃsaḥ dravyaścaiva tvamedhyakaḥ ।। socchvāsaśca nirucchvāsaḥ vṛkāsyaśca tathaiva ca ।।
śvavaktro atha davāgniśca kṣārakūpastathā tamaḥ ।। virūpo rūpavāṃścaiva citrī citradharastathā ।। kubjaḥ uttaptatailākhyaḥ aśanī vṛṣṭimudgarau ।। krimikūṭaḥ bahuśākhaḥ śalmaliśca phaḍistathā ।।
tanubhedaścoragaśca vṛścikaḥ kāla eva ca ।। ghoraścājagaraścaiva mahāvaitaraṇī tathā ।। kardamaḥ durduraścaiva lamboṣṭho vajranāsikaḥ ।। kākaḥ kaṅkumamukhaścaiva śivārāvastataḥ paraḥ ।।
mahāgrāhastathā nakro mūṣikākīṭasāgaraḥ ।। trapulepastrapukūpaḥ ikṣuyantraḥ girerlatā ।। ete atighorā narakās trikoṇāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। nistriṃśakarmakartṝṇāṃ śaṭhānāṃ pāpināṃ tathā ।।
paradāraratānāṃ ca śivaśāstrasya dūṣiṇām ।। goghnānāṃ ca kṛtaghnānāṃ mitravisrambhaghātinām ।। dayādākṣiṇyahīnānāṃ paiśunyānṛtacetasām ।। śubhakarmaratā lokā narake na patanti hi ।।
satyaṃ kṣāntirahiṃsā ca śaucaṃ snānamakalkatā ।। śānto dāntaḥ suhṛṣṭātmā tv anahaṃkāravānsamaḥ ।। amātsaryamamānitvaṃ śivabhaktiracāpalam ।। vratāni niyamāścaiva svādhyāyaśca tridaṃdhyatā ।।
tejaḥ praśāntiḥ saṃtoṣo apriyavākyavivarjanam ।। adambhitvamamāyitvam akalko jñānaśīlatā ।। agnau homo gururdānaṃ jñānināṃ paryupāsanam ।। avyāpāraḥ parārtheṣu audāsīnyamanāgasaḥ ।।
yastvetānbhajate bhāvān so amṛtatvāya kalpate ।। śivācāraratānāṃ tu dhārmikāṇāṃ hi dehinām ।। yasya cittamasaṃbhrāntaṃ nirvikalpamakalmaṣam ।। yasya buddhirasaṃmūḍhā sarvabhūteṣvapātakī ।।
jitāni yenendriyāṇi mano yasya vaśe sthitam ।। svakārye parakārye vā yasya buddhiḥ sthirā bhavet ।। ityeṣa tāntriko nyāyaḥ kathitastu samāsataḥ ।। śivaśāstraratā ye tu gurubhaktiparāyaṇāḥ ।।
eteṣāṃ narakāṇāṃ tu pradhānāni nibodha me ।। catvāriṃśacchataṃhyetat samāsātparikīrtitam ।। pañcatriṃśadyadā vaite dvātriṃśadvā viśodhitāḥ ।। tribhiḥ śuddhaistu dvātriṃśac chuddhā eva bhavanti hi ।।
avīciścaiva vikhyātaḥ kumbhīpākaśca dāruṇaḥ ।। adhomadhyordhvabhāgeṣu saṃsthitāste yathākramam ।। narakaikādaśagatam avīciṃ śodhayetpriye ।। mahārauravasaṃjñaṃ cāpy evameva na saṃśayaḥ ।।
avīciḥ kriminicayo nadī vaitaraṇī tathā ।। socchvāsaśca nirucchvāsaḥ pūtimāṃsaḥ parastathā ।। antarbhūtā avīcau tu kumbhīpākasya śrūyatām ।। vasāmiśrohyayastuṇḍas trapulepaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।
tapralohaśca vijñeyaḥ kṣuradhārapathastathā ।। ekādaśāntarvijñeyāḥ kumbhīpākasya dāruṇāḥ ।। kālasūtro mahāpadmaḥ kumbhaḥ saṃjīvanekṣukau ।। daṇḍayantrastvamedhyaśca ghorarūpastathāparaḥ ।।
avīcau kṛminarakān kumbhīpāke sudāruṇān ।। dvātriṃśannarakāṇāṃ ca mānaṃ caiva nibodha me ।। lakṣamātrāntarā jñeyā dvātriṃśaccāpyanukramāt ।। yogaiśvaryaguṇopetaḥ kūṣmāṇḍādhipatiḥ sthitaḥ ।।
tasyopariṣṭātpātālān kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। mahātalaṃ ca sutalaṃ rasātalamataḥ param ।। ābhāsādyāvatsauvarṇaṃ pramāṇaṃ kathayāmi te ।। ekaikasyāntaraṃ jñeyaṃ sahasraparisaṃkhyayā ।।
sarvakāmaiḥ sametāni guṇaiḥ sarvairyutāni tu ।। kiṅkiṇījālamukharais toraṇāṭṭālamaṇḍitaiḥ ।। tantrīmurajavādyaiśca geyatūryaravākulaiḥ ।। prāsādaistuṅgaśikharaiś candrātapasamaprabhaiḥ ।।
kokilārāvamadhuraiḥ śikhiṣaṭpadasevitaiḥ ।। sārasārāvasaṃghuṣṭapadminīṣaṇḍamaṇḍitaiḥ ।। puruṣaiśca mahākāyair mahābalaparākramaiḥ ।। divyavastraiḥ sutāmbūlair divyagandhānulepanaiḥ ।।
śivārādhanasaktā ye tatprasādena sādhakāḥ ।। rasaṃ rasāyanaṃ divyaṃ siddhadravyaṃ labhanti te ।। kāminaḥ kāmarūpaistu mattamātaṅgagāmibhiḥ ।। divyavastraparīdhānaiḥ stanabhārasamānataiḥ ।।
sakiṅkiṇīnitambaiśca hārakeyūraśobhitaiḥ ।। evaṃ te kathitā devi pātālāntaravāsinaḥ ।। ekaikatra ca pātāle kathitāste varānane ।। balohyatibalaścaiva balavānbalavikramaḥ ।।
etaiḥ śuddhairime śuddhāḥ saptapātālavāsinaḥ ।। tatra vasatyasau devo hāṭakaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। siddhairudragaṇairdivyair bhaginīmātṛbhirvṛtaḥ ।। siddhadravyasamairmantraiś cintāmaṇirasāyanaiḥ ।।
haṭhatpraveśayellokāṃ stadbhāvagatamānasān ।। tasyordhve tu sahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ tu viṃśatiḥ ।। ato bhagavatī pṛthvī nānājanapadākulā ।। tasyācalasya vistāram ūrdhvādhaḥ kathayāmi te ।।
ṣoḍaśaiva sahasrāṇi adhobhāge praropitaḥ ।। tasyordhve tu sabhā divyā nāmnā caiva manovatī ।। sarvaratnasuśobhāḍhyā strīsahasrasamanvitā ।। siddhavidyādharākīrṇā ṛṣibhiḥ parivāritā ।।
sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ gaṇaprathamasevitam ।। strīsahasrasamākīrṇaṃ sarvaiśvaryasamanvitam ।। lokapālairvṛto asau hi brahmaviṣṇvindranāyakaḥ ।। adhikāraṃ prakurute parecchāsaṃpracoditaḥ ।।
yojanānāṃ parityajya cakravāṭaḥ samantataḥ ।। pūrveṇendrasya vikhyātā purī nāmnāmarāvatī ।। dakṣiṇe yamarājasya nāmnā saṃyamanī purī ।। paścimena jaleśasya nāmnā śuddhavatī smṛtā ।।
uttareṇāpi somasya purī nāmnā mahodayā ।। etāsāmuttare devi śṛṇu ṣaḍviṃśatiṃ purīḥ ।। sauvarṇī siddhasaṅghānāṃ tasyā vai dakṣiṇena tu ।। ādityānāṃ purīkhyātā nāmnācāṃśumatī śubhā ।।
vahneḥ paścimadigbhāge viśveṣāṃ revatī purī ।। paścime dharmarājasya mātṛnandā purī smṛtā ।। rudrāṇāṃ paścime tasyā rohitā nāma kāñcanī ।। tasyāḥ paścimato jñeyā nāmnā guṇavatī purī ।।
nirṛteḥ pūrvabhāge tu piṅgalā nāma vai purī ।। nairṛtyuttarasāmīpye purī kṛṣṇāvatī smṛtā ।। tasyā apyuttare bhāge purī haimī sukhāvatī ।। tasyā apyuttare haimī gāndharvī nāma viśṛtā ।।
daśakoṭisahasrāṇi teṣāṃ saṃkhyā prakīrtitā ।। hemasaṃjñā vasūnāṃ tu varuṇasyāpi cottare ।। sarvavidyādharāṇāṃ tu sā purī parikīrtitā ।। vasanti kinnarāstatra purairhemārkasaprabhaiḥ ।।
gandharvarājamukhyasya divyagandharvanāditā ।। grāmatrayaparīdhānā jātimekhalamaṇḍitā ।। lakṣaṇavyañjanopetā madhyamenāvaguṇṭhitā ।। nāradādyaiśca ṛṣibhir nāgakinnarasevitā ।।
somasya paścātpramadā guhyakānāṃ purī smṛtā ।। sarvadhātumayī citrā kuberasya mahātmanaḥ ।। yakṣāṇāmuttamaḥ śrīmān āste bhogairanuttamaiḥ ।। tatra vai karmadevāstu devatvaṃ karmaṇā gatāḥ ।।
tatrāste śrīpatiḥ śrīmān atasīpuṣpasannibhaḥ ।। īśasya dakṣiṇebhāge nāmnā padmavatī purī ।। padmapatrāyatākṣasya brahmaṇaḥ padmajanmanaḥ ।। aśvinau tatra deveśi tathā dhanvantariḥ sthitaḥ ।।
vināyakānāṃ sā divyā vasatistatra kalpitā ।। vināyakā mahādīptā agnijvalitatejasaḥ ।। evaṃvidhairadhaścordhvaṃ meruḥ puravarairvṛtaḥ ।। purakoṭisahasraistu sarvāstāḥ saṃbhṛtāḥ priye ।।
divyastrībhiḥ samākīrṇā divyapuṃbhiḥ samākulāḥ ।। vimānanagarārāmaiś caturodyānamaṇḍapaiḥ ।। dvandvabhīnandiśabdaiśca śaṅkhakāhalaniḥsvanaiḥ ।। iṣṭāpūrtaratā devi ye narā puṇyabhārate ।।
gaṅgātoyasusaṃsiktāḥ krīḍanti surasattamāḥ ।। kathayasva prasādena samāsātsurasattama ।। jaganmātā mahādevi mama patnī purā hi sā ।। punarudghāṭite netre jaganmātaḥ purā tvayā ।।
daśadhā niḥsṛtā gaṅgā kapālāvaraṇe mama ।। dvitīyā brahmalokordhve tṛtīyā satyalokagā ।। somāccaiva viniḥ sṛtya purakāśe vyavasthitā ।। gaṅgānadīṃ mahāpuṇyāṃ martyānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।
tato mayā sureśāni proktā sā tvaparājitā ।। āgatya mama mūrdhānaṃ merumūrdhni punargatā ।। pūrve sītā samuddiṣṭā suvahā dakṣiṇena tu ।। mandarastu mahādevi gandhamādanasaṃjñakaḥ ।।
viṣkambhāśca samākhyātāḥ varṇāṃścaiva nibodha me ।। prāgviṣkambhasamīpe tu nāmnā citrarathaṃ vanam ।। gandhamādanasāmīpye nandanaṃ tu mahāvanam ।। vipulasya samīpe tu vaibhrājaṃ tu mahāvanam ।।
vanaṃ pitṛvanaṃ nāma svapārśvasya samīpataḥ ।। kalpadrumāṃśca caturaḥ kathayāmi nibodha tān ।। sahasrayojanāyāmaṃ śākhāpañcaśatocchritam ।। tatpramāṇā smṛtā jambūr gandhamādanamūrdhani ।।
tena jambūnadī jātā priye vegavatī bhṛśam ।। tatsaṃparkātsamutpannaṃ kanakaṃ devabhūṣaṇam ।। tatra vṛkṣālatāgulmāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ śvāpadādayaḥ ।। vipule api tathāśvatthaḥ ketumāla iti śrutaḥ ।।
tenāsau ketumāleti khyātaḥ siddhaniṣevitaḥ ।। anekaguṇasaṃpanno meruḥ khyātaḥ samāsataḥ ।। merumadhyāccaturdikṣu lakṣārdhaṃ tu samāsataḥ ।। parvatāntaritāstatra nava bhāgā bhavanti hi ।।
niṣadho hemakūṭaśca himavāniti te trayaḥ ।। prāk paścimāyātā hyete ṣaḍeva tu mahīdharāḥ ।। śvetaśca hemakūṭaśca sahasranavatiḥ smṛtau ।। lavaṇodadhiparyantāḥ sahasradvayavistṛtāḥ ।।
śṛṅgavāṃścandrakanibhaḥ sitaḥ śveto virājate ।। sauvarṇo hemakūṭaśca himābho himavāniti ।। catustriṃśatsahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ sureśvari ।। tathaivāparadigbhāge tattulyo gandhamādanaḥ ।।
catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ samucchritāḥ ।। jaṭharo hemakūṭastu pūrvabhāge vyavasthitau ।। niṣadhaḥ pāriyātraśca apareṇa mahīdharau ।। meroḥ samantato ramyam ilāvṛtamudāhṛtam ।।
yojanānāṃ caturdikṣu caturaśraṃ samantataḥ ।। prabhavanti hi lokānāṃ merorbhāsā prabhāsitam ।। jambūrasaphalāhārā jarāmṛtyuvivarjitāḥ ।। devagandharvasiddhāśca ṛṣayo atha vināyakāḥ ।।
evamādyairasaṃkhyātair vṛtaṃ caitadilāvṛtam ।। ketumālamiti khyātaṃ varṣaṃ sarvaguṇottamam ।। panasasya rasaṃ pītvā jīvantyayutameva ca ।। viśālaḥ kambalaḥ kṛṣṇas tatra sapta kulādrayaḥ ।।
varṣaṃ bhadrāśvasaṃjñaṃ ca tatrāpi tvayutāyuṣaḥ ।। kaurañjaḥ śvetaparṇaśca nīlo mālāgrakastathā ।। dvātriṃśattu sahasrāṇi pūrvapaścāyate smṛte ।। varṣe dve tu samākhyāte kuruvarṣanivāsinaḥ ।।
trayodaśasaharāṇi jīvanti sthirayauvanāḥ ।। śyāmāpuṣpanibhāḥ snigdhāḥ surūpāḥ puruṣāḥ striyaḥ ।। navayojanasāhasraṃ dhanvākāraṃ prakīrtitam ।। kalpavṛkṣaḥ kururnāma tatraiva kusumojjvalaḥ ।।
tasyacottaradigbhāge praviśya lavaṇodadhim ।। tathā vāyavyadigbhāge praviśya lavaṇodadhim ।। daśayojanasāhasraṃ dvīpaṃ bhadraṃ prakīrtitam ।। ayutāyuṣo janāstatra divyāmṛtaphalāśinaḥ ।।
śvetaśṛṅgavatoścaiva madhye jñeyaṃ hiraṇmayam ।। jīvantyabdasahasrāṇi mānenārdhatrayodaśa ।। ramyakaṃ nāma varṣaṃ tu nyagrodhaphalabhojanāḥ ।। dvādaśābdasahasrāṇi teṣāmāyuḥ prakīrtitam ।।
hemakūṭasya saumyena dakṣiṇe niṣadhasya tu ।। dvādaśaiva sahasrāṇi jīvantīkṣurasāśinaḥ ।। hemakūṭasya yāmyena himavatastvathottare ।। navavarṣasahasrāṇi jīvanti plakṣabhojanāḥ ।।
yāmye himācalendrasya uttare lavaṇodadheḥ ।। janā rogabhayatrastā duḥkhitā mandasaṃpadaḥ ।। bhogino mandabhogāśca tathānye atyantaduḥkhitāḥ ।। varṇajātiprabhedena nānākarmānurūpataḥ ।।
svadeśabhāṣāyuktāni dvīpadvīpāntarāṇi ca ।। yogino jñāninaścaiva dharmiṣṭhāḥ pāpino apare ।। preṣyā dāsāśca bahavo mānavāḥ satataṃ priye ।। naṣṭāsu vidyate kācid yugatrayamayī sthitiḥ ।।
tatraiva yatkṛtaṃ karma śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham ।। mahākālastathaikāmram evamādi varānane ।। gaṅgādīnāṃ nadīnāṃ ca tatra pañca śatāni ca ।। nava bhedāḥ smṛtāstatra sāgarāntaritāḥ priye ।।
śatāni pañca vijñeyaṃ sthalaṃ pañca jalaṃ tathā ।। indradvīpaṃ kaśeruṃ ca tāmravarṇaṃ gabhastimat ।। dvīpaṃ kumārikākhyaṃ ca navamaṃ parikīrtitam ।। yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ tu nānāvarṇāśramānvitam ।।
te tatraiva sthitā loke kumārīsaṃjñake priye ।। mahendro malayaḥ sahyaḥ śaktimānṛkṣaparvataḥ ।। dakṣasāgaramadhyasthāny upadvīpāni ṣaṭ priye ।। kumudaṃ ca varāhaṃ ca ityevaṃ parikīrtitam ।।
tasyapāde trikūṭo vai laṅkā tasyoparisthitā ।। citraprākāraracitā vajravaiḍūryamaṇḍitā ।। ramante kanyakāsaktā mahābalaparākramāḥ ।। tatrāśramo mahāpuṇya āgastyaḥ sphāṭikaprabhaḥ ।।
na tatra jāyate mārī nākālaḥ saṃpravartate ।। na vadatyanṛtaṃ kaścid rāgadveṣau na kutracit ।। tatra vai ṛṣayo vīrā jñānayogakṛtāśramāḥ ।। tryambakasya mahādevi nityamārādhane ratāḥ ।।
tiṣṭhanti bhāvitātmānaḥ śāpānugrahakāriṇaḥ ।। lakṣayojanavistīrṇaṃ lavaṇāmbhaḥ sthitaṃ bahiḥ ।। vṛtrāribhayasaṃtrastāḥ praviṣṭāstatra parvatāḥ ।। vṛṣabho dundubhirdhūmraḥ praviṣṭāḥ pūrvabhāgataḥ ।।
aśoko atha varāhaśca nandanaśca tṛtīyakaḥ ।। cakro mainākasaṃjñaśca tṛtīyastu balāhakaḥ ।। cakramainākayormadhye tiṣṭhedve vaḍavāmukhaḥ ।। svāyaṃbhuvo manurnāma tasya putraḥ priyavrataḥ ।।
agnīdhraścāgnibāhuśca medhā medhātithirvapuḥ ।। medhāḥ satro agnibāhuśca ete pravrajitāstrayaḥ ।। jambudvīpe tathāgnīdhrāḥ tasya putrā nava smṛtāḥ ।। bhadrāśvaḥ ketumālaśca ramyakaśca hiraṇmayaḥ ।।
agnīdhratastu jātā vai śūrāścātibalotkaṭāḥ ।। nābheḥ putro mahāvīryo vṛṣabho dharmatatparaḥ ।। tannamnaiva tu vijñeyaṃ bhārataṃ varṣamuttamam ।। bhārate tvaṣṭadvīpe atra aṣṭau putrā niveśitāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ nāmnā tu te dvīpā bharatena prakīrtitāḥ ।। gomedaṃ puṣkaraṃ caiva sapta dvīpāni pārvati ।। kṣāraḥ kṣīraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ tathā ikṣuraso api ca ।। jambudvīpaṃ smṛtaṃ lakṣaṃ yojanānāṃ pramāṇataḥ ।।
evaṃ dviguṇavṛddhyātra samudrā dvīpasaṃsthitāḥ ।। śāke medhātithirnāma vapuṣmān kuśasaṃjñake ।। gomede havyanāmā tu savanaḥ puṣkare tathā ।। tathā varṇāśramācārā jñeyāstatra nivāsinām ।।
śānto abhayastvaśiśiraḥ sukhado nandakaḥ śivaḥ ।। varṣāṇi sapta khyātāni parvatāṃśca nibodha me ।। somaka ṛṣabhaścaiva vaibhrājaśca kulādrayaḥ ।। vipāśā tridivā kumbhī tathā cāmṛtanālikā ।।
pūrvādārabhya niṣkrāntāḥ praviṣṭāḥ kṣīrasāgaram ।। candrakāntasamāḥ sarve surūpāḥ priyadarśanāḥ ।। kuśe vapuṣmatā pūrvaṃ sapta putrā niveśitāḥ ।। mānasaḥ suvrataśceti varṣanāmnaiva cāṅkitāḥ ।।
mahiṣaḥ kusumaścaiva sapta sīmantaparvatāḥ ।। vīvṛtā ca vivṛndā ca saptaitāstu saridvarāḥ ।। janāstu sukhinastatra dadhnāmṛtaphalāśinaḥ ।। jyotiṣmatā sapta putrāḥ krauñcadvīpe niveśitāḥ ।।
rathakāraśca lavaṇo dhṛtimānsuprabhākaraḥ ।। vaidrumo hemanābhaśca dyutimān puṣpadantakaḥ ।। mahī dhātā śivāpāpā pavitrā saṃtatadyutiḥ ।। ghṛtodaṃ praviśantyetāḥ sarvāḥ pāpaharāḥ priye ।।
ghṛtāmṛtaphalāhārāḥ sutṛptāḥ smarapīḍitāḥ ।। sapta dyutimatā putrāḥ śālmalāvabhiṣecitāḥ ।। munirdundubhināmā ca kuśalaśceti te smṛtāḥ ।। krauñco atha vāmanaścaivāpy andhakāro divākṛtiḥ ।।
pauṇḍarī kauśikī gaurī siddhā caiva kumudvatī ।। nadyastāḥ śailaniṣkrāntā gacchantīkṣurasārṇavam ।। divyakāntiyutāḥ śāntāḥ surūpāḥ priyavādinaḥ ।। havyarājaḥ sutānsapta gomode cābhyaṣecayat ।।
kumudaśconnataścaiva mahābhadra iti smṛtāḥ ।। udayaḥ kesaraścaiva jaṭharo atha suraivataḥ ।। gabhastī sukumārī ca kumārī nālinī tathā ।। madirodaṃ vahantyetāḥ puṇyāḥ puṇyajalodvahāḥ ।।
bhakṣayanti ca tallokāḥ pibanti madirāmṛtam ।। nānāyuvativṛndaiśca rūpayauvanagarvitaiḥ ।। ataśca puṣkarākhye ca savanastatra nāyakaḥ ।। parvato valayākāro mānasottarasaṃjñitaḥ ।।
yojanānāṃ varārohe sarvaratnasamanvitaḥ ।। īrṣyayā rāgatṛṣṇābhir ītibhiśca vivarjitāḥ ।। cakrākārastu boddhavyo mānasastu varānane ।। harervasvekasārākhyā yāmyā saṃyaminī purī ।।
puṣkaradvīpaguṇitaḥ svādūdo ante vyavasthitaḥ ।। yojanānāṃ tu lakṣāṇi koṭidvitayameva ca ।। tato hemamayī bhūmir daśakoṭyo varānane ।। parvato valayākāro yojanāyutavistṛtaḥ ।।
sarvaratnasamopeto hemavarṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। lokapālāḥ sthitāstatra rudrāścāmoghaśaktayaḥ ।। hiraṇyaromā parjanyaḥ ketumān bhājanastathā ।। pūrvādārabhya kramaśo yāvadīśānagocaraḥ ।।
asya madhye varārohe yonayastu caturdaśa ।। lokālokopariṣṭāttu saviturdakṣiṇāyanam ।। ardharātro amarāvatyām astameti yamasya ca ।। yadaiva cāmarāvatyām udayastasya dṛśyate ।।
suvīthī uttare tasya ajavīthī ca dakṣiṇe ।। asya bāhye tamo ghoraṃ duḥprekṣyaṃ jīvavarjitam ।। catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ varānane ।। brahmaṇo aṇḍakaṭāhena yuktā vai merumadhyataḥ ।।
evametacchataṃ jñeyaṃ koṭīnāṃ pārthivaṃ mahat ।। atha vātra mahādevi paripāṭyā samantataḥ ।। śaktiṃ tattvaṃ ca bhuvanaṃ yoniṃ caiva niveśayet ।। anantaṃ caiva kālāgniṃ narakāṃśca yathākramam ।।
upasthānaṃ tataḥ kuryād bhuvarlokasya varānane ।। tataḥ paśustu saṃprokṣya stāḍyo viśleṣya eva ca ।। garbhadhāritvajanane adhikāraṃ tathaiva ca ।। caturdaśa samāsena kathayāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।।
saumyaṃ tathā ca prājeśaṃ brāhmaṃ caivāṣṭamaṃ viduḥ ।। paśupakṣimṛgāścaiva tathānye ca sarīsṛpāḥ ।। devayonisamāyuktaṃ proktaṃ saṃsāramaṇḍalam ।। ātmā saṃsaratihyatra māyādyavanigocare ।।
sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ tathā mohaṃ bhuṅkte caivādhvamadhyagaḥ ।। īśvareṇa nimittena sṛṣṭisaṃhāravartmani ।। adhvamadhye tu ye pāśā jñeyāścānantakoṭayaḥ ।। tasmādevaṃ vijānīyāt adhvā bandhasya kāraṇam ।।
tasya bhedāhyanantāśca bhidyante karmabhedataḥ ।। ātmanā badhyatehyātmā muñcennātmānamātmanā ।। nacodveṣṭayituṃ śakta ātmānaṃ sa punaryathā ।। na ca mocayituṃ śaktāḥ paśavaḥ pāśabandhanāḥ ।।
śivaśaktinipātāttu mucyante pāśabandhanāt ।। yattatsvābhijanaṃ śuddham anaupamyamanāmayam ।। nigūḍhāstatra tiṣṭhanti kāṣṭhe vahniryathā tathā ।। svasvarūpaṃ prapaśyeta bhāsvaraṃ yatsunirmalam ।।
prakāśayati vastūni hatvā vai raśmibhistamaḥ ।। manthakasya vaśāddevi nānyathā tu kathaṃcana ।। ācāryatanumāsthāya sadā cānugrahe sthitaḥ ।। vāgīśī yonisaṃsthānā dhūmo jñeyo malādivat ।।
udbodhito yathā vahnir nirmalo atīva bhāsvaraḥ ।। malakarmakalādyaistu nirmukto vigataklamaḥ ।। rasavahnisamāyogāt tāmraṃ kālikayā yathā ।। na bhūyastāmratāṃ yāti tathātmā na kadācana ।।
tajjñaścaiva śivo jñeya ācāryatanuvigrahaḥ ।। mantradravyakriyāyogād vahnyādhāre tathā priye ।। na bhūyo malatāṃ yāti śivatvaṃ yāti nirmalam ।। śodhayenmukhyapāśāṃśca ye proktāste mayā purā ।।
caturdaśavidhaṃ caiva yaduktaṃ tu mayā purā ।। tadvakṣyāmi kramātsarvaṃ yathā śodhyaṃ śivādhvare ।। brāhmaṃ caiva tu prājeśaṃ saumyamaindraṃ tathaiva ca ।। paiśācaṃ kramataḥ śodhyaṃ sthāvaraṃ mānuṣaṃ tathā ।।
pakṣiṇāṃ garuḍaṃ caiva mṛgāṇāṃ siṃhameva ca ।। antyajāñchūdraviṭ kṣatra brāhmaṇāṃśca viśodhayet ।। daśāhutiprayogeṇa antyajān brāhmaṇāvadhi ।। garbhaḥ puṃsavanaṃ caiva sīmanto jātakarma ca ।।
anenaiva varārohe śodhyāstvaṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ ।। navamo vratabandhastu sa cāṅgī parikīrtitaḥ ।। mekhalā dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca ajinaṃ tryāyuṣaṃ tathā ।। niyantṝṇi ca dṛṣṭāni dīkṣākāle varānane ।।
unmattakāsidhāraṃ ca ghṛteśaṃ saptamaṃ viduḥ ।। caryāvratāni bodhyāni aṅgatve kīrtitāni tu ।। tasyāntarbhūtamevaitat kathitaṃ vratasaptakam ।। vedavratāni catvāri hotavyāni na saṃśayaḥ ।।
vrateśvarāstu catvāro brahmacāriniyāmakāḥ ।। tato bhavati godānaṃ taccaturdaśakaṃ priye ।। kṛtvā darbhamayīṃ patnīṃ tayā saha yajetkratūn ।। naimittikāṃśa tānāhuḥ pravakṣyamyanupūrvaśaḥ ।।
caitrī cāśvayujī ceti sapta pākamakhāḥ kramāt ।। āgneyaṃ cāgnihotraṃ ca darśaṃ caiva tataḥ param ।। paśubandhaḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ sautrāmaṇirataḥ param ।। ebhiḥ saha vijānīyāt saṃskāraikonatriṃśakam ।।
vājapeyo atirātrastu āptoryāmastu saptamaḥ ।। hiraṇyapādaḥ prathamas tathā guhyahiraṇyadhṛt ।। hiraṇyaśrotro hiraṇyatvag ghiraṇyākṣastathaiva ca ।। śatena tu ghṛtaṃ cātra ekaikaṃ tu vijāyate ।।
aśvamedhaṃ tataḥ paścāj juhuyāttu yathākramam ।। aṣṭātriṃśattamaṃ taṃ tu vānaprasthaṃ tato bhavet ।। ata ātmaguṇānaṣṭau kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। śaucaṃ caivamanāyāso maṅgalaṃ cāpyataḥ param ।।
catvāriṃśadathāṣṭau tu saṃskārāśca samāsataḥ ।। ato anteṣṭiṃ tu hutvā vai guṇānāpādayecchiśoḥ ।। tilairghṛtena vātāṃśca ūrdhve tu viniyojayet ।। tasmin saṃyojanaṃ kāryaṃ nacānyatra vidhīyate ।।
yattatra paripāṭyā tu karma tatra niyojayet ।। pañcāhutiprayogeṇa bhogārthaṃ caivamātmanaḥ ।। tasminyuktasya kartavyaṃ nacānyasminkadācana ।। tasmāttu yogaśabdena tattatkarmaikacintanā ।।
śivenāṣṭaśatāhutyā tatastu bhuvanādhipān ।। homenaiva tu saṃśodhya viśleṣaṃ chedanaṃ tathā ।। prāyaścittaṃ tato hutvā nyūnādhikanimittataḥ ।। bhūrlokastu samākhyāto bhuvolokaṃ nibodha me ।।
daśa vāyupathā madhye tv ayutāyutasaṃkhyayā ।। pañcāśadyojanādūrdhvam ṛtarddhirnāma mārutaḥ ।। bṛṃhayecca mahīṃ sarvām āpyāyayati cāvyayaḥ ।। yato gṛddhrāndhārayati tena gṛddhradharaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
sa vai nāśayate vṛkṣān kadācitsaṃpravartayet ।। yadā dahati veśmāni tadāsau samudāhṛtaḥ ।। yojanānāṃ śatādūrdhvaṃ senānīrvāyurucyate ।। te bhuvaḥ krośamātreṇa tiṣṭhanto apasṛjantyapaḥ ।।
matsyamaṇḍūkakūrmāṃśca varṣantyete ca durdine ।। tasmiṃstu rogadā meghā varṣanti ca viṣodakam ।। tasmādūrdhvaṃ tu tāvadbhyo devyamoghaḥ sthito marut ।। vajrāṅgo nāma vai vāyuḥ pañcāśadyojanasthitaḥ ।।
tāvadbhiryojanaireva tato vai vaidyuto anilaḥ ।। aśanirvāyusaṃkṣobhāt teṣvasau jāyate mahān ।। tasminpuṣṭivaho nāma puṣṭiṃ varṣati dehinām ।। pañcāśadyojane te vai tasmiṃstiṣṭhanti toyadāḥ ।।
tasminkrodhodakā nāma meghā vai saṃpratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। rājñāṃ kṣayakaraṃ caiva prajānāṃ kṣayadaṃ tathā ।। aghopyamegho vajrāṅgo vaidyuto raivatastathā ।। agho vasanti vai divyāḥ piśācāḥ skandadehajāḥ ।।
te vai divyaiśca kusumair arcayanti harātmajam ।। triṃśatkoṭisahasrāṇi tasmin vāyau pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। vajrāṅge api tathā vāyau mātaṅgāḥ krūrakarmiṇaḥ ।। vidyādharāṇāmadhamā manaḥ pavanagāminaḥ ।।
sādhayitvā tataḥ siddhās te asmin vāyau pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। tiṣṭhanti sarvadā tatra pṛthivīpurapālane ।। gograhe bandimokṣe vā mriyante puruṣottamāḥ ।। patākādīrghikākīrṇair divyaghaṇṭānināditaiḥ ।।
raivate tu mahātmānaḥ siddhā vai saṃpratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। sādhayitvā mahātmānaḥ siddhāste kāmarūpiṇaḥ ।। saṃvarte api mahāvāyau vidyādharagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। divyagandhānuliptāste divyasragdhāmabhūṣitāḥ ।।
viṣāvartaṃ nāvamiva te vāyuṃ yānti miśritāḥ ।। vaṃśavīṇāvidhijñāśca pakṣiṇaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ ।। upariṣṭādyojanaśatād durjayasyopari sthitāḥ ।। parāvahābhidhaṃ vāyuṃ te samāśritya saṃsthitāḥ ।।
puṣkarāvartakā nāma meghā vai padmajodbhavāḥ ।। parāvahastānvahati manujāniva vāraṇaḥ ।। ekādaśa tu vai koṭyas teṣāṃ tu samudāhṛtāḥ ।। dvitīyamāvahaṃ vāyuṃ meghāste ca samāśritāḥ ।।
āvahastu tato vāyur yatra droṇāḥ samāśritāḥ ।। hitārthaṃ tu prajānāṃ vai nirmitāste mayā purā ।। mahāparivaho nāma vāyusteṣāṃ samāśrayaḥ ।। siddhāśca patayaścaiva kathitā meghacāriṇaḥ ।।
tā vasanti guṇopetā rudraśaktyātvadhiṣṭhitāḥ ।। svakarmabhogasaṃsiddhāḥ sarvasiddhairadhiṣṭhitāḥ ।। nārācacakracāparṣṭi śūlaśaktīṣumudgarāḥ ।। airāvato añjanaścaiva vāmanaśca mahāgajaḥ ।।
kumudaḥ puṇḍarīkaśca sārvabhaumo api cāṣṭamaḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhe vāyupathe devi pakṣirājo mahābalaḥ ।। saptame vyomagaṅgā tu nānājalacarānugā ।। sā bhrāntā nabhaso madhye samantātparimaṇḍalā ।।
puṣpamāleva sā bhāti nabhasaḥ śirasi sthitā ।। gandharvairapsarobhiśca sādhyairviśvairmarudgaṇaiḥ ।। rakṣobhirguhyakaiścaiva divyastutiparāyaṇaiḥ ।। nṛtyadbhirvalgamānaiśca divyadundubhiniḥsvanaiḥ ।।
vaṃśavāditranādaiśca manovāyusamīritaiḥ ।। kesaraiḥ padmarāgaiśca mahācakrapramāṇakaiḥ ।। maṇḍitā ca vanairdivyair dharmādhārā mahānadī ।। mahāmandākinī devī tridaśaiḥ paryupāsitā ।।
śobhitāsau bhagavatī nityamāste nabhastale ।। papāta dharaṇīpṛṣṭhe lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। yojanānāṃ śataṃ pūrṇaṃ vistāro asyāḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। sā bhramantīva saṃtiṣṭhet samantātparimaṇḍalā ।।
divyāmṛtavahā puṇyā sarvapāpapraṇāśinī ।। vasati tvapratīghātaḥ pratyakṣo dharma eva saḥ ।। brahmaiva sākṣādvasati brahmaśaktyā tvadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। atra cāṅgārakaḥ sarpir nairṛtaḥ sadasatpatiḥ ।।
ajaśca bhuvaneśaśca mṛtyuḥ kāpālikastathā ।। dhātā dhruvaśca somaśca varuṇaścānilo analaḥ ।। vasavaḥ kathitāhyete ādityāṃśca nibodha me ।। mitraścaiva samākhyātas tv ajaghanyo jaghanyakaḥ ।।
kāśyapeyānvidustvetān teṣāṃ tejonidheratha ।। yajñaścakraṃ rathe tasmin sarvajñānamayī ca dhūḥ ।। nāgā yoktrāṇi teṣāṃ vai aruṇaścaiva sārathiḥ ।। navayojanasāhasro vigraho bhāskarasya tu ।।
jñānaśaktiḥ parāhyeṣā tapatyādityavigrahā ।। ahorātraṃ bhramantyete bhuvarlokaṃ samantataḥ ।। āpyāyayañjagatsarvaṃ sudhādhārāpravarṣaṇaiḥ ।। indūrdhve lakṣamātreṇa sthitaṃ nakṣatramaṇḍalam ।।
lakṣadvayena tasyordhve saṃsthitaḥ somanandanaḥ ।। tasyordhve api dvilakṣeṇa tiṣṭhate bhṛgunandanaḥ ।। lakṣamātreṇa tu ṛṣīn kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। bhṛgvaṅgirāmarīciśca ṛṣayaḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ ।।
bhītāśca parapīḍāyāḥ śūrāḥ śāstravicāraṇe ।। mantrayogakriyācāryā saṃnaddhā duratikramāḥ ।। tebhyo lakṣādhruvo devi tārakāḥ sa caturdaśa ।। brahmaivāpararūpeṇa brahmasthāne niyojitaḥ ।।
niścalaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ śivaśaktyātvadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। vāyuskandhānsthitāṃstvatra kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। ṛṣisaptakanirdeśād ādhruvāntaṃ ca saptamaḥ ।। atra rājā mahendro vai tiṣṭhate surapūjitaḥ ।।
agnihotraṃ kratūnvāpi kṛtvā jñānavivarjitāḥ ।। svarlokasyoparisṭāttu dve koṭī yojanāni tu ।। ṛṣayaścaiva siddhāśca mārkaṇḍādyā vasanti vai ।। maharlokopariṣṭāttu janalokovyavasthitaḥ ।।
bhautiko vāḍvaliścaiva janalokanivāsinaḥ ।। tapolokaḥ samākhyāta ṛṣiyogeśvarākulaḥ ।। śaṅkuścaiva triśaṅkuśca tapolokanivāsinaḥ ।। bhūrlokāntaṃ samārabhya yāvatsatyaṃ varānane ।।
koṭyaḥ ṣoḍaśamānena tapolokordhvataḥ priye ।। krīḍate bhagavāndevo vṛta ātmasamairdvijaiḥ ।। ānandapadasaṃprāptā ānandapadamāgatāḥ ।। divyagandhaviliptāṅgo divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।।
uttareṇa yajurvedaḥ śuddhasphaṭikasaṃnibhaḥ ।। sthitaḥ paścimadigbhāge sāmavedaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। sragdāmadhārakaścitram ālābhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। piṅgākṣo lohitagrīvo harikeśo mahātanuḥ ।।
vedopaniṣadaścaiva mīmāṃsāraṇyakaṃ tathā ।। gāyatrī ca sthitā tatra yatra devaścaturmukhaḥ ।। koṭiyojanamānena satyalokordhvataḥ priye ।। raktendīvaramadhyasthaḥ padmarāgasamaprabhaḥ ।।
brahmavidbhiḥ samākīrṇo brahmā muniniṣevitaḥ ।। dharmādiphalasaṃbandhapradātā ca yuge yuge ।। sraṣṭā ca sarvabhūtānāṃ sadevāsuramānuṣe ।। nīlendīvarasaṃkāśā indranīlasamaprabhā ।।
sarvakāmasamopetā sarvaratnasamujjvalā ।। ghaṇṭāvitānavistīrṇā cārucāmaraśobhitā ।। kāmakārmukanirghoṣavitrastamṛgalocanaiḥ ।। manobhavaśarāyāsa nipātaśatajarjaraiḥ ।।
saṃsevyate sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ kamalalocanaḥ ।। caturbhujo mahākāyaḥ pīnavakṣā gadādharaḥ ।। saṃsevyate sa bhagavān nikāyairātmavikramaiḥ ।। te tu gacchanti tatsthānaṃ viṣṇoramitavikramāḥ ।।
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaś catvarodyānamaṇḍitaḥ ।। vimānaiḥ puṣpakairyukto haṃsakundendunirmalaiḥ ।। mārutāḥsukhasaṃsparśā vartikarpūragandhayaḥ ।। vareṇyāvaradācaiva variṣṭhā varavarṇinī ।।
gaṅgāhyetāḥ samākhyātā rudralokavahāḥ sadā ।। indranīlanibhairnālair yojanāyatagandhibhiḥ ।। śaradindunibhānāryo navanītasukomalāḥ ।। alipuñjanibhaiḥ keśair mṛgāmodasugandhibhiḥ ।।
dāḍimīpuṣpasaṃkāśair oṣṭhairutpalagandhibhiḥ ।। aśokapallavākāraiḥ pādaiḥ padmadalopamaiḥ ।। svabhāvasusugandhāḍhyaiḥ prasravadbhirivāmṛtam ।। kāñcīḍoraiḥ suraktaiśca kusumairbhūṣitāḥ sadā ।।
suvṛttaiḥ pīnapārśvaiśca pīnakaṇṭhasamāśritaiḥ ।। rājahaṃsagatispardhi mattamātaṅgavibhramāḥ ।। hāsyalāsyavilāsāḍhyabhrūbhaṅgataralekṣaṇāḥ ।। kāmagrahagrahāviṣṭā ghūrṇantyo madavihvalāḥ ।।
yadyapyevaṃvidhānāryaḥ nijabhartṛbhayāturāḥ ।। avagūhya ca sarvāṅgair āpīya vadanairmukham ।। rudrāścaivaṃvidhākārā jñānayogabalotkaṭāḥ ।। keyūrakaṭakairḍoraiḥ puṣpavastravibhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।
mahākāyā mahoraskās trinetrāḥ śūlapāṇayaḥ ।। surasiddhanutāḥsarve suprasanna varapradāḥ ।। na tatra mṛtyurna jarā na śoko asti viyogajaḥ ।। adhikārakṣaye rudrā rudrakanyāsamāvṛtāḥ ।।
gatvā bhūyo na jāyante kalpakoṭiśatairapi ।। mahāvṛṣagajārūḍhaiḥ siṃhavājisuvāhanaiḥ ।। tanmadhyesarvatobhadraṃ siṃhadvāraiḥ sutoraṇaiḥ ।। nandīśvaramahākāla dvārapālagaṇairvṛtam ।।
vitānacchatraṣaṇḍaiśca muktāhārapralambitaiḥ ।। kalaśairdvāranyastaiśca ratnapallavasaṃyutaiḥ ।। svastikaiḥ patravalyāḍhyaiś citritaṃ bhuvanājiram ।। gopurāṭṭālarathakair vīthībhiśca bhramāntrakaiḥ ।।
nirgamaiḥsugavākṣaiśca viṭaṅkaiḥsphaṭikaprabhaiḥ ।। pūrṇacandranibhākārair aṇḍaiḥ śikharamaṇḍitaiḥ ।। nāṭyaśālaiḥ suśobhāḍhyair nṛttagītaravākulaiḥ ।। āsīnairudravṛndaiśca rudrakanyākadambakaiḥ ।।
dhūpitaṃ dhūpavartībhiḥ kuṅkumodakasecitam ।। tūryaśabdajayadhvānakāhalākūjitena ca ।। paṇavaistālavādyaiśca śaṅkhabherīraveṇa ca ।। karasphoṭamahāśabdaiḥ siṃhanādapraguñjitaiḥ ।।
vandināṃstotraśabdena sāmavedaraveṇa ca ।। vṛṣananditaśabdena gajavājiraveṇa ca ।। sarvasaṃpatkaraṃ śrīmacchaṅkarasya tu mandiram ।। gaṅgāyāsnapitonityaṃ divyavastrāmbaracchadaḥ ।।
saptasvarapramukhyaiśca sarasvatyā ca saṃstutaḥ ।। gaṅgātūttarikācchatre sarvādityāśca dīpakāḥ ।। kapilaḥ karkaṭaścaiva vimardaḥ kaṅkaṭastathā ।। aṣṭau te harayaḥproktās trinetrā bhūrivikramāḥ ।।
śaktirūpadharairmantrair yogaiśvaryasamanvitaiḥ ।। tatrabhadrāsane rudraḥ sthitaścandrārdhaśekharaḥ ।। tryakṣodaśabhujodevo jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitaḥ ।। baddhapadmāsanāsīnaḥ karpūrakṣodadhūsaraḥ ।।
śatapatrāṅkitaiścaiva hastapādaiḥ sukomalaiḥ ।। suśliṣṭajānugulphaiśca pādaiścaiva samunnataiḥ ।। cāmaravyajanokṣepai rudrastrībhiḥ samantataḥ ।। jñānāmṛtasutṛptātmā yogaiśvaryapradāyakaḥ ।।
prahasansa ivābhāti nirmalajñānaraśmibhiḥ ।। sarvasaukhyapradātā ca rudramātṛgaṇāvṛtaḥ ।। pūjitā yoginīvṛndaiḥ sādhakaiḥ surakinnaraiḥ ।। yogasiddhipradā nityaṃ mokṣābhyudayadāyikā ।।
śaktiścāpararūpeṇa śaktimāṃśca harastathā ।। dīkṣājñānavihīnā ye liṅgārādhanatatparāḥ ।। jarāmaraṇanirmuktā vyādhiśokavivarjitāḥ ।। śivaṃyānti tataścordhvaṃ śrīkaṇṭhenasamīkṣitāḥ ।।
uttarottaravṛddhyā ca bhuvanaṃ bhuvanaṃsthitam ।। daṇḍapāṇeḥ puraṃjñeyaṃ nānārudragaṇāvṛtam ।। daṇḍaḥ pāṇitalenaiva dhṛtoyena śivecchayā ।। vidhinārādhitaścaiva anudhyānācchivecchayā ।।
śarvorudrastathā bhīmo bhava ugrastathaiva ca ।। brahmalokesthitobrahmā viṣṇurvai vaiṣṇave pure ।। kālāgner daṇḍapāṇyantam aṣṭānavatikoṭayaḥ ।। kaṭāhastu adhaścordhvaṃ brahmāṇḍasya varānane ।।
pañcāśatkoṭayaścordhvaṃ bhūpṛṣṭhāttu varānane ।। evaṃ koṭiśataṃ jñeyaṃ pārthivaṃ tattvamucyate ।। vajrasārādhikasāraṃ durbhedyaṃ tridaśairapi ।। śatarudrānato vakṣye samāsena kṛśodari ।।
pūrvādikramayogena kathayāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।। vibhūtiravyayaḥ śāstā pinākī tridaśādhipaḥ ।। vicarantimahādevā indreṇa ca supūjitāḥ ।। jvalanodahanobabhrur bhasmāntakakṣayāntakau ।।
vicarantimahādevā agnirājasupūjitāḥ ।। saṃyoktā ca viyoktā ca dharmo dharmapatistathā ।। vicarantimahādevā yamarājasupūjitāḥ ।। ūrdhvakeśovirūpākṣo dhūmalohitadaṃṣṭrakau ।।
vicarantimahādevā nairṛtendrasupūjitāḥ ।। śveto atha jayabhadraśca dīrghabāhurjalāntakaḥ ।। vāruṇaṃbalamākramya prabhuśaktisamanvitāḥ ।। śīghrolaghurvāyuvegaḥ sūkṣmastīkṣṇo bhayānakaḥ ।।
vāyostu balamākramya prabhuśaktisamanvitāḥ ।। nidhīśorūpavāndhanyaḥ sau,yadeho jaṭādharaḥ ।। saumyasya balamākramya prabhuśaktisamanvitāḥ ।। vidyādhipo atha sarvajño jñānadṛgvedapāragaḥ ।।
īśānānumatā devāś ceṣṭante surapūjitāḥ ।। vṛṣovṛṣadharo anantaḥ krodhano mārutāhvayaḥ ।। viṣṇostubalamākramya prabhuśaktisamanvitāḥ ।। śaṃbhurvibhurgaṇādhyakṣas tryakṣaśca tridaśeśvaraḥ ।।
brahmaṇobalamākramya prabhuśaktisamanvitāḥ ।। ekaikasya sahasraṃ tu parivāro abhidhīyate ।। asaṃkhyātāḥ sahasrāṇi ye ca ūrdhvādidiggatāḥ ।। pūrvādidaśadigrudrāḥ sthitā daśa daśaiva tu ।।
sthito vai pūrvato aṇḍasya śveto vai nāma nāmataḥ ।। dīptimadbhirmahātīvrair mayūkhairiva bhāskaraḥ ।। so api vidyutprabhairudra śataistu parivāritaḥ ।। śatarudrairvṛto devi tiṣṭhatyamitavikramaiḥ ।।
saṃtiṣṭhate mahātejā dvitīya iva bhāskaraḥ ।। śatarudrairvṛtaḥ so api tiṣṭhatyamitavikramaḥ ।। śatena ca vṛtaḥ śrīmāṃs tiṣṭhatyatra mahābalaḥ ।। mahāvīryabalopetas tiṣṭhatyatra mahābalaḥ ।।
vidyādharo nāma rudra aiśānyāṃ vai pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। mahāvīryabalopetas tiṣṭhate anantavikramaḥ ।। samāvṛto rudraśataiḥ sthitaistvatra varānane ।। vīrabhadro vṛtorudrair uparyaṇḍasya saṃsthitaḥ ।।
evaṃte atramahātmāna ekaikaṃ tu śatena ca ।। eṣāmaparisaṃkhyeyaḥ parivāro mahātmanām ।। kadambakusumaṃyadvat kesaraiḥ parivāritam ।। gṛhaiḥ satoraṇāṭṭālair nānāratnavicitritaiḥ ।।
divyanārībhirākīrṇaṃ sarvakāmasamanvitam ।। janmavyādhijarāmṛtyumahodadhipariplutam ।। paśujñānaparikrāntaṃ gatitrayasamākulam ।। parāparavibhāgaṃ tu naivajānanti mohitāḥ ।।
īśamāyāsamāviṣṭasyātmavargasya bhūtaye ।। uttarottarayogena daśadhā saṃsthitāni tu ।। ūrdhvaṃ sahasradhā jñeyaṃ pradhānaṃ varavarṇini ।। tadūrdhvaṃ daśalakṣāṇi kalā yāvattu suvrate ।।
daśakoṭiguṇā vidyā māyāṃvyāpya vyavasthitā ।। sādākhyaṃ koṭisāhasraṃ bindunādaṃ tadūrdhvataḥ ।। vyāpinī sarvamadhvānaṃ vyāpyadevi vyavasthitā ।। bhuvanāni pravakṣyāmi aptattvādāvanukramāt ।।
yanna dṛṣṭaṃ paśujñānaiḥ kupathabhrāntadṛṣṭibhiḥ ।। svabhāvavādibhirnāpi na ca karmapravādibhiḥ ।। na bhūtavādibhiścaiva nāpi syāllokikairapi ।। na ca vaiśeṣikairvāapi ṣaṭpadārthaparāyaṇaiḥ ।।
nāpyekajanmavādaiśca nacāpyekatvavādibhiḥ ।। ityevaṃvādināṃ teṣāṃ vādānāṃ tu śatatrayam ।। ajñānatimirādhānām unmīlanakṛduttamam ।। mahāmohatamo andhānāṃ tamonudamidaṃ param ।।
jñānāmṛtamidaṃ divyaṃ nanabhuvanavistaram ।। ananto bhuvanavrātas tv avyucchedādvyavasthitaḥ ।। mīnaśaṃkhakulāyābhaṃ dāṣimībījavatsthitam ।। mahāsenāvāsakavad vane tarusamūhavat ।।
nānākārāṇi citrāṇi sarvaratnamayāni ca ।। puruṣākṛtīni cānyāni nandyāvartākṛtīni ca ।। śarāvākṛtīni cānyāni jvālārūpākṛtīni ca ।। murajākṛtīni cānyāni tryaśrākṛtipurāṇi ca ।।
sahasraśṛṅgāvartāni tathānyāni varānane ।। vṛttāni caturaśrāṇi trikoṇānyaparāṇi ca ।। bherinādasvarāḍhyāni divyagītadhvanīni ca ।। nānāvāditraghoṣāṇi bhuvanāni ca sarvadā ।।
candrakāntasavarṇāni muktādāmanibhāni ca ।। indragopakavarṇāni indranīlanibhāni ca ।। bālādityasavarṇāni padmagarbhanibhāni ca ।। madhyāhnārkasavarṇāni sūryakoṭinibhāni ca ।।
śakracāpasavarṇāni gokṣīradhavalāni ca ।। taptahemasavarṇāni nirdhūmāgninibhāni ca ।। nānāvarṇāni cānyāni nānārūpākṛtīni ca ।। aprameyamasaṃkhyeyam agamyaṃ sarvavādinām ।।
nacāpi bhāvo bhavati dīkṣāmaprāpya dehinām ।। śivecchayā prapadyeta dīkṣāṃ jñānamayīṃ śubhām ।। nānyathā mokṣamāyāti api jñānaśatairapi ।। sa eva mokṣaṃ vrajati śivaḥ sarvamaheśvaraḥ ।।
saṃsārārṇavamagnānāṃ naurivottāraṇaṃ param ।। anantaṃ pāramakṣobhyaṃ subodhaṃ parameśvaram ।। vakṣye jñānāmṛtamidaṃ śṛṇuṣvaikamanāḥ priye ।। ekādaśānāṃ rudrāṇāṃ yugāntāgnisamatviṣām ।।
indranīlamayaṃ divyaṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam ।। vasatīndīvaraśyāmā snigdhakaṅkuṣṭasaprabhā ।। paurṇamāsyāṃ yathā sandhyā candrarkābhyāṃ virājate ।। asitāñjanaśailābhyāṃ madhye srotovahā yathā ।।
sarvavajramaye divye divyaratnavibhūṣite ।। śukle himavataḥ śṛṅge nīlamegha iva sthitā ।। pītamālyāṃśukavatī śarvarīvāruṇodaye ।। udayastha ivādityo raśmijālavibhūṣitaḥ ।।
kṛṣṇameghoparisthena candreṇeva vibhāvarī ।। āvṛtā candralekheva nakṣatraistu nabhastale ।। priyaṅgukalikāśyāmāś candragauryaḥ sayauvanāḥ ।। hāvabhāvavidhijñāstu nṛttagītaviśāradāḥ ।।
upāsīnāstu tāṃ devīṃ ramante tatra yoṣitaḥ ।। yā durgeti smṛtā loke brahmāṇḍodaravartinī ।। avatāritā vadhārtāya mahiṣasya mahātmanaḥ ।। śuṣkaparṇamiva kṣiptaḥ bhagavatyā vināśitaḥ ।।
sā devī sarvadevīnāṃ nāmarūpaiśca tiṣṭhati ।। acintyā cāprameyā ca anyatra paripaṭhyate ।। bhaginītvena cāyāti nāmarūpaviparyayaiḥ ।। rakṣaṇārthaṃ hi lokānāṃ māteva hitakāriṇī ।।
tadbhaktāstatra gacchanti tasyā maṇḍaladīkṣitāḥ ।। na dānairvividhaiścāpi śakyaṃ prāptuṃ varānane ।। dīkṣāṃ prāpya prāpnuvanti maṇḍalaṃ cakravartinām ।। sā muktidīkṣā paramā vidhivatparikīrtitā ।।
tāvatīṃ gatimāpnoti bhuvane atra varānane ।। kathayiṣyāmi te sarvaṃ śṛṇuṣvaikamanāḥ priye ।। koṭimātreṇa deveśi yugāntāgnisamaprabhaḥ ।। śatabāhurmahātejā divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।।
śikhikaṇṭhanibhaḥ kiñcit kiñcidāpāṇḍulohitaḥ ।। indranīlanibhaḥ kiñcit kiñcidbhṛṅganibhākṛtiḥ ।। yutaṃ koṭisahasreṇa rudrāṇāṃ ca mahātmanām ।। indranīlanibhaṃ divyaṃ sarvavajranibhaṃ mahat ।।
antarbhuvanasaṃghātair anyaiśca parivāritam ।। rudrairdivyairmahāvīryaiḥ samantātparivāritam ।। paṇavairveṇuvīṇābhir bherījhallari gomukhaiḥ ।। mṛddalaistaṭṭarībhiśca tālakairmurajaistathā ।।
vāditrairvalgitaistālai roṭanairmukhamṛddalaiḥ ।। dhyāyādbhiśca japadbhiśca dhāvadbhiśceṣṭitaistathā ।। nānārutavilāsaiśca vikurvadbhirmahātmabhiḥ ।। gajavaktraiḥ siṃhavaktrair aśvavaktraiḥ śubhānanaiḥ ।।
vyāghravānaravakaiś ca bhagavānparyupāsyate ।। āsanaṃ tasya devasya sarvavajramayaṃ mahat ।। rājate atrāṣṭabhiḥ siṃhair vṛtaṃ bhīmaparākramaiḥ ।। jale marutsvathāgnau vā śiraśchedena vā mṛtāḥ ।।
bhuvanasyāsya deveśi hy uparyāvaraṇaṃ mahat ।। vitānamiva tadbhadram antare samavasthitam ।। tatra yojanakoṭirvai viṣkambhādūrdhvamucyate ।। āvṛtaṃ tena tatsarvaṃ mahāmbhodhivisāriṇā ।।
vīrabhadraniketaśca bhadrakālyālayastathā ।। nānārudragaṇairdivyair nirantaramalaṃkṛtam ।। ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dharitryā bhuvanaṃ mahat ।। hairaṇyamatulaṃ prāptā ādhāraṃ yatra saṃsthitā ।।
āvṛtaṃ bhūtasaṃghātair ācāryaistatparāyaṇaiḥ ।। antarbhuvanasaṃghātai rudrāṇāṃ parivāritam ।। raktotpalanibho divya aśokastabakacchaviḥ ।। tasya madhye bhagavatī dharitrī lokadhāriṇī ।।
candrārkamaṇḍalākārakapolatalabhūṣitā ।। śatayojanavistīrṇe kūrmapṛṣṭhe vyavasthitā ।। rūpayauvanasaṃpannā nṛttagītaviśāradāḥ ।। triṃśatkoṭyastu tāsāṃ vai divyābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।।
taptajāmbūnadanibhā divyābharaṇaśobhitāḥ ।। puraḥsthito mahātejā yo asau merurmahāgiriḥ ।। nīlotpaladalaśyāmo nīlajīmūtasaṃnibhaḥ ।। atikāntena rūpeṇa kaiṭabhāririvāparaḥ ।।
tasyottare candranibho nānālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ ।। tasyottareṇa sūryābho mukuṭādivibhūṣitaḥ ।। atikāntena rūpeṇa kusumāstra ivāparaḥ ।। candrāvadātadīptaujā divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।।
taptahemapratīkāśo divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। pītāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān pītamālyānulepanaḥ ।। rājate bhagavān śailaḥ sandhyāvṛta ivāṃśumān ।। śuklāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān divyakuṇḍalabhūṣitaḥ ।।
himavāniti vikhyāto dvitīya iva bhāskaraḥ ।। raktāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān astādristha ivāṃśumān ।। kirīṭī kuṇḍalī śrīmān mālyavānnāma parvataḥ ।। lokālokāvasānaiśca tathānyaiḥ kulaparvataiḥ ।।
dhāraṇāṃ gandhatanmātre prāṇāṃstyaktvā tu yoginaḥ ।। ataḥ parataraṃ devi sāmudraṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat ।। nīlotpalasamacchāyaṃ sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalam ।। śatayojanasāhasraṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam ।।
kirīṭī kuṇḍalī sragvī divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। taṃ tu devaṃ mahātmānaṃ parivārya samantataḥ ।। śuklāmbaradharā devī śuklagandhānulepanā ।। śuklainaivātapatreṇa dhriyamāṇena mūrdhani ।।
nīlāmbaradharā devī nīlagandhānulepanā ।। evamādyā mahānadyaḥ parivārya mahādyutim ।। upāsate sadā bhaktyā vāruṇīṃ paramāṃ tanum ।। rasatanmātra atraiva kṛtvā samyaktu dhāraṇām ।।
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bhuvanaṃ varavarṇini ।। vimānaśatasaṃghātair nirantaramavasthitaiḥ ।। sarobhirmānasairdivyair dīrghikābhiśca śobhitam ।। vaidūryanālaiḥ kamalair divyagandhasugandhibhiḥ ।।
saṃśobhitaṃ vicitraistair vikacairvajrakesaraiḥ ।। nānākāmapradairvṛkṣaiḥ samantātsamalaṅkṛtam ।। mānasībhiśca nārībhir divyayauvanakāntibhiḥ ।। vicitrairmaṇipadmaiśca sitapatraiśca suvrate ।।
gāyadbhiścātha nṛtyadbhir divyastraiṇaiḥ samākulam ।। śaradindunibhaṃ divyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ raśmisaṃkulam ।। candrakoṭisahasrāṇāṃ yā kāntimativartate ।। nirvāṇamiva yā śāntā sarvānandamanoharā ।।
śatayojanavistīrṇe uditādityasaprabhe ।। koṭipatre mahādivye gandhapuṣpaguṇānvite ।। upaviṣṭātra sā nityaṃ vibhūtyā parayā yutā ।। vahantī sā tu śuśubhe jyotsneva tripathāpatham ।।
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśe dhārayantī ca kuṇḍale ।। hemābhā pītavasanā mahāhāravibhūṣitā ।। upagītā ca gandharvair mānasai rudrasambhavaiḥ ।। yā prāptā tapasārādhya viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā ।।
ardhena sā bhagavatī viṣṇoraṅge pratiṣṭhātā ।। tadardhena punardevi pārthiveṣu vyavasthitā ।। svarūpā kāmarūpā ca dvidhā sā parikīrtitā ।। rudrakrīḍāvatāreṣu prayāgādiṣu suvrate ।।
satsvanyeṣvapi bhāgeṣu tv iyaṃ sā gaditā gatiḥ ।। bhūtvā tu sāṣṭadhā divyā deveṣvapi ca tiṣṭhati ।। yadarthaṃ tārakādyaiśca saṃgrāmastridaśeśvaraiḥ ।। asaṅkhyeyāśca saṃgrāmāḥ kṛtā vai cakravartibhiḥ ।।
śrīpuraṃ tu samākhyātaṃ yathāvacca varānane ।। sārasvatamiti khyātaṃ gāndharvamiti ca smṛtam ।। yojanānāṃ samākhyātaṃ pramāṇena samantataḥ ।। vimānairvividhākārair nānāratnamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।
nṛtyadbhiśca tathānyaiśca gaṇaiḥ pārśvagataistathā ।। tasya madhye tu deveśi śaraccandranibhaṃ śubham ।। tasya madhye bhagavatī sthitā sākṣātsarasvatī ।। pītāmbaradharā devī padmapatrāyatekṣaṇā ।।
hemapaṭṭaparīdhānā divyakuṇḍaladhāriṇī ।। sphuranmayūkhasaṃghātakuṇḍaladvayamaṇḍitā ।। tānamūrdhāruhā devī mūrcchanāṅgaruhodvahā ।। aṅgulyaḥ sandhayaścaiva lakṣaṇāni varānane ।।
sthitā sthitirivābhāti sarvasya jagataḥ śubhā ।। hāhā hūhūścitrarathas tumbururnāradastathā ।। saṃyojya manasātmānaṃ tyaktvā karmaphalaspṛhām ।। ye ca vāgdhāraṇāṃ dhyātvā prāṇānmuñcanti dehinaḥ ।।
eṣā sarasvatī devī mūrtirvai pārameśvarī ।। brahmaloke ca sā devī pādenaikena tiṣṭhati ।। siddheṣu ca tadardhena kinnareṣu tadardhataḥ ।। piśāceṣu tadardhena sā vai tiṣṭhati bhāgaśaḥ ।।
taistu taptvā tapo ghoram ārādhya ca pinākinam ।। svarāṃstu smaratastasya kalpādau brahmaṇaḥ purā ।। sā sthitā sarvaśāstreṣu kavīnāṃ kāvyamāsthitā ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ medhābudhivivardhinī ।।
merorvāyavyadigbhāge puraṃ tasyāḥ prakīrtitam ।। sārasvataṃ tu bhuvanaṃ kīrtitaṃ paramā tanuḥ ।। amareśaṃ prabhāsaṃ ca puṣkaraṃ naimiṣaṃ tathā ।। guhyāṣṭakamiti khyātaṃ jalāvaraṇagaṃ priye ।।
agnestu bhuvanaṃ tatra kathayāmi varānane ।। utphullakiṃśukacchāyaṃ japākusumasaṃnibham ।। parimaṇḍalamāgneyaṃ tejomaṇḍalamucyate ।। yo avatīryāṇḍamadhye tu sthito nityaṃ tridhā tridhā ।।
sthito jihvāsvarūpeṇa svayaṃbhūrnīlalohitaḥ ।। tasya rūpaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvāvahitā priye ।। raktāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān raktamālyānulepanaḥ ।। mahāhāreṇa dīptena uraḥsthena virājate ।।
sarvavajramaye pīṭhe upaviṣṭaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।। daśakoṭisahasrāṇi āgneyāstu gaṇeśvarāḥ ।। hitāya sarvalokānāṃ rudrā vai sūryavarcasaḥ ।। nāryaśca vividhā divyā divyagītavicakṣaṇāḥ ।।
sa vai śivāgniḥ paṭhitaḥ sarvahomeśvaraḥ paraḥ ।। tamagnimaiśvaraṃ yānti kṛtvāgneyīṃ tu dhāraṇām ।। sa tejastejasāṃ yoniḥ tasmājjajñe divākaraḥ ।। bhinnaśca janmabhedaiśca pañcāśadbhiśca bhūtale ।।
bhuvanādhipāṃśca bhuvane kathayāmi tvataḥ param ।। mahākālaṃ madhyamaṃ ca kedāraṃ bhairavaṃ tathā ।। athordhve vāyvāvaraṇaṃ tatrastho vāyuravyayaḥ ।। śaṅkhagokṣiradhavalaṃ śaratkundendusaprabham ।।
madhye tu maṇḍalaṃ divyaṃ śaraccandrasamaprabham ।। tasya madhye tu deveśi vāyostu paramā tanuḥ ।। nānābharaṇacitrāṅgaś citramālyānulepanaḥ ।। mārutā nāma vai devāḥ śatakoṭyo mahābalāḥ ।।
yo vyāpayeccharīrāṇi ekadhā pañcadhā vibhuḥ ।। svamaṇḍalasya sā divyair vibhātyekā parā tanuḥ ।। dhyātvā tyaktvā tu vai prāṇān kṛtvā tasminstu dhāraṇām ।। iti prāṇasya bhuvanam ākhyātaṃ tava suvrate ।।
gayāṃ caiva kurukṣetraṃ nākalaṃ kanakhalaṃ tathā ।। guhyādguhyataraṃ hy etad veditavyaṃ prayatnataḥ ।। sūkṣmarūpo avyayo nityo madhyadeśe vyavasthitaḥ ।। atrākāśe pravakṣyāmi ye rudrāḥ saṃvyavasthitāḥ ।।
gokīrṇaṃ bhadrakarṇaṃ ca svarṇākṣaṃ sthāṇumaṣṭamam ।। asya bāhye ahaṃkāraḥ tatra rudrānnibodha me ।। kālañjaraṃ śaṅkukarṇaṃ sthūleśvarasthaleśvarau ।। madhyadeśesthito rudras tv ahaṃkāreśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।।
pañcāṣṭakeṣu ye varṇāḥ samāsātkathitāstava ।। pītāḥ śuklāśca vijñeyāḥ adhastu dhūmravarcasaḥ ।। candrārdhamaulayaḥ sarve rudrāṇībhiḥ samanvitāḥ ।। śatarudrabhuvanāni bhogaiśvaryayutāni ca ।।
ākāśāvaraṇādūrdhvam ahaṃkārādadhaḥ priye ।। ādau tu gandhatanmātraṃ vistīrṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ mahat ।। śuklaraktasitāpītaharitaṃ sphaṭikaprabham ।। śarvo hyadhipatistatra eka eva varānane ।।
tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ rasatanmātramaṇḍalam ।। bhavo hyadhipatistatra eka eva varānane ।। tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ rūpatanmātramaṇḍalam ।। rudraḥ paśupatistatra eka evāvatiṣṭhate ।।
tattejaḥ sarvalokānāṃ vyāpakaṃ parameśvari ।। sandhyāruṇasamacchāyaṃ vāyavyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ priye ।। tatraiva maṇḍale devi tv īśānaḥ saṃvyavasthitaḥ ।। tasmātprāṇādayaḥ pañca vāyostadvyāpakaḥ paraḥ ।।
tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ śabdatanmātramaṇḍalam ।। vitānasadṛśākāraṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam ।। tasmānnabho viniṣkrāntaṃ bhīmecchācoditaṃ mahat ।। tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ sūryamaṇḍalamucyate ।।
vitānavadraśmidīptaṃ samantātparimaṇḍalam ।। sūryāstasmādviniṣkrāntāḥ kalpe kalpe varānane ।। candrakoṭisahasrāṇāṃ tejasā tulyamaṇḍalam ।। tasmāccandrādime candrā mahādevena coditāḥ ।।
tasmāttu maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ vedamaṇḍalamucyate ।। vitānavatsthitaṃ divyam ugreśasamadhiṣṭhitam ।। yajamānasahasrāṇi kalpe kalpe sthitāni hi ।। vedayajñāśca vividhā brahmaṇo anantavartmanaḥ ।।
tapodānādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ vāmaśaktyā niyantritāḥ ।। aparā brahmaṇo aṇḍaṃ vai vyāpya sarvaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ।। śuklaraktāsitaṃ pītaṃ haritaṃ cāpi varṇataḥ ।। karmadevāḥ pravartante tasmādvai sarvadehinām ।।
ebhyaḥ prakāśakaṃ nāma parataḥ sūryasaṃnibham ।। śrotraṃ tvakcakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā ca yathākramam ।। svākyādhipatayo nityaṃ teṣveva praticodakāḥ ।। vistārātpariṇāhācca sarvato raśmimaṇḍalam ।।
śabdaḥ sparśastathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaśca pañcamaḥ ।। tasmānmano viniṣkrāntaṃ raśmibhirdarśapañcabhiḥ ।। tasyādhipo mahātejāś candramāḥ saumyatejasā ।। japākusumasaṃkāśam aruṇādityasaṃnibham ।।
tasmāttu maṇḍalāddevi sandhyāruṇasamadyutiḥ ।। antaḥkaraṇamātmasthaṃ yenedaṃ raṃjitaṃ jagat ।। tasyādhidevo rudro vai yenāyaṃ preryate sadā ।। ahaṃkārādathordhvaṃ tu buddhyāvaraṇamucyate ।।
aṣṭānāṃ devayonīnām atraiva bhuvanaṃ śṛṇu ।। mānasībhistu tatstrībhir muditābhiḥ samākulam ।। daśakoṭisahasrāṇi teṣāṃ tatra nivāsinām ।। sandhyāruṇasamacchāyo bandhūkakusumākṛtiḥ ।।
kirīṭī cāṅgadī maulī hemacīnāmbaraḥ śubhaḥ ।। nānārūpadharairdivyair divyābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ ।। parivṛto mahātejā gaṇairiva mahāgaṇaḥ ।। kokilākaṇṭhasadṛśaṃ nīlajīmutasaṃnibham ।।
karālo rākṣaseśo vai jātyañjananibho mahān ।। jātyañjananibhaḥ śrīmān dāvāgniriva parvate ।। bhṛṅgajīmūtavarṇābhā vasantyatra mahāprabhāḥ ।। jāmbūnadamayaṃ sarvaṃ divyaratnasamujjvalam ।।
tasmiṃstu bhuvane bhadre subhadro nāma yakṣarāṭ ।। śatakoṭisahasraistu yakṣairamitavikramaiḥ ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi gāndharvaṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat ।। tasmiṃstu bhuvane divye surūpo nāma vai priye ।।
taptajāmbūnadanibhas taruṇādityasaprabhaḥ ।। daśakoṭisahasraistu gandharvaiḥ parivāritaḥ ।। svakāntā nāma gandharvāś citramālyānulepanāḥ ।। tasmātparataraṃ vakṣye sthānam aindraṃ ca pārvati ।।
śaṅkhagokṣīradhavalaṃ śaratkundendusannibham ।। vibhūtirnāma bhagavān mahendro bhuvaneśvaraḥ ।। śuklāmbaradharaḥ śrīmāñc chuklamālyānulepanaḥ ।। hārakeyūravāñchvetaḥ śvetoṣṇīṣavibhūṣitaḥ ।।
kirīṭinaḥ kuṇḍalino divyamālyavibhūṣitāḥ ।। tairāvṛto mahātejā nakṣatrairiva candramāḥ ।। śuklābhrakanibhaṃ dīptaṃ muktāhārasuvarcasam ।। śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaḥ śrīmāñcchuklāmbarodvahaḥ ।।
divyagandhānuliptāṅgo divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। divyāḥ saumyāstu te jñeyāḥ somatejaḥ samudbhavāḥ ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ tu deveśi prājeśāṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat ।। viśvarūpo viśvavarṇo viśvālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ ।।
daśakoṭisahasrāṇi viśvānāṃ bhūritejasām ।। brāhmaṃ caivamato jñeyaṃ śaṅkhagokṣīrasannibham ।। śuklāmbaradharaḥ śrīmāñ chuklamālyānulepanaḥ ।। daśakoṭisahasraistu candrabimbasamaprabhaiḥ ।।
paiśācaṃ rākṣāsaṃ yākṣaṃ gāndharvaṃ tvaindrameva ca ।। etāni surayonīnāṃ sthānānyeva purāṇi tu ।। parameśaniyogācca codyamānāśca māyayā ।। vyajyante te ca sargādau nāmarūpairanekadhā ।।
puryaṣṭakendriyaiḥ sārdham ātmā mantrairviśodhayet ।। viśodhyaivaṃ prayatnena krodhāṣṭakamataḥ param ।। mṛtyuhantā ca raktākṣo mahākrodhaśca durjayaḥ ।। ekaikasya parīvāraḥ koṭirdaśasahasrakam ।।
balādhyakṣo gaṇādhyakṣas tridaśastripurāntakaḥ ।। sahasraiḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ parivāro abhidhīyate ।। kūrmākārāṇi citrāṇi teṣāṃ vai bhuvanāni tu ।। akṛtaṃ ca kṛtaṃ caiva raibhavaṃ brāhmameva ca ।।
krīḍanti yoginastatra bhuvanaiḥ sphaṭikaprabhaiḥ ।। umā tvameyā viśvasya viśvayoniḥ svayambhavā ।। mahāpīṭhe maṇimaye siṃhāṣṭakayute śubhe ।। divyakuṇḍalinī devī mahāhāravibhūṣitā ।।
jayā ca padmagarbhābhā sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitā ।। sarvābharaṇacitrāṅgī sunandā ca manoharā ।। triṃśatkoṭisahasrāṇi triṃśatkoṭiśatāni ca ।। vimānakoṭirekā ca rudrāṇāṃ bhūritejasām ।।
upāsate tu tāṃ devīṃ mātaraṃ tanayā iva ।। anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ prādurbhūtā sanātanī ।। tṛtīye śāmbhavī nāma caturthe viśvarūpiṇī ।। vibhūtiḥ saptame kalpe subhūtiścāṣṭame tathā ।।
ekādaśe varārohā dvādaśe ca sumaṅgalā ।। kalpe caturdaśe caiva anantā nāma kīrtitā ।। sahasradhārā saptadaśe satī cāṣṭadaśe purā ।। avamānācca dakṣasya svāṃ tanuṃ tvajahāḥ purā ।।
punarhimavatārādhya duhitā tvātmanaḥ kṛtā ।। māṃ bhartāraṃ punaḥ prāpya jātāsyaṅgaruhā priye ।। tvaṃ tanurvāmabhāgasya matto naiva viyujyase ।। ekānaṃśāparā mūrtiḥ satīśānādviniḥsṛtā ।।
mahiṣasya vadhārthāya utpannā kṛṣṇapiṅgalā ।। manuṣyāṇāṃ tu bhaktānāṃ varadā bhaktavatsalā ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhuvanaṃ varavarṇini ।। kailāsaśikharākāraṃ śuddhasphaṭikasaprabham ।।
tasmiṃstu bhuvane divye sūryakoṭisamadyutiḥ ।। umāpatirjagannāthaḥ sarvānugrahakṛdvaraḥ ।। śatayojanavistīrṇe nānāratnavibhūṣite ।। āsane parame divye ratnapadmavicitrite ।।
hemacīnāmbaradharo hārakeyūrabhūṣitaḥ ।। sphuranmayūkhasaṃghāte kuṇḍale raśmisaṃkule ।। dedīpyamānamatyugraṃ kailāsaśikharopamam ।। gāṅgo himavataḥ śṛṅgāt patito nirjharo yathā ।।
śūlibhirjaṭibhistryakṣair divyābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ ।। divyābhirmānasībhiśca nārībhiḥ parivāritaḥ ।। mātaraḥ sapta rūpiṇyo nānālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ ।। brāhmī kamalapatrābhā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā ।।
śaṅkhagokṣīrasaṃkāśā tv aiśānyāṃ tu varānane ।। kaumārī padmagarbhābhā hārakeyūrabhūṣitā ।। snigdhanīlotpalanibhā hārakuṇḍalamaṇḍaitā ।। vaiṣṇavīti ca vikhyātā śivena paramātmanā ।।
vāruṇyāṃ diśi deveśi vārāhī paryupasthitā ।। aindryāṃ diśi ca sā devī indrāṇī paryupasthitā ।। nairṛtyāṃ diśi cāmuṇḍā upāste parameśvaram ।। aṃśena mānuṣaṃ lokaṃ brahmaṇā cāvatāritāḥ ।।
tapastaptvā mahāghoraṃ brahmaṇā lokadhāriṇā ।। svacchandāstu parāścānyāḥ paravyomni vyavasthitāḥ ।। umaiva saptadhā bhūtvā nāmarūpaviparyayaiḥ ।। āste paramayā lakṣmyā tatrastho dyotayañjagat ।।
śarvo bhavaśca bhagavān rudraḥ paśupatistathā ।। etābhiḥ kurute śarvo mūrtibhiḥ sṛṣṭimuttamām ।। somaśca yajamānaścety aṣṭau sṛṣṭiriyaṃ smṛtā ।। evamasminsthito devo brahmalokordhvatastathā ।।
śrīkaṇṭha iti nāmnā ca kailāsanilayastathā ।। ye tu māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ saguṇaṃ paryupāsate ।। dṛṣṭvā dehasthamātmānaṃ te atra yānti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। muktadvaitā yatātmānas tatra yānti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
vāmo bhīmastatheśaśca śivaḥ śarvastathaiva ca ।। īśānaścāpyumābhartā ajeśo ananta eva ca ।। sarve kuṅkumasaṃkāśāḥ sūryakoṭisamaprabhāḥ ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ vīrabhadro maṇḍalādhipatiḥ prabhuḥ ।।
ata ūrdhvaṃ mahādevi mahādevāṣṭakaṃ viduḥ ।। ekapiṅgekṣaṇeśānau bhuvaneśapuraḥsarāḥ ।। māyāñjanavinirmuktāḥ parameśānasaṃmatāḥ ।। athordhvaṃ guṇatattvaṃ tu tasmiṃścaiva vyavasthitam ।।
prathamā tamasaḥ paṅktir upariṣṭādvyavasthitā ।। śivaḥ prabhurvāmadevaś caṇḍaścaiva pratāpavān ।। mahendro dinakṛccaiva pratodo dakṣa eva ca ।। ambuhartā ca nārīśaḥ śveta ṛgveda eva ca ।।
virūpākṣastathā jyeṣṭho vipro nārāyaṇastathā ।। prathamā paṅktiruddiṣṭā rudrairdvātriṃśatā smṛtā ।। śuklo dāsaḥ sudāsaśca lokākṣaḥ sūrya eva ca ।। gautamaścaiva yogīśo dadhibāhustathāparaḥ ।।
guhyeśānaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca jaṭī mālī tathograkaḥ ।। aṭṭahāso dārukaśca lāṅgaliścātidaṇḍakaḥ ।। triṃśadrudrāḥ samākhyātā dvitīyā paṅktiruttamā ।। devo aruṇo dīrghabāhur atibhūtiśca sthāṇukaḥ ।।
cakrapāṇiśca kūrmākhyas tv ardhanārīśvarastathā ।। vauṣaṭkārastathā svāhā svadhā ca parikīrtitaḥ ।। ekaviṃśatirudrāstu paṅktireṣā tṛtīyakā ।। saṃsārapāśanirmuktāḥ mahāmohavivarjitāḥ ।।
sarvajñāḥ sarvagāścaiva lokānugrahakārakāḥ ।। buddheḥ prakṛtiparyante ye rudrāstānnibodha me ।। antarbhūtāḥ sthitāścānye ye te noktā varānane ।। tatra ye saṃsthitā rudrāḥ kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।।
pañcāntakaikavīrau ca śikhedasahiteśvarāḥ ।। guṇānāṃ yā parākāṣṭhā tatpradhānamihocyate ।। ambā ca salilā oghā vṛṣṭiḥ sārdhaṃ ca tārayā ।। uttamāmbhasikā caiva tuṣṭayo nava kīrtitāḥ ।।
pramoditā modamānā ramyakā ca tataḥ param ।। aṇimā laghimā caiva mahimā prāptireva ca ।। yatrakāmāvasāyitvam aṇimādyaṣṭakaṃ smṛtam ।। maskarī pūraṇaḥ kṛtsnaḥ kapilaḥ kāśa evaca ।।
kaśyapo nāsiketuśca gālavo bhautikastathā ।। vālmīkiśca guruśreṣṭhaḥ saparāśaragālavaḥ ।। maskaryādibhadantāntā dṛṣṭādṛṣṭasya vādinaḥ ।। jahnuśca tṛṇabinduśca munistārkṣyastathaiva ca ।।
agastyo vasubhaumaśca upādhyāyaśca kīrtitaḥ ।। sthūlaśirā bālakhilyo manuśceti prakīrtitaḥ ।। jahnvādicāruparyantā dvitīyā paṅktiriṣyate ।। kṛṣṇapiṅgeśarudraśca indrajidvṛṣakaḥ śivaḥ ।।
bhūteśvaraḥ kapālīśaḥ śaṅkaraśca tathaiva ca ।। mahākālaśca saṃvarto maṇḍalī tvekavīrakaḥ ।। jahnvādicāruparyantā ṛṣayaḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ ।। paṅktitrayaṃ samākhyātam ṛṣīṇāṃ guruśiṣyayoḥ ।।
iḍā ca candriṇī gaurī śāntiḥ śāntikarī tathā ।। athopariṣṭāddeveśi vigrahāṣṭakamucyate ।। jñānaṃ sādhyaṃ ca vikhyātaṃ sādhanaṃ kāraṇaṃ tathā ।। ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryamakalkatā ।।
evaṃ daśavidho dharmo yenokto dharmakṛnnaraḥ ।। raso gandhaśca rūpaṃ ca sparśaḥ śabdastathaivaca ।। vākpāṇipādaṃ pāyuśca upasthaḥ karmasaṃjñakam ।। buddhīndriyāṇi deveśi manaḥ ṣoḍaśakaṃ smṛtam ।।
dharmojñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ ca tataḥ param ।। ahaṃkāraṃ ca trividhaṃ pravakṣyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।। dīkṣākāle yathā śuddhis tathā caiṣāṃ nibodha me ।। śabdaḥ sparśastathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaśca pañcamaḥ ।।
kāmaḥ krodhaśca lobhaśca mohaḥ paiśunyameva ca ।। viṣādaśca bhayaṃ caiva mado harṣaṇameva ca ।। māyā mātsaryadharmaśca adharmaścāsvatantratā ।। devī nandimahākālau gaṇeśo vṛṣabhastathā ।।
anantastritanuḥ sūkṣmaḥ śrīkaṇṭhaśca śivottamaḥ ।। vidyeśvarātmakānpāśān dīkṣākāle viśodhayet ।। pauruṣeye tu śodhyāste tato mucyeta pudgalaḥ ।। vāmadevastathā śarvas tathā caiva bhavodbhavau ।।
suprabhedaśca daśamo niyatyāṃ śaṅkarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। niyatidalamahaṅkāra kesaraṃ buddhikarṇikam ।। śuddho buddhaḥ prabuddhaśca praśāntaḥ paramākṣaraḥ ।। daśaite tu śivā jñeyāḥ kālatattve varānane ।।
ekaikasya vinirdiṣṭā parivāro yaśasvini ।। kūrmākārāṇi sarveṣāṃ proktāni bhuvanāni tu ।। suhṛṣṭaḥ suprahṛṣṭaśca surūpo rūpavardhanaḥ ।। rāgatattve pravakṣyāmi ye anye rudrā vyavasthitāḥ ।।
medhātithiścchandakaśca dāhakaḥ śāstrakāriṇaḥ ।। vidyātattvamataścordhvaṃ tasminvai bhuvanaṃ śṛṇu ।। balavikaraṇaścaiva balapramathanastathā ।। kalātattve mahādevi mahādevatrayaṃ sthitam ।।
kalātattvaṃ samākhyātaṃ samāsena varānane ।। rudrakoṭisahasraistu samantātparivāritāḥ ।। rāge raktāstu vijñeyā jñānayogabalotkaṭāḥ ।। upariṣṭādbhavenmāyā kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।।
tatra rudrā mahābhāgā dvādaśaiva mahābalāḥ ।। daśeśānaśca deveśi trigalo gopatistathā ।। kṣemeśo brahmaṇaḥ svāmī vidyeśānastathaiva ca ।। ūrdhvamāyāpuṭasthāstu rudrā ete prakīrtitāḥ ।।
udbhavaṃ bhāvayitvā tu svecchayā kurute prabhuḥ ।। prathamena tu bhedena rudrā dvādaśa kīrtitāḥ ।। tathāhaṃ kathayiṣyāmi bhedatrayavibhāgaśaḥ ।। granthyūrdhve saṃsthito viśvas trikalaḥ kṣema eva ca ।।
adha ūrdhvamanantastu pāśāścaivātra saṃsthitāḥ ।। yonirvāgīśvarī caiva yasyāṃ jāto na jāyate ।। dhyānaṃ bhasmeśamevāhuḥ pramāṇāni tadūrdhvataḥ ।। hṛdayaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ caiva vyuhamākarṣameva ca ।।
ete parivṛtā devi rudrakoṭisahasrakaiḥ ।। nānānārīsahasraistu ramante patyuricchayā ।। aluptaśaktivibhavā māyātattvādhikāriṇaḥ ।। ataḥ paraṃ bhavenmāyā sarvajantuvimohinī ।।
idaṃ tattvamidaṃ neti vivadantīha vādinaḥ ।। gurudevāgniśāstrasya ye na bhaktā narādhamāḥ ।। bhramayatyeva tānmāyā hy amokṣe mokṣalipsayā ।। athopari mahāvidyā sarvavidyābhavodbhavā ।।
sā eva paramā devī vāgīśīti nigadyate ।। bhuvanāni pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। balavikaraṇī caiva balapramathanī tāthā ।। taptacāmīkarākārāḥ pañcavaktrāstrilocanāḥ ।।
sarvajñānugatāḥ sarvāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। pradhānāḥ sapta koṭyastu mantrāṇāṃ yā vyavasthitāḥ ।। padmākāreṣu divyeṣu krīḍanti bhuvaneṣu te ।। rūpiṇī mardinī jvālā saptasaṅkhyāstadīśvarāḥ ।।
bāhye tasyaiśvaraṃ tattvaṃ bhuvanānyatra me śṛṇu ।। sthitisaṃhārakartā vai mokṣaiśvaryapradāyakaḥ ।। tisraḥ koṭyo ardhakoṭiśca mantrāstasyāsane sthitāḥ ।। pañcavaktraḥ sutejasko daśabāhustrilocanaḥ ।।
divyāmbaradharo devo divyagandhānulepanaḥ ।। triśūlapāṇīndumaulir jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitaḥ ।। varadābhayahastaśca dhyeyo asāvīśayogibhiḥ ।। divyavastraparīdhānā divyamālyānulepanā ।।
muktāphalapratīkāśā pañcavaktrā trilocanā ।। prahasantīva sā bhāti maheśavadanekṣaṇāt ।। anantaścaiva sūkṣmaśca tathā caiva śivottamaḥ ।। śrīkaṇṭhaśca śikhaṇḍī ca jñeyā vidyeśvarāḥ kramāt ।।
dharmo jñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aisvaryaṃ ca caturthakam ।। vāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrī ca śaktayaḥ samudāhṛtāḥ ।। sarve sarvagatā mantrāḥ sarvajñāḥ sarvakāmadā ।। sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।।
śatapatrābjabhākāraiḥ śuddhahārenduraśmibhiḥ ।। īśvarānugatāḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti bhuvaneṣu te ।। vrataṃ pāśupataṃ divyaṃ ye caranti jitendriyāḥ ।। tatreśvarastu bhagavān devadevo nirañjanaḥ ।।
daśa pañca ca śodhyāni bhuvanānīśvare kramāt ।। śuddhāvaraṇamūrdhvaṃ tu tasmiñcchaktidvayaṃ smṛtam ।। bhāvasaṃjñāpyabhāvākhyā tasmiñcchaktidvaye smṛte ।। pramāṇāvaraṇe cordhve kathayāmi ca mānataḥ ।।
suśuddhāvaraṇaṃ cordhve tatra rudratrayaṃ viduḥ ।। śivāvaraṇamūrdhvaṃ tu tatraiko dhruvasaṃjñakaḥ ।। ekādaśaiva rudrāṃśca kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। janmamṛtyuharaścaiva praṇītaḥ sukhaduḥkhadaḥ ।।
punarūrdhve dhruvaṃ jñeyaṃ nirañjanapadaṃ śubham ।। icchāśaktyabhidhānāyāḥ antarbhūtāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। prītaḥ pramuditaścaiva pramodaśca pralambakaḥ ।। rudrāṣṭakaṃ samākhyātaṃ vijñeyaṃ prāgdiśaḥ kramāt ।।
prabhavaḥ samayaḥ kṣudro vimalaśca śivastathā ।। rudroṅkārastu pañcaite tālūrdhve tu vijānata ।। rudroṅkārāntamityetad dīkṣākāle viśodhayet ।। trinetrā varadāḥ sarve śuddhasāmarthyavigrahāḥ ।।
triśūlapāṇayaḥ sarve jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitāḥ ।। sārvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। saṃkriḍante puravaraiḥ śivecchāvidhicoditāḥ ।। suśivāvaraṇaṃ cordhve tasmiñjñeyaḥ sadāśivaḥ ।।
vaktrapañcakasaṃyukto daśabāhurmahābalaḥ ।। siṃhāsanopaviṣṭastu śvetapadmāsanasthitaḥ ।। daśabhiśca śivairyukto rudrāṣṭādaśakānvitaḥ ।। kṣapaṇaśca kṣayāntasthaḥ kaṇṭhyauṣṭhyaścāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
sakalādyairvṛto devaḥ oṃkāreśādibhiḥ kramāt ।। suśivaścaiva kāleśaḥ sūkṣmarūpaḥ sutejasaḥ ।। rudrāścāṣṭādaśa bahiḥ teṣāṃ nāmāni vai śṛṇu ।। rauravo mukuṭo visaraś candro bimbaḥ pragītavān ।।
paraśca kiraṇaścaiva pārameśvara eva ca ।। sarvakāraṇamadhyakṣaḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ ।। koṭayaḥ saptamantrāṇām āsane tasya saṃsthitāḥ ।। vāmādyairvibhupūrvaiśca pañcavaktraistrilocanaiḥ ।।
jñānaśaktiḥ kriyāśaktir vāme dakṣiṇataḥ sthite ।। utpattisthitisaṃhārāṃs tirobhāvamanugraham ।। tasyotsaṅgagatā sā tu nityaṃ caivātmavartinī ।। sa evāpararūpeṇa pañcamantramahātanuḥ ।।
śaktayastasya yāḥ proktāḥ tathā vai mantranāyakāḥ ।। tathā kharvanikharvaiśca pratirūpairmahābalaiḥ ।। sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ ।। candrakoṭiśataprakhyaiḥ prasravadbhirivāmṛtam ।।
puravaraiḥ sarvatobhadraiś candrakoṭisamaprabhaiḥ ।। adhikāraṃ prakurvanti sarvajñāmoghaśaktayaḥ ।। parapreryāḥ punarbhūyo na bhavanti kadācana ।। bindvāvaraṇamūrdhve ataś candrakoṭisamaprabham ।।
tatra padme sthito devaḥ śāntyatīto mahādyutiḥ ।। taḍitsahasrapuñjābhaḥ sphuranmāṇikyamaṇḍitaḥ ।। parivāraḥ smṛtastasya śāntyatītasya suvrate ।। pañcavaktrāḥ smṛtāḥ sarvā daśabāhvinduśekharāḥ ।।
ardhacandrastadūrdhve tu tadūrdhve tu nirodhikā ।। jyotsnā jyotsnāvatī kāntiḥ suprabhā vimalā śivā ।। rundhanī rodhanī raudrī jñānabodhā tamopahā ।। tasyāpyardhamardhacandras tv aṣṭāṃśaśca nirodhikā ।।
nirodhinīti vikhyātā tāṃ bhittvā tu varānane ।। tasyordhve tu smṛto nādaḥ sa kiñjalkarajaḥ prabhaḥ ।। teṣāṃ vai nāyikā vaksye bhuvane pañcasaṅkhyayā ।। ūrdhvagā tu samākhyātā kalātveṣā tu pañcamī ।।
candrārbudapratīkāśaḥ pañcavaktrastrilocanaḥ ।। indhikādivṛto devaḥ śūlapāṇirjaṭādharaḥ ।। tataḥ suṣumṇābhuvanaṃ suṣumṇā tatra saṃsthitā ।। daśabāhustrinetraśca śvetapadmoparisthitaḥ ।।
iḍā ca piṅgalā caiva vāmadakṣiṇataḥ sthite ।। śvetapadmakarā devī padmamālāvibhūṣitā ।। tasyotsaṅgagatā devī dhyātavyā sādhakādibhiḥ ।। nāḍyādhārastu nādo vai bhittvā sarvamidaṃ jagat ।।
nāḍyā brahmabile līnas tv avyaktadhvanirakṣaraḥ ।। evaṃ jñātvā varārohe śodhayettaṃ śivādhvare ।। tatra brahmā paro jñeyaḥ śaśāṅkaśatasaprabbhaḥ ।। triśūlapāṇirbhagavāñ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitaḥ ।।
dvāraṃ yā mokṣamārgasya rodhayitvā vyavasthitā ।। tāṃ bhittvātra varārohe gantavyamūrdhvataḥ priye ।। ādhāro bhuvanānāṃ sā tāṃ pravakṣyāmi suvrate ।। vyāpinī madhyato jñeyā śeṣāḥ pūrvāditaḥ kramāt ।।
śaktitattvaṃ samākhyātaṃ śivatattvaṃ śṛṇu priye ।। hemaprākāraracitaṃ ratnamāṇikyamaṇḍitam ।। bhuvanāni pravakṣyāmi tatraiva saṃsthitāni tu ।। kāraṇānāṃ pañcakaṃ ca śivatattve vyavasthitam ।।
tasya padmasya madhyastho devaścāyamanāśritaḥ ।। daśabāhurmahādīptaḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ ।। bhuktimuktipradātā ca sūryakoṭyarbudaprabhaḥ ।। divyāmbaradharo devo divyagandhānulepanaḥ ।।
ābaddhamaṇiparyaṅkaś cāmarotkṣepavījitaḥ ।। vyāpinī vyomarūpā cānantānāthātvanāśritā ।। trinetrāḥ śūlahastāśca kāraṇaiśca samanvitāḥ ।। anāśrito madhyagastu saṃsthitaḥ prabhuravyayaḥ ।।
evaṃ vai śivatattvaṃ tu kathitaṃ tava sundari ।। samanā nāma sā jñeyā manaścordhvaṃ na jāyate ।। sarveṣāṃ kāraṇānāṃ ca kartṛbhūtā vyavasthitā ।। tatrāruḍhastu kurute śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।।
hetukartā maheśānaḥ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam ।। tayādhitiṣṭheddeveśo hy adhaḥkāraṇapañcakam ।। sa vai prerayate bhūyas tv anāthaṃ tu jagatpatim ।। vyomavyāpī mahādevo vyāpinaṃ bodhayetprabhum ।।
karmarūpā sthitā māyā yadadhaḥ śaktikuṇḍalī ।। yatsadāśivaparyantaṃ pārthivādyaṃ ca suvrate ।। yā sā śaktiḥ purā proktā samanā tvadhvamūrdhani ।। dhyātvā caitāṃ samāvāhya sthāpayettu vidhānavit ।।
sthāpanaṃ pūjanaṃ caiva paśoryāgaṃ tathaiva ca ।। yogaṃ bhogaṃ layaṃ caiva niṣkṛtiṃ tadanantaram ।। bhuvanānāṃ yathāyogaṃ homaṃ kṛtvā varānane ।। viśleṣapāśacchedau ca kṛtvā pūrṇāṃ tu pātayet ।।
śikhāṃ cchitvā samarpyaitāṃ śiśuṃ saṃsnāpayedguruḥ ।। sruco agre tu śikhāṃ kṛtvā hutvā snāyādanantaram ।। śiśorapi vidhiṃ kṛtvā śivakumbhaṃ samarcayet ।। pūrṇāṃ sampūrya vidhivad vāmamantramanusmaran ।।
heyādhvānamadhaḥ kurvan necayettaṃ varānane ।। nātra kālaḥ kalāścāro na tattvaṃ na ca devatāḥ ।। tadatītaṃ varārohe paraṃ tattvamanāmayam ।। niṣkampe kāraṇātīte viraje nirmale śubhe ।।
ityadhvā caiṣa vai proktaḥ samāsena mayānaghe ।। evaṃ jñātvā varārohe mucyate mocayatyapi ।। jagatsṛṣṭistvayā deva sūcitā na tu varṇitā ।। yo asau sūkṣmaḥ paro devaḥ kāraṇaṃ sarvagaḥ śivaḥ ।।
akāmātsaṃsṛjetsarvaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। upādānaṃ tu tatproktaṃ saṃkṣubdhaṃ samavāyataḥ ।। tasmānnādaḥ samutpannaḥ pūrvaṃ vai kathitastava ।। ghoṣo rāvaḥ svanaḥ śabdaḥ sphoṭākhyo dhvanireva ca ।।
navamastu mahāśabdaḥ sarveṣāṃ vyāpakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tasmāt sadāśivo devo vyakto vai dṛkkriyātmakaḥ ।। sa caiva daśadhā jñeyo daśatattvaphalapradaḥ ।। bindoḥ sadāśivo jñeyaḥ so aṣṭabhedāṅgasaṃyutaḥ ।।
pañcabhiśca mahājñānair mūrtibhiśca samanvitaḥ ।। dvidhāvasthaḥ sa ca jñeyaḥ soccāroccāravarjitaḥ ।। kriyājñānasvarūpeṇa icchārūpasvarūpataḥ ।। sthūlaḥ sūkṣmaḥ paraścaiva parātīto nirañjanaḥ ।।
unmanātīto deveśi śivo jñeyaḥ śivāgame ।। pañcakāraṇarūpeṇa tadadhaḥ punareva saḥ ।। vyāpakaḥ śaktimūrdhastho biladvāramanāśritaḥ ।। vyomarūpī mahādevi bindvīśaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
anātho viṣṇurityuktas tv ananto rudra eva ca ।। vyāpakaśca punardevi hāṭakaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। anantaścaiva deveśi rudraḥ kālāgnivigrahaḥ ।। anāśrito mahādevi sthito vai hūhukaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
tasyāśritaṃ jagatsarvam unmanyantaṃ varānane ।। aptattvaṃ caiva tadadha āgneyaṃ tadanantaram ।। viṣayāśca manaścaiva ahaṃkārastvanukramāt ।। niyatiḥ kālarāgau ca vidyā caiva kalā tathā ।।
bindvardhendunirodhī ca nādo nāḍī tvataḥ param ।। pañcakāraṇasaṃyuktā vyāpinī ca tataḥ param ।। evaṃ vai prakriyāṇḍaṃ tu adhordhvaṃ saṃvyavasthitam ।। yathā ātmāṇavo devi asaṃkhyātā vyavasthitāḥ ।।
ekena varṇiteneha sarvo adhvā varṇitaḥ priye ।। sarveṣāṃ prakriyāṇḍānāṃ svasvarūpeṇa suvrate ।। sarvātiśayanirmuktaḥ sarvakāraṇavarjitaḥ ।। nirmalo vimalaḥ śāntas tv adha ūrdhvaṃ vyavasthitaḥ ।।
evaṃ sarvagato devaḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।। evaṃ jñātvā varārohe na bhūyo janmabhāg bhavet ।। tattve tu pārthive brahmā adhiṣṭhātā vyavasthitaḥ ।। īśvaro vāyutattve tu ākāśe tu sadāśivaḥ ।।
grahāṇāmadhipo rudro nakṣatrāṇāṃ tatheśvaraḥ ।। sadyojātastu vai brahmā vāmo viṣṇuḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। īśānastu varārohe svayaṃ devaḥ sadāśivaḥ ।। aghoraḥ sāmavedastu puruṣo atharva ucyate ।।
laukikaṃ devi vijñānaṃ sadyojātādvinirgatam ।। puruṣāccātimārgākhyaṃ nirgataṃ tu varānane ।। tathā tattvavibhāgena punaśca śṛṇu suvrate ।। pradhānāntaṃ tu deveśi pauruṣaṃ tu janārdanaḥ ।।
vidyā tathaiśvaraṃ tattvaṃ vyāptaṃ caiveśvareṇa tu ।। tattvatrayavibhāgena punarvakṣyāmi suvrate ।। vidyātattve tathā viṣṇur yāvat sādākhyagocaram ।। sādākhyamūrdhvamadhvānaṃ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitaḥ ।।
vyāptaśca vāmayā viṣṇur jyeṣṭhayā ca pitāmahaḥ ।। icchāśaktiḥ paro rudraḥ sa śivaḥ parigīyate ।। sadāśivaḥ śivāddevi utpannaḥ prabhurīśvaraḥ ।। jñānaśaktikarāgreṇa svecchayā parameśvaraḥ ।।
te ca sādākhyaparyante pārthivādye tu suvrate ।। śivaśaktisamāviṣṭās trinetrāścandramaulayaḥ ।। jagadvyāpya sthito māyī śūlapāṇiranekadhā ।। icchāśaktyā samāviṣṭaḥ kriyāśaktyā tu suvrate ।।
tatsthaṃ kṛtvātmavargaṃ tu yugapat kṣobhayetprabhuḥ ।। tiryagūrdhvamadhastācca nirgacchanti samāsataḥ ।। ūrdhvaṃ gacchanti te sarve śivaṃ paramanirmalam ।। saṃsārabhājanaṃ ye tu malakarmakalānvitāḥ ।।
tasmātkalā samutpannā vidyā rāgastathaiva ca ।। sattvaṃ rajastamaścaiva prakṛtestu guṇāstrayaḥ ।। tamo avaṣṭambhakaṃ proktaṃ vijñeyaṃ tu guṇatrayam ।। brahmatve sṛjate lokān viṣṇutve sthitikārakaḥ ।।
jāgratsvapnasuṣuptaṃ ca tisro avasthāśca tadgatāḥ ।। brahmā tatrādhipatyena buddhitattve vyavasthitaḥ ।। guṇeṣvārahatānāṃ ca pradhānaṃ vedavādinām ।। ṣaḍviṃśakaṃ ca deveśi yogaśāstre paraṃ padam ।।
mausule kāruke caiva māyātattvaṃ prakīrtitam ।। tejeśo vaimalānāṃ ca pramāṇe ca dhruvaṃ padam ।। kapālavratamāsthāya svaṃ svaṃ gacchati tatpadam ।। sarvādhvāno viniṣkrāntaṃ śaivānāṃ tu paraṃ padam ।।
sāttviko rājasaścaiva tāmasaśca prakīrtitaḥ ।। tanmātrāṇyatha bhūtādes tebhyo bhūtānyajījanat ।। etāni pañca khyātāni tanmātrāṇi krameṇa tu ।। rūpāttejaḥ samutpannam āpo jātā rasāt punaḥ ।।
karmendriyāṇi jātāni tasmādvaikārikādatha ।। buddhīndriyāṇi pañcaiva taijasāttu bhavantyatha ।। ubhayātma manaḥ proktaṃ vyāptṛ sarvendriyāṇi tu ।। ātmā caivāntarātmā ca bāhyātmā caiva sundari ।।
abudhaśca budhaścaiva budhyamānastathaiva ca ।। pradhānasāmyamāśritya sukhaduḥkhavivarjitaḥ ।। puryaṣṭakasamāyogāt paryaṭet sarvayoniṣu ।। buddhikarmendriyairyukto mahābhūtaiḥ samāvṛtaiḥ ।।
bhūtabhāvavinirmuktas tattvadharmakalojjhitaḥ ।। nirātmā tu tadā jñeyaḥ paramātmātha kathyate ।। sarvādhvasamatītaśca māyāmohojjhitaśca yaḥ ।। paramātmā tadā devi procyate prabhuravyayaḥ ।।
tattvabhūtātmasaṃhāre kalākṣityantagocare ।। nirvyāpāro bhavettāvad yāvadvai nodaya punaḥ ।। malanidrāvimūḍhātmā ruddhacaitanyadṛkkriyaḥ ।। kāraṇaṃ na vijānāti na ca sthānaṃ svakaṃ priye ।।
abudhastiṣṭhate tatra yāvanmāyā aharmukham ।। paripākagate karmaṇīśvarecchākaroddhṛte ।। karaṇānyanugṛhṇāti tadvadīśvara ātmanām ।। rāgo asya rañjakatvena viṣayānandalakṣaṇaḥ ।।
niyatirniścitaṃ nityaṃ yojayecca śubhāśubhe ।। pumbhāvaṃ tamanuprāpya tattve ca puruṣāhvaye ।। tatpuraṃ poṣayedyasmāt tasmādvai puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pradhānapāśajāleva veṣṭayedasamañjasam ।।
tanmātrendriyabandhena dṛḍhaṃ bhūtaiśca veṣṭitaḥ ।। saṃsārī procyate tasmāt saṃsaredyat punaḥ punaḥ ।। viṣayāḥ paramityāha nānābhedairvisarpitāḥ ।। evaṃ bhuṅkte tu vai yasmāt tasmādbhoktā sa ucyate ।।
mahābilāṣamālokya kṛṣedvai lobhalāṅgalaiḥ ।। dharmādharmamayaṃ bījaṃ pravikīrya samantataḥ ।। vardhate kāmakrodhena siktā rāgāmbunā bhṛśam ।। uptaṃ śubhāśubhaṃ karma tatkāle labhate phalam ।।
yasmādevaṃ vijānāti tasmāt kṣetrajña ucyate ।। tadevāniṣṭarūpeṇa yadā bhāvayate pumān ।। yadā jugupsate bhogān śubhāṃścaivāśubhāṃstathā ।। māyādyavaniparyantam indrajālaṃ tu budhyate ।।
yadarjitaṃ mayā dravyaṃ śubhenāpyaśubhena vā ।। ekākī cāhamevaiṣa yāsyāmi yamasādanam ।। svāmīyamapyayaṃ dehaṃ nityameva jugupsate ।। nānāvyādhisamākīrṇaṃ jarāmṛtyubhayākulam ।।
nityamudvignacittastu cintayedvai punaḥ punaḥ ।। evaṃ prabuddho deveśi tallayastatparāyaṇaḥ ।। prabuddhastu samākhyātaḥ suprabuddhaṃ tu me śṛṇu ।। yadā prāptaḥ paraṃ sthānam adhvātītaṃ nirāmayam ।।
niṣkampaṃ kāraṇātītaṃ sarvajñaṃ sarvatomukham ।। aluptaśaktivibhavaṃ suprabuddhaṃ sanātanam ।। suprabuddhaḥ sa evokto bhairavasya vaco yathā ।। adhunā kathayiṣyāmi bhāvabhedān varānane ।।
ekādaśendriyavadhā ahaṅkārastu vai tridhā ।। nāmānyeṣāṃ vibhāgena kathayāmi yathākramam ।। pṛthivyāpastathā tejo vāyurākāśameva ca ।। sparśaḥ śabdaśca pañcaiva tanmātrāṇīritāni tu ।।
vākpāṇipādaṃ pāyuṃ ca upasthaṃ ca tathā viduḥ ।। bahiṣkaraṇakaṃ devi daśadhā saṃvyavasthitam ।। mūkatā kauṇyapaṅgutvaṃ tathānutsargatāpi ca ।। śīrṇatā caiva gātrasya tathā cāndhatvameva ca ।।
itīndriyavadhāḥ khyātā ekādaśa tu tatkramāt ।। ahaṅkārastridhā prokto mayā ta varavarṇini ।। adharmaṃ ca tathājñānam avairāgyamanaiśvaram ।। tamo moho mahāmohas tāmisro anyo viparyayaḥ ।।
bhāvabhedāḥ samākhyātāḥ pañcāśatte yathākramam ।। teṣāṃ bhedā yathā bhinnās tathāhaṃ kathayāmi te ।। mocayejjñānabhāvena sāṃkhyajñānaratānnarān ।। tāmasāścāpyadharmādyāś catvāro vai varānane ।।
vairāgyaṃ navadhā caivam aiśvaryaṃ cāṣṭadhā viduḥ ।। akrodho guruśuśrūṣā śaucaṃ santoṣa ārjavam ।। evaṃ daśavidho dharmaḥ kathitastu varānane ।। pramuditaṃ ramyakaṃ ca sadāpramuditaṃ tathā ।।
ambhā ca salilā odhā vṛṣṭisaṃjñā tathāparā ।। aṣṭamī ca kumārī syād uttamāmbhasikā tathā ।। aṇimā laghimā caiva mahimā prāptireva ca ।। yatrakāmāvasāyitvam aṣṭamaṃ parikīrtitam ।।
krodhaścāguruśuśrūṣā aśaucaṃ ca tataḥ param ।। steyamabrahmacaryaṃ ca tathā caiva sakalkatā ।। atāramasutāraṃ ca atāraṇamathāpi ca ।। apramodo apramuditam aramyakamathāpi ca ।।
anambhā asalilā ca anoghāvṛṣṭireva ca ।। akumārī ca vijñeyān uttamāmbhasikā tathā ।। aprāptiraprākāmyaṃ cānīśitvaṃ ca tathaiva ca ।। anaiśvaryādibhiścaite paiśācādyā adhiṣṭhitāḥ ।।
anaiśvaryaṃ hi paiśāce avairāgyaṃ ca rākṣase ।। dharmaṃ caiva tathaindre tu jñānaṃ saumye pratiṣṭhitam ।। catuṣṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ caitat pade brāhme vyavasthitam ।। aṣṭacatvāriṃśadguṇaṃ saumye vai parikīrtitam ।।
dvātriṃśadguṇitaṃ devi gāndharvaiśvaryamucyate ।। aiśvaryamaṣṭaguṇitaṃ paiśācaṃ parikīrtitam ।। anye saptasvarūpeṇa saṃsthitā devayoniṣu ।। pradhānaguṇabhāvena sthāvarāntaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ।।
sattvenādhiṣṭhitā devā brahmādyā maghavāntakāḥ ।। yātudhānāḥ piśācāśca tāmasāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। anyonyābhibhavāste ca pṛthivyāṃ saṃvyavasthitāḥ ।। pādapādavihīnāśca tāmasāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।
eṣāmantargatāścānyā anantā eva yonayaḥ ।। na śakyā gadituṃ tā vai karmānantyaprabhedataḥ ।। dharmādyeṣu nibaddhāni yāni jñānāni suvrate ।। hetuśāstraṃ ca yalloke nityānityaviḍambakam ।।
hetuniṣṭhāni vākyāni vastuśūnyāni suvrate ।। dharmārthakāmamokṣeṣu niścayo naiva jāyate ।। nirayaṃ te pragacchanti ye tatrābhiratā narāḥ ।। catvāraste varārohe duḥkhadā narake sadā ।।
dharmeṇaikena deveśi baddhaṃ jñānaṃ hi laukikam ।। bauddhamārahataṃ caiva vairāgyeṇaiva suvrate ।। jñānaṃ vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ yogajñānapratiṣṭhitam ।। lokātītaṃ tu tajjñānam atimārgamiti smṛtam ।।
teṣāmatītāste jñeyā ye atimārge vyavasthitāḥ ।। sṛṣṭirna vidyate teṣāṃ īśvare ca dhruve sthitāḥ ।। laukikānāṃ punaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ punaḥ saṃhāra eva ca ।। dharmādyarakasaṃyuktam aṣṭāraṃ cakrakaṃ priye ।।
malakarmakalāviddhaṃ bhramate kālavegataḥ ।। hetuśāstraparā ye tu ye cānye pāpakarmiṇaḥ ।। laukikādyeṣu ye sādhyā atimārgāntagocare ।। na sarvaiḥ sādhyate tadvai yato atīva sunirmalam ।।
abhāvaṃ bhāvanātītaṃ prapañcātītagocaram ।। pratyakṣādipramāṇaiśca vyatītaṃ prabhu cāvyayam ।। sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ śāntaṃ nirmalaṃ nirupaplavam ।। sarvātiśayanirmuktam anādibhavavarjitam ।।
evaṃ sṛṣṭāni tattvāni jñānāni ca varānane ।। bhuvanāni vicitrāṇi śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। vijñānaṃ kuhakaṃ śilpaṃ siddhisandohalakṣaṇam ।। prakriyā śivadīkṣā ca tattvairetairhi labhyate ।।
na prakriyāparaṃ jñānaṃ nāsti yogastvalakṣakaḥ ।। evaṃ sṛṣṭiḥ samākhyātā sthitiḥ saṃhāra ucyate ।। kṣaṇadvayaṃ tuṭirjñeyā taddvayaṃ tu lavaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। daśa pañca nimeṣāśca kāṣṭhā caiva prakīrtitā ।।
muhūrtastu punastriṃśad ahorātrastu mānuṣaḥ ।। saṃvatsarastu vijñeyo mānuṣaḥ kamalekṣaṇe ।। daśa pañca tvahorātrāḥ pakṣastu parikīrtitaḥ ।। ṛtudvayena kālaḥ syād ayanaṃ ca tribhistribhiḥ ।।
dakṣiṇaṃ cāyanaṃ rātrir uttaraṃ cāyanaṃ dinam ।। evaṃ daivastvahorātras tatrāpyabdādi pūrvavat ।। caturbhistu kṛtaṃ devi sahasraistu yathākramam ।। sahasreṇaiva varṣāṇāṃ vijñeyastu kaliḥ priye ।।
śatāni catvāri kṛte tv ādirantaśca kīrtyate ।। kalau cāpi śataṃ jñeyaṃ sandhyāmānamidaṃ smṛtam ।। tricatvāriṃśallakṣāṇi sahasrāṇi ca viṃśatiḥ ।। ekaikasya punardevi yugasya kathayāmi te ।।
kṛtasyaitadbhavenmānaṃ tretāyāṃ kathayāmi te ।। tretāyugasya mānaṃ tu dvāparasya nibodha me ।। dvāparasya tu mānaṃ ca kalestu kathayāmi te ।। etanmānaṃ kaleḥ proktaṃ samāsāttava suvrate ।।
caturyugaikasaptatyā bhavenmanvantaraṃ punaḥ ।। etaddivyena mānena mānaṃ manvantare smṛtam ।। saptaṣaṣṭistu lakṣāṇi triṃśatkoṭyo varānane ।। caturdaśabhirdeveśi kalpo manvantare bhavet ।।
pañca varṣasahasrāṇi madhye sandhyā bhavet sadā ।। kalpo brahmadinaṃ proktaṃ caturyugasahasrakam ।। koṭirekā tu varṣāṇāṃ lakṣāṇāṃ caiva viṃśatiḥ ।। ṣaṇṇavatyā sahasraistu sandhyākālaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।
varṣavṛndāni catvāri tv arbudatrayameva ca ।। sandhyā koṭitrayaṃ caiva pañca lakṣāṇi kīrtitā ।। paścimaḥ sandhirevaṃ hi pūrvasandhyāpi tatsamā ।। lokānāṃ caiva saptānāṃ sthitireṣā prakīrtitā ।।
brahmaṇaḥ svadinānte vai kalpaḥ saṃhāra ucyate ।। rājyaṃ kṛtvā kramādyānti manvantaravyavasthayā ।। supte pitāmahe devi ūrdhvaṃ kālāgnirīkṣate ।। tasmādvaktrānmahājvālā lakṣayojanavistṛtā ।।
lokeṣu ye sthitā lokā ye ca pātālavāsinaḥ ।। sattāmātrāstu te sarve bhavanti brahmaviṣṭape ।। tāvattiṣṭhanti te mūḍhā yāvadbrahmā na budhyate ।। kūṣmāṇḍahāṭakādyāstu te tisṭhantyatinirmalāḥ ।।
śūnyabhūteṣu lokeṣu jvālā dahati durdharā ।। trīṃllokāṃścaiva dahati bhūrbhuvaḥsvaḥpadāntikān ।। mahojanastapaḥsaṃjñāḥ satyaloko api suvrate ।। evaṃ dagdghā jagatsarvaṃ jvālā vaktraṃ viśet punaḥ ।।
nāśayanti ca tadbhasma jagaddāhodbhavaṃ priye ।। tenaiva vāriṇā devi jagadekārṇavaṃ bhavet ।। karmataḥ sarvalokasya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। ṣaḍvidhāṃ kurute sṛṣṭiṃ yathāpūrvavyavasthayā ।।
narakān vividhākārān paśūn vai sthāvarāntagān ।। rajaḥsattvasamāviṣṭaḥ sṛjenmunivareśvaram ।। sṛjeddevān salokāṃśca pūrvayaiva vyavasthayā ।। adhikāraṃ prakurvanti sve sve viṣayagocare ।।
dinamānaṃ ca yatproktaṃ rātrisaṃkhyā ca tāvatī ।। abdānāṃ tu śate pūrṇe mahākalpaḥ sa ucyate ।। ekanavatikoṭistu tathā lakṣāṇi viṃśatiḥ ।। brāhmaṃ varṣaśataṃ caitaj jñātavyaṃ kālavedinā ।।
laukikena tu mānena punaścaiva nibodha me ।। kharvadvayaṃ ca deveśi nikharvāḥ pañca eva tu ।। etaddevi samākhyātaṃ jñātavyaṃ ca mumukṣubhiḥ ।। ekaṃ daśaguṇaṃ pūrvaṃ śataṃ daśaguṇaṃ tu tat ।।
sahasraṃ daśaguṇitam ayutaṃ taddhi kīrtitam ।। daśa tāni ca koṭiḥ syād daśa koṭistathārbudam ।। daśabhistairnikharvaṃ tu śaṅkuḥ syāddaśa tāni tu ।। sāgarairdaśabhirmadhyam antyaṃ tairdaśabhiḥ smṛtam ।।
evamaṣṭādaśaitāni sthānāni gaṇitasya tu ।। viṣṇośca taddinaṃ proktaṃ rātrirvai tatsamā bhavet ।। varṣāṇāṃ ca śate pūrṇe so api yāti pare layam ।। dine dine sṛjatyanyau brahmaviṣṇū prajāpatī ।।
yaṃ cādhitiṣṭhatyātmānaṃ tatsaṃjñāṃ sa prapadyate ।। brahmaviṣṇvindrarudrāśca vidyeśā īśvarastathā ।। grahādimātaro rudrā yoganakṣatrarāśayaḥ ।। tatparākramavīryāstu svakīye tu pade sthitāḥ ।।
