sā śaktirbhidyate devi bhedairānantyasambhavaiḥ ।। saṃhāraṃ ca dinānte vai rātrirvai tatsamā bhavet ।। vatsarāṇāṃ śate pūrṇe śatarudradinakṣayāt ।। tasmin sthāne punaścānyas tatsamaśca prabhurbhavet ।।
śatarudrāstu deveśi svābdānāṃ tu śatakṣaye ।। sarvabhūtaguṇādhāraṃ sarvatattvālayālayam ।। vimānamālākulitaṃ grahanakṣatramaṇḍitam ।। ṛṣibhirmānuṣādyaiśca saptalokanivāsibhiḥ ।।
aśeṣabhuvanādhāramaṇḍamapsu pralīyate ।। aptattvāttu samārabhya yāvanmāyāntagocaram ।। tadūrdhvaṃ śuddhamadhvānaṃ yāvacchaktyantagocaram ।। triṣvevaṃ saṃsthito rudraḥ kālarūpī maheśvaraḥ ।।
evaṃ bhūtādyāvaraṇapatayaśca śatātyaye ।। āpastejasi līyante tattejaścānile punaḥ ।। tanmātreṣu pralīyante yathotpannāni ca kramāt ।। sa buddhau sā ca gahane guṇasāmye pralīyate ।।
tasmin jagadaśeṣaṃ tu prasuptamiva tiṣṭhati ।। ṣaḍviṃśakasya rudrasya caitaddinamiha smṛtam ।। sāṅkhyajñānena ye siddhāḥ vedena brahmavādinaḥ ।। ahni tiṣṭhanti te sarve parameśasya dhīmataḥ ।।
ṣaṭtriṃśattu sahasrāṇi brahmaṇāṃ pralayodbhavāḥ ।। tasmin saṃharate sarvaṃ pradhānasya dinakṣaye ।। tasyāpyanena nyāyena parimāṇasthitirbhave ।। tato niyatikālau ca rāgo vidyā kalā tathā ।।
kalādyavaniparyantaṃ gahaneśadinakṣaye ।। saguṇādhāraparyantarudrakṣetrajñasaṅkulam ।। rātryante jāyate bhūyo gahaneśapracodanāt ।। pralayaśca sa evokto bhūtānāṃ parameśvari ।।
māyā saṃharate sarvaṃ punaścaiva sṛjejjagat ।। īśvaraḥ kurute sṛṣṭiṃ punaśca saṃharejjagat ।। sṛjate ca punarbhūya ātmīye devyaharmukhe ।। bindutattve layaṃ yāti pañcamantramahātanuḥ ।।
nādatattve layaṃ yāti gṛhītvā sacarācaram ।। śaktitattve layaṃ yāti śaktitattvadinakṣaye ।। tacca śivatattvasthasya vyāpīśasyāpyaharmukham ।। līyate so apyananteśe so anāthe so apyanāśrite ।।
anāśritasya devasya dinametat prakīrtitam ।। so api yāti paraṃ sthānaṃ kāraṇaṃ svamanāśrayam ।। tato apyūrdhvamameyastu kālaḥ syāt paramāvadhiḥ ।। sa cādhaḥ kalayet sarvaṃ vyāpinyādiṃ dharāvadhim ।।
ūrdhvamunmanaso yacca tatra kālo na vidyate ।। yaḥ śāṅkaryunmanātītaḥ sa nityo vyāpako avyayaḥ ।। arūpā rūpanirmuktaḥ so anādirbhavavarjitaḥ ।। sa evāpararūpeṇa unmanyā mūrdhni saṃsthitaḥ ।।
paryānukramayogena so akāmāt sṛjate jagat ।। evaṃ praśnavaraṃ guhyaṃ kathayasva prasādataḥ ।। vahniḥ saṃjāyate tasmād ravestatra na kāmitā ।। ādityavacchivo jñeyaḥ śaktirmaṇiriva sthitā ।।
yadvacchivasamāyogāt tadvacchakterjagatsthitiḥ ।। jagatsaṃbhavahetuśca tvatprasādācchrutaṃ mayā ।। pṛthivyādi śivāntaṃ ca kathayāmi samāsataḥ ।। māṃse asthiṣu tathā caiva snāyulomanakheṣu ca ।।
kaphāsṛgāmamūtreṣu rasasvedavasāsu ca ।। pacane dahane caiva tejasyūṣmaṇi saṃsthitam ।। vāyurucchvāsaniḥśvāsasparśanavyūhalakṣaṇaḥ ।। vāyurebhiḥ sthito dehe vijñeyastu dvilakṣaṇaḥ ।।
suṣirātmakaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ navadhā cchidralakṣaṇam ।। vāgindriyaṃ vadedvāṇīṃ sā ca vāṇī caturvidhā ।। chedanaṃ bhedanaṃ dānaṃ vyadhanaṃ śilpayojanam ।। samanimnonnatāścaiva loṣṭakaṇṭakavālukāḥ ।।
pādendriyeṇa gamyante deśāntaragamāgame ।। ānandakṛdupasthaśca gamyāgamyapravartakaḥ ।। buddhīndriyāṇi deveśi vartante buddhiyogataḥ ।। dhaivato niṣadhaścaiva svarāḥ sapta prakīrtitāḥ ।।
saptasvarāstrayo grāmā mūrchanāścaikaviṃśatiḥ ।। sūkṣmaśabdāḥ smṛtā hyete carācararavasthitāḥ ।। bherīpaṭahaśaṅkhottho mṛdaṅgapaṇavotthitaḥ ।। tantrīvādyāni citrāṇi karavādyāni yāni ca ।।
apabhraṃśo anunāsikyaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ prākṛto ravaḥ ।। uktānuktāni gṛhṇāti śravaṇendriyayogataḥ ।। mṛduṃ ca kaṭhinaṃ caiva karkaśaṃ śītalaṃ tathā ।। śarakuntāsighātādi tāḍanaṃ chedanaṃ tathā ।।
sparśo asya viṣayo hyeṣa yena budhyeta pudgalaḥ ।। sitaṃ raktaṃ ca pītaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ haritadhūmrakam ।। naranārīpaśumṛgāñ jyotiḥ sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। rūpākhyo viṣayo hyasya yenātmā pratibuddhyate ।।
kaṣāyamiśraṃ svāduṃ ca jihvā vedayate rasam ।। surabhirdivyagandhaśca durgandhaścāpyanekadhā ।। yenāsau budhyate kṣetrī ahaṅkāreṇa mohitaḥ ।। anivāritasandeham ajayyaṃ sarvadehinām ।।
svarūpadharmaṃ vakṣyāmi tanmātrāṇāṃ yathārthataḥ ।। jihvayā rasatanmātraṃ rasaṃ gṛhṇāti saṃsthitam ।। gṛhṇāti sparśatanmātraṃ tvacā sparśamupāgatam ।। sūkṣmastanmātradharmo ayaṃ bhūtānāṃ prakṛtikramāt ।।
ahaṃ vidvānahaṃ bhogī tv ahaṃ jāto mahākule ।। ahaṃ yoddhā ca saṃgrāme śatravaśca mayā jitāḥ ।। ahaṃ pāpī durācāro mūrkhaścāhaṃ durākṛtiḥ ।। ityahaṅkāracittānāṃ mamatvavaśavartinām ।।
trividhasyāpyayaṃ dharmo ahaṅkārasya prakīrtitaḥ ।। dharmo jñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ ca catuṣṭayam ।। badhnāti saptadhā sā tu jñānabhāvena mohayet ।। dharmādīnāmathāṣṭānāṃ lakṣaṇāni śṛṇu priye ।।
satyaṃ śaucaṃ ca dānaṃ ca dayā kṣāntiśca sarvadā ।। iṣṭāpūrtaṃ tīrthasevā pitṛṇāṃ caiva tarpaṇam ।। dhīguṇaḥ prathamo hyeṣa dharma ityabhidhīyate ।। punarmārtyaṃ punaḥ svargyaṃ tīryak tvaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ ।।
caturviṃśatikaḥ piṇḍaḥ karaṇendriyasaṃyutaḥ ।। akartā nirguṇaścāhaṃ na me bandho asti prākṛtaḥ ।। sāṅkhyajñānaṃ mayā proktaṃ prakṛteryena mucyate ।। baddhaḥ saṃsarate bhūyo yāvaddevaṃ na vindati ।।
vairāgyātsantyajetputrān dārāniṣṭānsusaṃmatān ।। upavāsaṃ japaṃ tīrthaṃ pañcāgniṃ jalaśāyitām ।। girivṛkṣajalāgnibhyaḥ prahārodbandhanāśanaiḥ ।। aiśvaryabhāvamāpanno dravyaistṛptiṃ na gacchati ।।
tapo vratāni mantrāṃśca aiśvaryārthe tu sādhayet ।। anyānyapi tvayuktāni visrambhacchalaghātitām ।। prāṇihiṃsārato nityaṃ caurikānṛtadambhavān ।। nāstidharmo na cādharmaḥ svargaṃ mokṣaṃ ca ko gataḥ ।।
nityaṃ duḥkhī parapreṣyo bhāraṃ yānaṃ vahannapi ।। rājyaṃ kṛtvā tu sāmantaḥ sāmantyādgrāmabhugbhavet ।। na śocati na codvignaḥ krīḍate pūrvarājyavat ।। avyaktaṃ triguṇaṃ vakṣye saṃsārasya pravartakam ।।
asya dharmaṃ pravakṣyāmi rajaḥ sattvatamo abhidham ।। saṃvibhāgī ca satataṃ nityaṃ sattvopakārakaḥ ।। prītirdānaṃ dhṛtirmedhā tapaḥ śaucaṃ damastathā ।। yasminnete sadā dharmā bhavanti puruṣottame ।।
nistriṃśaścātilobhī ca vidveṣī krodhanastathā ।। mānī dambhasamāyukto apyahaṅkāre vyavasthitaḥ ।। kāmakrodhābhibhūtatvaṃ lobhena ca samanvayaḥ ।। nidrālasya makarmitvaṃ daurmedhyājñānite tathā ।।
tamaḥ cihnāni caitāni dṛśyante yatra mānave ।। etatriguṇamavyaktaṃ triguṇaṃ sāmudāhṛtam ।। guṇadharmā na caivāhaṃ buddhyahāṃkṛdguṇo nahi ।। akartā nirguṇaścāhaṃ cinmātraḥ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
prakṛtyā kāritāṃ manye akartā puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। nāhaṃ kartā na me bandha evaṃ budhyeta yo naraḥ ।। sāṅkhyajñānena saṃmūdho muktirityabhimanyate ।। tiṣṭhetprakṛtinirmuktaḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhāravarjitaḥ ।।
tāvatprakṛtibandhena saṃsāre kṣipyate punāḥ ।। dharmādhārmanibaddhastu sāṅkhyajñānena mohitaḥ ।। mamatvenaiva saṃmūḍho bhrāmyate ghaṭayantravat ।। pṛthvīṃ kaṭhinarūpeṇa catuḥ sāgaramekhalām ।।
susthitāṃ pītavarṇābhām ūbījena samanvitām ।। acālyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yathaiva vasudhā bhavet ।। evamabhyasyamānastu viṣasattvānvināśayet ।। jagadāpūrayetsiddhaḥ pūrvabījasamanvitaḥ ।।
kṛṣṇareṇvātmako vāyur dhyeyo bījena saṃyutaḥ ।। suṣirātmakaṃ svadehaṃ tu jagacca suṣirātmakam ।। vāgindriye tathā vahnir dhyāto vāksiddhidāyakaḥ ।। pādayordūrasaṃcāraṃ dhyāto viṣṇuḥ prayacchati ।।
śiśne prajāpatiṃ śyāmaṃ dhyāyedyuktena cetasā ।। śrotrendriye diśaścitrā dhyāyedvījena saṃyutāḥ ।। mārutaṃ kṛṣṇarūpeṇa dhyāyettu tvaci saṃsthitam ।। ādityaṃ cakṣuṣi dhyāyej jihvāyāṃ varuṇaṃ tathā ।।
pītakaṃ gandhatanmātraṃ rasatanmātrakaṃ sitam ।। arūpaṃ śabdatanmātraṃ dhyātavyaṃ bindurūpi ca ।। vaikārike tathā rudro dhyātavyaḥ siddhimicchatā ।। brahmāṇaṃ buddhisaṃsthaṃ tu dhyāyedyuktena cetasā ।।
divyā ca jāyate buddhiḥ saṃśayocchittikārikā ।। prakṛtiḥ kṛṣṇavarṇā tu raktaśuklā virājate ।। dhyātavyā tattvabījena yadīcchetsiddhimātmanaḥ ।। ṣaṇmāsābhyāsayogena divyā dṛṣṭiḥ pravartate ।।
eṣa te prākṛto yoga uktaḥ mokṣakaraḥ paraḥ ।। citsvarūpaśca sarveṣu dehamāpūrya saṃsthitaḥ ।। nirgatena mṛtā yena acetāḥ śīryate tanuḥ ।। na tasya rūpaṃ varṇo vā pramāṇaṃ dṛśyate kvacit ।।
vālāgraśatabhāgasya śatadhā kalpitasya tu ।। ādityavarṇaṃ rukmābham abbindumiva puṣkare ।। rāgavidyākalopetaḥ kālabaddho hi rūpavān ।। dakṣiṇena sitāṅgī tu vāmenāsitarūpiṇī ।।
karmabandhena badhnāti sukhaduḥkhaṃ prayacchati ।। pūrvabījasahadhyānā dvirūpeṇa samanvitā ।। trinetraṃ ca caturvaktraṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ caturbhujam ।। svabījadhyānarūpajñaḥ kālena nahi kalyate ।।
evaṃ kālaṃ sadā dhyāyet dhyeyasiddhiśca jāyate ।। sitavarṇāṃ kalāṃ dhyāyec cetanyonmīlinīṃ tu tām ।। kacordhvapiṅgakeśī ca sthūlakāyā mahodarī ।। nirvairaparipanthitvān māyā granthirduruttarā ।।
na tāṃ laṅghayituṃ śaktā ye cānye mokṣavādinaḥ ।। svabījadhyānayogena pūrvadhyānasvarūpataḥ ।। caturvarṇā bhavedvidyā sā varṇavyāpinī smṛtā ।। ākāśavāyumārūḍhā rūpayauvanaśālinī ।।
divyā siddhiramoghā tu siddhavidyaśca jāyate ।। kuṅkumābhaṃ ca nāreśaṃ trinetraṃ tu jaṭādharam ।। tatpuṇyaphalamāpnoti aśvamedhāyutasya ca ।। ṣaḍbhirmāsairasandehaḥ dakṣiṇaṃ ca tathaiva hi ।।
bhrukuṭīkarālavaktraṃ ca kapālāhi vibhūṣitam ।। sukhaduḥkhavināśāya ītijvaravināśanam ।। agnivajjvalate yogī jarāmṛtyuvivarjitaḥ ।। sitaṃ trinayanaṃ devi sākṣāsūtrakamaṇḍalu ।।
hatvā prāṇisahasrāṇi paradāraśatāni ca ।। trinetramuttaraṃ vaktraṃ raktotpalasamadyuti ।। tapate varṣate caiva sṛjate saṃharatyapi ।। sitamūrdhvaṃ sadā dhyāyec chūlahastaṃ jaṭādharam ।।
vīṇāḍamaruhastaṃ ca nāgayajñopavītakam ।। anenaiva tu dehena sarvajñaḥ kāmarūpavān ।। īpsitā martyaloke tu siddhistasya prajāyate ।। māsenaikena paśyetsa sūkṣmaṃ liṅgaṃ tanūpari ।।
siddhistu mānuṣe loke ṣaṇmāsena prajāyate ।। ākrāmetsarvalokāṃśca īśvareṇa samo bhavet ।। tanmātrāṇi hayāstasya manaḥ sārathi coditaḥ ।। indriyāṇi śarāstasya mṛgo dharmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।
puṇyapāpairvartamāna icchayā parameśvari ।। matvā ceśvaravijñānaṃ sarvakarmaṇi santyajet ।। tamahaṃ śaraṇaṃ prāpto na me bandho asti kaṛtṛtā ।। dhyeyaḥ pūrvoktarūpeṇa tatsiddhiphalamicchatā ।।
dakṣiṇottarasaṃkrāntyā viṣuvajjñasya mokṣadaḥ ।। sadāśivaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ dhyānātsiddhiphalaṃ śṛṇu ।। tṛtīye paśyate siddhān divyadṛṣṭiścaturthake ।। divyāsiddhistathābdena sāyujyaṃ tu dvitīyake ।।
aṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ śrutī netre tarjanīmadhyamākramāt ।। daśadhā varṇarūpeṇa dṛśyate ca sadāśivaḥ ।। nīlaṃ citrakavarṇaṃ tu sphaṭikābhaṃ manoramam ।। ekameva tu gṛhṇīyād anye tu guṇarūpakāḥ ।।
tārakācalitākāraṃ bindumevaṃ vilakṣayet ।। ābhiḥ kalābhiḥ saṃyukto dhyātavyo bindurīśvaraḥ ।। khaṃ vīkṣya mīlitākṣo yad udyadbhāskarasannibham ।। pītā raktā tathā kṛṣṇā sphaṭikābhā manoramā ।।
vyāpinīṃ ca tataścordhve pañcarūpāṃ vicintayet ।। samanāmunmanāṃ coktāṃ dhyāyedyuktena cetasā ।। tataścordhve śivaḥ śāntaḥ pūrvaṃ vai kathito mayā ।। manaścintayate yāni buddhiryāni vyavasyati ।।
yaśca nāsti sa tatraiva tv anveṣṭavyaḥ prayatnataḥ ।। sukhāsīnaḥ saṃyatātmā ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। bhāvanāttasya tattvasya tatsamaścaiva jāyate ।। taistu dharmaiḥ samāyukti yogī vai bhavati priye ।।
evaṃ jñātvā ca dhyātvā ca siddhyate mucyate api ca ।। tamākhyāhi samāsena sādhakānāṃ hitāya vai ।। praṇavāsanamārūḍham aṅgavaktraiḥ samanvitam ।। sa eva homavinyāsaḥ dīkṣā saiva prakīrtitaḥ ।।
samudragasarittīre sahāyaiḥ parivarjitaḥ ।। jitendriyaikacittastu brahmacarye vyavasthitaḥ ।। yāni kānīha karmāṇi catuṣpīṭhasthitāni ca ।। tāni siddhyanti deveśi bhairavasya vaco yathā ।।
yaṃ jñātvā devadeveśi vicarantīha sādhakāḥ ।। abhimukhakhaḍgani pātitaśūraśiraḥ śoṣitaṃ samādāya । raktālaktakalikhitaṃ sādhyatanau mantrayuktamabhidhānam ।। pretānale sutaptaṃ vidhāya niśi yatkṛte śataṃ japati ।
asurendracakravartinamasurendraguruṃ vā tamānayatyanilavegāt ।। pretālaktakalikhitaṃ naraśirasi pretavahnisantaptam । yamalokādapyacirādānayati balena pūrvavat sādhyam ।। mṛtanāryā vāmapadādudbaddhāyāstu pāṃsulīṃ samādāya ।
rudhirālaktakarocanayā sādhyatanuṃ mantrasaṃyuktām ।। khadirānale sutaptāṃ rātryardhe sammukho japaśatena । ānayati śacīmahalyāmathavā divasasya śatabhāgāt ।। udbaddhastrītanuvāmāṅghreḥ pāṃsulīṃ samādāya ।
pretālaktakanijarudhirarocanābhirvilikhya sādhyatanum ।। pretānale sutaptāṃ śatābhijaptāṃ svanāmamantrayutām । kṛtvā yakṣasurāsurapannaganārīḥ samānayatyāśu ।। nijavāmakare alaktakarocanayā sādhyanāma parilikhitam ।
mantravidarbhitametajjapaśatayuktaṃ sutāpitaṃ rātrau ।। khadirānale vidhūme asuragurumapyānayatyanilavegāt । sādhyamabhidhānalikhitaṃ bhūmitale gairikeṇa raktena ।। gandhodvartitavāmahastena tu tattvabījayuktena ।
ākramya bhūmilikhitaṃ sādhyābhimukho ardharātrakāle tu ।। kṣitipatimapi sāmātyaṃ cānayati nimeṣaśatabhāgāt । nṛkapālamadhyalikhitaṃ rocanayā raktamiśrayā sādhyam ।। nāma ca tasya lalāṭe mantreṇa vidarbhitaṃ samālikhya ।
gandhodakena liptaṃ nṛkapālaṃ vai dvitīyamādāya ।। kṛtvā kapālasampuṭamatha mṛtasūtreṇa veṣṭayet samyak । khadirāṅgārasutaptaṃ sikthakaliptaṃ tu tatpunaḥ kṛtvā ।। yāvat sikthakametat kapālalagnaṃ vilīyate tāvat ।
surapatimapyākarṣati japaśatayogānnimeṣamātreṇa ।। bhittau gairikalikhitaṃ mantrārṇavidarbhitaṃ tadabhidhānam । sādhyābhimukho rātrau vāmakarākrāntamatha japan kruddhaḥ ।। kroṅkārāṅkuśayogādānayati surāsurān kṣipram ।
raṇaśastraghātapatitaṃ narapiśitaṃ trimadhusaṃyutaṃ juhuyāt ।। viparītacakramudrāṃ baddhvā sādhyaṃ tu nikṣipenmadhye । sampīḍitakarasampuṭavihvalavaktraṃ karāntare dhyātvā ।। ānayati mahāpuruṣaṃ kṣitipatimapi divasaśatabhāgāt ।
śitaśastrapātarahitadhvajanaraśīrṣaṃ pragṛhya lakṣamayutam ।। tatra trirūpagaditaṃ dhāma likhitvābhipūjayedyastu । tasya haripavanakamalajadhanadayamendrāḥ sasiddhagandharvāḥ ।। vividhavarasiddhijātaṃ vidadhati vicitrāstathāparāḥ siddhīḥ ।
vyaktāvyaktaṃ tathā vyaktamavyaktaṃ tu trirūpakam ।। jāyate trividhā siddhir girirājatanūdbhave ।। raktacandanadhūliṃ tu rājikāṃ lavaṇaṃ tathā ।। japan svacchandadevaṃ tu nirmathnaṃśca karadvayam ।।
sādhyasyābhimukho bhūtvā prayogamimamācaret ।। vaśamāyāti bhūnātha ātmanā ca dhanena ca ।। tāmeva dhūliṃ saṃgṛhya lohacūrṇavimiśritām ।। nikhanyāṣṭāṅgulaṃ bhūmau ripunāmasamanvitām ।।
tāmeva dhūliṃ saṃgṛhya pañcakonmattasaṃyutām ।। śatajaptāṃ tu tāṃ kṛtvā śmaśāne nikhaned drutam ।। uddhṛtaṃ vastramādāya kṣīreṇa pariśodhayet ।। atha raktāśvamārasya kusumāni samāharet ।।
sakṛjjaptena puṣpeṇa liṅgamūrdhani tāḍayet ।। tatastvekādaśaitāni saṃgṛhya kusumāni tu ।। ānupūrvyeṇa sarvāṇi sakṛjjaptvā tu mantravit ।। tadgṛhītvāmbusammiśraṃ dantairaspṛṣṭamāpibet ।।
tarjanyagre tu tatkṛtvā aṅguṣṭhenākramed budhaḥ ।। apasavyaṃ bhrāmayitvā punastasya visarjanam ।। uttānamañjaliṃ kṛtvā kapālaṃ parikīrtitam ।। aṅguṣṭhenākrameddevi ṛjvīṃ kṛtvā pradeśinīm ।।
khaṭvāṅgaṃ kīrtitaṃ hyetat khaḍgamudrāṃ nibodha me ।। madhyamāṃ tarjanīṃ cordhvaṃ khaḍgamudrā prakīrtitā ।। ātmanaḥ sammukhaṃ kṛtvā spharaste kathito mayā ।। aṅkuśaḥ kathito hyeṣa pāśamudrāṃ nibodha me ।।
pāśastu kathito hyeṣa duṣṭajālanibandhakaḥ ।। nārācastu samākhyātaḥ samāsāttava bhairavi ।। agre nikuñcayet kiñcit pinākaṃ parikīrtitam ।। parāṅmukhaṃ tu taṃ kṛtvā tv abhayaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
prasṛtaṃ darśayeddevi varaḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ ।। dakṣahastasya tarjanyā ghṛṣed ghaṇṭā prakīrtitā ।। prasārya cāṅgulīstisras triśūlaṃ parikīrtitam ।। vāmahastamadhaḥ kṛtvā uttānaṃ tu samāhitaḥ ।।
ubhayorapi saṅghṛṣya vajramudrāṃ pradarśayet ।। suṣireṇa samāyuktaṃ darśayettu varānane ।। mudgaraḥ kathito hyeṣa vallakīṃ ca nibodha me ।। anāme kuñcayitvā tu vīṇāmudrā prakīrtitā ।।
aṅguṣṭhenākramedādyāṃ paraśuḥ samudāhṛtāḥ ।। āvāhane nirodhe ca tathā caiva visarjane ।। kapālaṃ dhavalaṃ jñeyaṃ khaṭvāṅgaṃ ca tathaiva hi ।। spharaṃ raktaṃ pinākaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ samparikīrtitam ।।
pāśo bhinnāñjananibhaḥ sphaṭikābho abhayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। ḍamaruṃ hemasaṅkāśaṃ vīṇāṃ caitatsamaprabhām ।। rājāvartanibho devi mudgaraḥ paraśustathā ।। praṇavāsanamārūḍhā oṃkārādyā varānane ।।
sādhayanti mahādevi phalāni vividhāni tu ।। veditavyaṃ prayatnena sādhitavyaṃ mahātmanā ।। chummakāḥ sampravakṣyāmi sādhakasya varānane ।। sādhakastu girirjñeyaḥ putrako vimalaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
madyaṃ tu harṣaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ muditā tu surā smṛtā ।। jātaṃ prarūḍhamityāhur mṛtaṃ caiva parāṅmukham ।। śukraṃ candraḥ samākhyātaḥ snāyuḥ sūtraṃ prakīrtitam ।। piśāco romajananaḥ ruhā jñeyā rajasvalā ।।
nayane cañcale jñeye jihvāṃ saṃgrāhikāṃ viduḥ ।। liṅgaṃ santoṣajananaṃ bhagaḥ prītivivardhanaḥ ।। dūtī saṃvāhikā jñeyā dhūpo hlādana ucyate ।। paśurvibodhako jñeyaś carukaḥ sārvakāmikaḥ ।।
diśāṃ mukhaṃ tu śravaṇaṃ tvak ca saṃvedanī smṛtā ।। paśu pracāro vijñeyaḥ mātā dhātrīti kathyate ।। bhaginī śubhakarī jñeyā sakhī sarvārthasādhikā ।। chit sphijau kīrtito devi dṛṣṭiścakṣuḥ prakīrtitam ।।
hṛdayaṃ guhyamityuktaṃ kaṭhinaṃ tvasthi viddhi hi ।। viṣṭhāṃ vidūṣikāṃ viddhi mūtraṃ snāva ihocyate ।। melakaṃ caiva saṅghātaḥ putraḥ soddyotakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। dūṣako jāra ityuktaḥ pītaṃ vanditameva ca ।।
dūṣitaṃ karṣitaṃ jñeyaṃ sammataṃ samayaṃ viduḥ ।। vinayo dehakarma syāt sādhanaṃ tu japaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। kadambaṃ vṛndamityāhur viralo aśliṣṭa ucyate ।। devatādarśanaṃ yattat labdhaṃ śastrahataṃ viduḥ ।।
ānītaṃ sāritaṃ jñeyaṃ rakṣitaṃ pihitaṃ tathā ।। śiraḥ pradarśayedyā tu sā ca binduṃ vinirdiśet ।। tālukaṃ darśayedyā tu tayā rudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। sapta koṭayastu mantrāṇāṃ tasyā jñeyāstu suvrate ।।
kaṇṭhaṃ tu saṃspṛśeyā sā kālatattvaṃ vinirdiśet ।। nābhiṃ pradarśayedyā tu prakṛtiṃ sā vinirdiśet ।। yadā guhyaṃ spṛśeddevi ahaṃkāro adhidaivatam ।। ūrukau darśayeddevi pavanaṃ sā vinirdiśet ।।
jaṅghe pradarśayedyā tu varuṇaṃ sā vinirdiśet ।। pūjāgnijapayuktasya dhyānayuktasya mantriṇaḥ ।। kriyopetasya deveśi yoginyastu varapradāḥ ।। girirājasya deveśi yaṃ gatvā phalamaśnute ।।
anyāśca siddhīrvividhā adhamā madhyamottamāḥ ।। evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ melakaṃ tu varānane ।। yasya samprāśanāddevi vīreśasadṛśo bhavet ।। kurvanti bhāvitātmānas tataḥ siddhyanti mantriṇaḥ ।।
